# Papaen IELTS Speaking Part 2 Combo Archive

## 1. 新法律 + 重要决定 + 动物故事书 + 困难后成功的人 / 事件 / NEW
1. [Part 4] 同学可以结合题库的具体问题，练习素材。
1.为了更好的匹配每一道题，素材本身的字数会超过真实的考试同学们能表达字数。
2.针对不同的问法，同学的开头和结尾需要进行调整。
3.一定要注意表达的自然程度~必要时增加重音，表情和手势
   - Answer: 想为流浪动物立法 (6.5~7)
   - Summary: 我想颁布保护流浪猫狗的法律。我常看到被遗弃的宠物，甚至有人伤害它们。这个想法源于一个重要决定：我读了《流浪狗日记》后选择学环境科学。这本书讲普通人救助受伤流浪狗的故事，其中一个工人花三个月治好了一条腿断的狗。书中还提到李博士，她想建收容所但没钱，打三份工攒了两年，后收到小额捐款。十年后她的收容所帮助了200多只狗。她的故事让我明白坚持就有回报。因为她和那本书，我选了现在的专业，也希望能像她一样帮助流浪动物。
   - Content: If I could create a new law, it would be to protect stray dogs and cats. In my city, I often see abandoned pets on the streets. Some people buy animals because they look cute, but then they throw them away when they become inconvenient. Some stray animals are even hurt by cruel people. My law would make it illegal to abandon any pet. People who abandon or harm stray animals would have to pay a heavy fine, and repeat offenders would face community service at animal shelters.

This idea came from an important decision I made a few years ago. I decided to study environmental science at university. That decision was heavily influenced by a book I read called “Stray Dog Diaries.” This book tells true stories of ordinary people who rescued injured stray dogs. One story was about a construction worker who found a dog with a broken leg. He had no money for a vet, but he spent three months learning how to treat the dog himself. In the end, the dog walked again. That story made me cry.

The book also introduced me to someone who succeeded after many difficulties. Her name is Dr. Li, a scientist in my hometown. She wanted to build a shelter for stray dogs, but she had almost no money at the beginning. Many people told her to give up because helping stray animals was not a real job. For two years, she worked three part-time jobs — as a tutor, a cashier, and a cleaner — and saved almost every penny. Then she received a small donation from a kind stranger. She used that money to rent a small house for stray dogs. Now, ten years later, her shelter helps over 200 dogs and has three full-time volunteers. She also works with local schools to teach children not to abandon pets.

Dr. Li’s story taught me that persistence pays off. Because of her and the book, I chose my major. And that is why I would make that animal protection law. I hope one day I can help stray animals too, just like Dr. Li.

## 2. 无聊地方 + 科技问题 + 近期看的节目 + 花很久回信息 / 事件 / NEW
1. [Part 4] 同学可以结合题库的具体问题，练习素材。
1.为了更好的匹配每一道题，素材本身的字数会超过真实的考试同学们能表达字数。
2.针对不同的问法，同学的开头和结尾需要进行调整。
3.一定要注意表达的自然程度~必要时增加重音，表情和手势
   - Answer: 无聊博物馆与坏Wi-Fi (6~6.5)
   - Summary: 我去过一个无聊的地方——本地历史博物馆，里面只有老照片和落灰的工具，十分钟后我就困了。更糟的是Wi-Fi连不上，我想查资料都不行，只能干坐。最近我在B站看到一个vlog，博主也去了同一个博物馆，吐槽了同样的问题。说到回信息，我曾经花了三天才回复朋友。他问我要不要再去看那个博物馆，我不想去又不知道怎么拒绝，就一直拖着，最后只说“抱歉我很忙”。那个博物馆太无聊，让我连回信息都想逃避。现在我去博物馆前都会先看网上评价。
   - Content: A really boring place I have been to is a local history museum near my home. I went there with my class last year because our teacher said it was educational. However, the museum only had a few old photos and some dusty tools behind glass. There were no interactive exhibits, no videos, and no guided tours. I felt sleepy after just ten minutes. Most of my classmates were standing around, looking at their phones.

To make the experience even worse, I also had a tech problem there. The museum offered free Wi-Fi, but it did not work at all. I tried to connect three times, but my phone kept showing “no internet connection.” I wanted to search for more information about the exhibits online because the signs next to them were very brief and boring. Without internet, I could only walk around in silence. I ended up sitting on a bench for twenty minutes just waiting for the trip to end.

Recently, I watched a funny short video on Bilibili. It was a vlog made by another visitor who had gone to the exact same museum. The vlogger also complained about the bad Wi-Fi and the boring exhibits. He made jokes about the dusty tools and the old photos. I laughed a lot because I had the exact same experience. I even left a comment saying, “I feel you, bro.”.

Speaking of replying to messages, I once took three days to reply to a friend. He sent me a message asking, “Do you want to visit that museum again next week?” I did not want to go at all, but I also did not know how to say no politely. So I kept delaying my reply. Every time I opened his message, I closed it again and told myself I would reply later. Finally, after three full days, I simply said, “Sorry, I am busy.” That museum was so boring that it even made me avoid replying to messages. Now I always check online reviews before visiting any museum to avoid wasting my time like that again.

## 3. 高建筑 + 特别场合食物 + 喜欢拜访但不想住的家 + 改变重要想法 / 事件 / NEW
1. [Part 4] 同学可以结合题库的具体问题，练习素材。
1.为了更好的匹配每一道题，素材本身的字数会超过真实的考试同学们能表达字数。
2.针对不同的问法，同学的开头和结尾需要进行调整。
3.一定要注意表达的自然程度~必要时增加重音，表情和手势
   - Answer: 矮屋饺香，家不在高 (6~6.5)
   - Summary: 我不喜欢太高的建筑，比如上海中心大厦让我头晕害怕。我更喜欢祖母的老房子，传统矮屋有小院子。春节全家在那里包饺子吃，非常温暖。但我只喜欢去做客，不想长住，因为没有现代厕所和淋浴，冬天冷房间小。这改变了我一个想法：以前觉得好家必须是高大现代建筑，现在明白家的本质是家人温暖，不是高度。充满爱的小旧房子比豪华公寓更像家。我很高兴改变这个想法，学会了珍惜简单的东西。
   - Content: To be honest, I do not like very tall buildings. For example, the Shanghai Tower makes me feel dizzy and scared. I went to the top once with my cousins, and I could not even stand near the window. My legs felt weak. I prefer low, cozy buildings instead.

That is why I really like my grandmother’s old house. It is a traditional one-story building with a small yard and a wooden door. The rooms are small, but they feel warm and full of memories. In that house, we always eat dumplings during special occasions, especially during Chinese New Year. The dumplings are made by hand by my grandmother. The whole family sits around a big table, wrapping dumplings together and chatting. It is one of the warmest moments in my life.

However, I only like visiting my grandmother’s old house. I do not want to live there permanently. The house does not have a modern toilet or a proper shower. In winter, it gets very cold because the walls are thin. Also, the rooms are too small to have my own private space. Visiting for one day is fun and nostalgic, but living there every day would be difficult.

This experience actually changed an important idea in my mind. Before, I used to think that a good home must be a tall, modern building with all the latest facilities — things like a gym, a swimming pool, and a big elevator. I thought height equaled quality. But after visiting my grandmother’s old house so many times and comparing it to the tall buildings in the city center, I changed my opinion completely. I now believe that a home is about family warmth and emotional comfort, not about height or modern facilities. A small, old house can be a better home than a luxury apartment if it is filled with love. I am glad I changed this idea because it helped me appreciate the simple things in life.

## 4. 喜欢种菜的人 + 团队中工作 + 名人广告 + 坏掉的电子设备 / 人物 / NEW
1. [Part 4] 同学可以结合题库的具体问题，练习素材。
1.为了更好的匹配每一道题，素材本身的字数会超过真实的考试同学们能表达字数。
2.针对不同的问法，同学的开头和结尾需要进行调整。
3.一定要注意表达的自然程度~必要时增加重音，表情和手势
   - Answer: 爷爷种菜教我耐心 (6~6.5)
   - Summary: 爷爷喜欢在阳台种菜，每天早晨浇水除虫，他说种菜让他平静耐心。这教会我如何在团队中工作。上次小组作业组员意见不合，我本想争论，但想起爷爷从不着急，于是耐心听完所有人想法，最后结合优点做出好计划。团队合作就像种菜，不能急于求成。期间我手机坏了，黑屏三天不能用。这三天我反而多了时间陪爷爷。我还看了姚明拍的手机广告，他用手机拍蔬菜，让我想起爷爷的菜园。手机坏掉让我意识到，没有科技的生活也可以很平静。
   - Content: My grandfather is a person who loves growing vegetables at home. He has a small garden on our balcony where he plants tomatoes, cucumbers, and green peppers. Every morning, he waters them carefully and checks for any insects. He says gardening makes him feel peaceful and patient.

This hobby of his actually taught me a lot about how to work in a team. Last semester, I had a group project at school. My team members had very different opinions about how to do the research. Some wanted to start with surveys, while others preferred interviews. At first, I felt frustrated and wanted to argue. But then I remembered how my grandfather cares for his plants. He never rushes. He observes first, then acts. So I decided to listen to everyone’s ideas carefully before saying anything. Finally, we made a good plan together by combining the best parts of each suggestion. I realized that teamwork is like gardening — you need patience and you cannot force things to grow faster than they should.

Around the same time, I had a problem with my electronic device. My mobile phone broke last month. The screen suddenly went black, and I could not use it for three days. I felt very anxious because I use my phone for almost everything — studying, messaging, and entertainment.

During those three days, I spent more time with my grandfather in his garden. I also saw a funny TV advertisement with Yao Ming, the famous basketball player. He was selling a mobile phone and used it to take pictures of vegetables. That ad reminded me of my grandfather’s garden because the vegetables in the ad looked exactly like the ones on our balcony. It was funny because Yao Ming is so tall but holding a small phone.

The experience of my broken phone actually helped me realize something important. Life without technology can also be peaceful, especially when you have a patient grandfather and a small garden to take care of.

## 5. 最喜欢的城市 + 想旅游的地方 + 喜欢现场体育赛事 + 推荐旅行过的地方 / 地点 / NEW
1. [Part 4] 同学可以结合题库的具体问题，练习素材。
1.为了更好的匹配每一道题，素材本身的字数会超过真实的考试同学们能表达字数。
2.针对不同的问法，同学的开头和结尾需要进行调整。
3.一定要注意表达的自然程度~必要时增加重音，表情和手势
   - Answer: 最爱成都，现场看球 (6~6.5)
   - Summary: 我最喜欢的城市是成都，两年前暑假去的。火锅很美味，但最吸引我的是当地人悠闲的生活方式。我还去看了现场足球赛，全场呐喊助威的气氛让我非常兴奋。因此我向所有人推荐成都，既适合年轻人也适合家庭，可以看熊猫、吃小吃、看比赛。如果有空再去旅游，成都也是我的首选。上次只待三天太短，下次想去一周，品尝更多美食，再去熊猫基地，再看一场比赛。成都不像北上广那么快节奏，它让我感到快乐放松，是我最想重游的地方。
   - Content: My favorite city that I have visited is Chengdu, the capital of Sichuan Province. I went there two years ago during the summer holiday. The first thing that impressed me was the food. The hotpot in Chengdu is incredibly delicious, with a perfect balance of spice and aroma. But what I loved most was the relaxed lifestyle. People there enjoy a slow pace of life, sitting in teahouses and chatting for hours.

One of the best memories from that trip was watching a live football match at the Chengdu Sports Center. I really enjoy watching live sports events because the atmosphere is completely different from watching on television. The stadium was full of people shouting, cheering, and waving flags. I felt the energy from the crowd, and even though I am not a big football fan, the live atmosphere made me very excited.

That is why I strongly recommend Chengdu to anyone who wants to travel. The city is suitable for both young people and families. You can see giant pandas, eat cheap and tasty street food, and enjoy live sports. The people are friendly and welcoming.

If I have free time in the future, Chengdu is the first place I want to visit again. Last time I only stayed for three days, which was too short. Next time, I want to go for at least one week. I want to try more local dishes, visit the panda base again, and watch another live sports event. Chengdu makes me feel happy and relaxed. It is not too fast-paced like Beijing or Shanghai. That is why it is my favorite city, my top travel recommendation, and the place I dream of revisiting.

## 6. 发小 + 早起经历 + 近期改变的计划 + 别人帮助解决问题 + 长久目标 / 人物 / NEW
1. [Part 4] 同学可以结合题库的具体问题，练习素材。
1.为了更好的匹配每一道题，素材本身的字数会超过真实的考试同学们能表达字数。
2.针对不同的问法，同学的开头和结尾需要进行调整。
3.一定要注意表达的自然程度~必要时增加重音，表情和手势
   - Answer: 发小助我早起自律 (6~6.5)
   - Summary: 我的发小张伟非常自律。去年我备考重要考试时总是起不来床，他连续一周每天早上6点来我家叫我起床。开始很痛苦，但三天后我就适应了，早上复习让我精力更充沛，最终顺利通过考试。受此影响，我近期改变计划，从熬夜睡到中午变成每天6点起床、运动半小时、学习两小时，整个人更健康专注。我的长久目标是成为自律的人，坚持早起五年，并帮助其他拖延的学生。张伟的帮助让我明白，小习惯长期坚持就能带来大成功。
   - Content: My childhood best friend is Zhang Wei. We grew up in the same neighborhood and went to the same primary school. He is one of the most disciplined people I have ever known. When I was preparing for a very important exam last year, I faced a serious problem: I could not wake up early. Every morning, I would turn off my alarm and go back to sleep. I was worried because I had so much material to review, but I kept wasting my mornings.

Zhang Wei noticed this and decided to help me. For one whole week, he came to my home at 6 a. m. every day and woke me up personally. That was a truly memorable early rising experience. At first, it was painful because I love sleeping. But after three days, I got used to it. I reviewed my notes in the morning and felt much more energetic throughout the day. With his help, I passed the exam successfully.

Recently, I changed my daily plan because of that experience. Before, I used to stay up late and sleep until noon. Now I wake up at 6 a. m. every day, exercise for 30 minutes, and study for two hours in the morning. This change has made me healthier and more focused.

My long-term goal is to become a disciplined person like Zhang Wei. I want to keep this early rising habit for the next five years. I also hope to help other lazy students who struggle with time management. This goal gives me direction and motivation in life. Without Zhang Wei’s help, I might still be wasting my mornings. Now I truly believe that small changes in daily routine can lead to big success in the long run.

## 7. 免费物品/去过且推荐的宜居之地 / 地点
1. [Part 4] Describe a place you have been to and would like to recommend others to live there (not your hometown)
You should say:
Where it is
What the place is like
When you visited there
Who you went there with
And explain why you would recommend this place to others；
Describe something you received for free
You should say:
What it was
Who you received it from
Where you received it
And how you felt about it
   - Answer: 杭州 (6~6.5)
   - Summary: 我非常推荐中国杭州，它是一个适合居住的好地方。它位于浙江省，以其美丽的景色、丰富的历史和生动的文化而闻名。去年春天，我有机会和家人一起去杭州旅游，我印象非常深刻。杭州还有充满活力的街头市场，在那里你可以找到各种各样的当地食品和纪念品。发生了一件很酷的事情，当我参观那里的博物馆时，我得到了一张免费的明信片！
   - Content: I really recommend Hangzhou, China as a great place to live. It’s in Zhejiang Province and is famous for its beautiful views, rich history, and lively culture. I got the chance to visit Hangzhou with my family last spring, and I was super impressed.

Hangzhou is well-known for its gorgeous West Lake, which is surrounded by lush greenery and stunning scenery. I spent a few hours exploring the lake on a boat, soaking up the peaceful vibe and enjoying the warm breeze. The lake has temples, pagodas, and gardens all around it—making it such an enchanting spot to check out.

During this trip, I also went to Lingyin Temple, one of the oldest and biggest Buddhist temples in China. The intricate architecture and calm atmosphere make it an awesome place for some quiet reflection.

Plus, Hangzhou has these vibrant street markets where you can find all sorts of local food and souvenirs. One cool thing that happened was when I visited a museum there—I got a free postcard! The museum highlights the region's famous silk products along with its breathtaking scenery. When I walked into the museum, the staff greeted me warmly and handed me this lovely postcard showing off Hangzhou’s natural beauty and silk culture. It was such a nice surprise! That postcard means a lot to me; every time I see it, I'm reminded of how fascinating Hangzhou is—the beauty there really sticks with you!

All in all, Hangzhou perfectly blends traditional Chinese culture with modern life. I'd totally recommend it because its amazing natural beauty, lively cultural scene, and friendly locals make it an ideal place to live or just explore!

## 8. 帮助小孩\造福社会的工作 / 事物
1. [Part 4] Describe a person who contributes to the society
You should say:
Who the person is 
How you knew him/her
What type of work he/she does
And explain why you think he/she contributes to the society；
Describe a time when you helped a child
You should say:
When it was
How you helped him/her
Why you helped him/her
And how you felt about it
   - Answer: 王警官 (6~6.5)
   - Summary: 今天，我想谈谈我认为对社会作出杰出贡献的一位先生，他保证了社会成员的安全和福利。这个人便是王警官。有次我遇到了走失的儿童，在王警官的帮助下，小孩成功回家了，这一事件反映了他的职业素养。
   - Content: This society is privileged to have numerous individuals who have made remarkable contributions in diverse manners. Today, I wish to speak about a gentleman whom I deem has made an outstanding contribution to society by guaranteeing the safety and welfare of its members. This man is a police officer, we call him Officer Wang.

I first became acquainted with Officer Wang several years ago when he delivered a lecture at our school regarding the role of the police in our community. I was instantly struck by his genial and amicable demeanour, and I discerned that he genuinely cared for people.

Officer Wang was a devoted police officer who toiled unremittingly to uphold law and order in our community. He was responsible for safeguarding and serving our communities, responding to emergency calls, conducting investigations, and keeping our streets secure.

What impressed me the most about Officer Wang's work was his dedication to assisting and protecting the most vulnerable members of society, especially children. He actively participated in community outreach programmes, visiting schools to educate children about safety measures and how to handle emergencies.

One incident that reflects Officer Wang's commitment to his duty and his influence on society was that he helped a lost child find his way home. It was a few months ago when I encountered a young boy in a park near my home who had got separated from his family and was evidently frightened. I comforted the child, pacified him, recalled the parents' phone number, and contacted Officer Wang. Officer Wang promptly arrived to handle the matter, patiently consoling the child until his family was located, while maintaining excellent communication with his police colleagues. I was truly touched to witness his efforts and the expression of relief on that child's face.

I believe Officer Wang has made a significant contribution to society because he has exceeded his duty. He not only ensured our safety but also took an active interest in education and the protection of children.

## 9. 有趣的歌曲/提高注意力/节约时间的方法&改变 / 事物
1. [Part 4] Describe an interesting song
You should say:
What the song is
What story the song tells
Whether the song is popular
And explain why you think it is interesting；
Describe something you do that can help you concentrate on work/study
You should say:
What it is
How it helps you concentrate
When you do it
And explain how you feel about it；
Describe a way/change that helps you save a lot of time
You should say
What it is
How you implement it
How difficult it is
And explain how you feel about the way/change
   - Answer: 《月光》 (6~6.5)
   - Summary: 帮助我集中精力工作的歌是克劳德·德彪西的《月光》。这首歌是一首以优美的旋律和舒缓的氛围而闻名的古典歌曲。总的来说，听克劳德·德彪西的《月光》是帮助我集中精力工作的宝贵工具。它舒缓的旋律和平静的气氛为生产力和创造力创造了理想的环境。这是一部真正的杰作，它不仅提高了我的注意力，而且在学习时给我一种快乐和宁静的感觉。
   - Content: The last song I listened to recently that helped me concentrate on work was "Clair de Lune" by Claude Debussy. The song is a classical piece that is known for its beautiful melody and soothing ambiance. It is about capturing the essence of moonlight and evoking a sense of calm and tranquility.

I heard the song while studying in my favorite corner of the library. The peaceful environment combined with the soft notes of the piano created the perfect atmosphere for concentration and focus. The song transported me to a serene place where I could escape the distractions of the outside world and immerse myself fully in my work.

"Clair de Lune" is a composition by a French composer, Claude Debussy. It is considered one of the most famous and beloved classical pieces in the world. Debussy's music often explores themes of nature and emotions, and "Clair de Lune" is no exception. It beautifully captures the ethereal and contemplative qualities of moonlight, creating a sense of introspection and inner peace.

As for my feelings about the song, I find it truly enchanting. The gentle melodies and delicate harmonies evoke a sense of nostalgia and tranquility that helps me focus and concentrate on my work. The intricate musical structure and the subtle dynamics of the piece never fail to captivate me. Whenever I listen to "Clair de Lune," it transports me to a different world, allowing me to delve deep into my work with unwavering attention and productivity.

Overall, listening to "Clair de Lune" by Claude Debussy has been a valuable tool in helping me concentrate on my work. Its soothing melodies and calming atmosphere create an ideal environment for productivity and creativity. It is truly a masterpiece that not only enhances my focus but also provides me with a sense of joy and tranquility while studying.

## 10. 壮志未酬/忙碌时期 / 事物
1. [Part 4] Describe an ambition that you haven't achieved
You should say:
What it is
Why you haven't achieved it
What you did
And how you felt about it;
Describe a period you were busy
You should say:
When it was
What you did during the period
What made you busy
And explain how you felt about the experience
   - Answer: 西语 (6~6.5)
   - Summary: 我还没有实现的一个抱负是能说一口流利的外语。最近，我设定了一个目标，要把西班牙语学得流利。然而，由于工作和其他事情的繁忙，我没有足够的时间来学习语言。
   - Content: One ambition that I haven't achieved is becoming fluent in a foreign language. Recently, I set a goal to learn Spanish fluently. However, because of my busy schedule with work and other commitments, I haven't been able to dedicate enough time to language learning.

In an attempt to achieve this ambition, I enrolled in a Spanish language course. Unfortunately, due to the heavy workload and limited free time, I had to miss several classes and couldn't keep up with the pace of the course. I also tried to practice on my own by using language learning apps and watching Spanish movies, but it wasn't enough to make significant progress.

I feel a tinge of disappointment about not being able to achieve this ambition. Language learning has always fascinated me, and being able to converse fluently in Spanish would have opened up so many doors for personal and professional growth. However, I understand that sometimes other responsibilities take precedence, and I need to accept that I may not be able to achieve everything at once.

Nevertheless, I haven't completely given up on my ambition. I still have a strong desire to learn Spanish and I plan to revisit my goal in the future when I have more time and resources available. Perhaps during a vacation or a break from work, I will be able to fully devote myself to language learning and finally achieve fluency in Spanish.

## 11. 听过的歌/提高注意力/节约时间的方法&改变 / 事件

Where you heard the song
What country the song is from
And explain how you feel about the song；

You should say:

And explain how you feel about it；

You should say
What it is
How you implement it
How difficult it is
And explain how you feel about the way/change
   - Answer: 《月光》 (6.5~7)
   - Summary: 最近我听的最后一首帮助我集中精力工作的歌是克劳德·德彪西的《月光》。这首歌是一首以优美的旋律和舒缓的氛围而闻名的古典歌曲。总的来说，听克劳德·德彪西的《月光》是帮助我集中精力工作的宝贵工具。它舒缓的旋律和平静的气氛为生产力和创造力创造了理想的环境。这是一部真正的杰作，它不仅提高了我的注意力，而且在学习时给我一种快乐和宁静的感觉。
   - Content: The last song I listened to recently that helped me concentrate on work was "Clair de Lune" by Claude Debussy. The song is a classical piece that is known for its beautiful melody and soothing ambiance. It is about capturing the essence of moonlight and evoking a sense of calm and tranquility.

I heard the song while studying in my favorite corner of the library. The peaceful environment combined with the soft notes of the piano created the perfect atmosphere for concentration and focus. The song transported me to a serene place where I could escape the distractions of the outside world and immerse myself fully in my work.

"Clair de Lune" is a composition by a French composer, Claude Debussy. It is considered one of the most famous and beloved classical pieces in the world. Debussy's music often explores themes of nature and emotions, and "Clair de Lune" is no exception. It beautifully captures the ethereal and contemplative qualities of moonlight, creating a sense of introspection and inner peace.

As for my feelings about the song, I find it truly enchanting. The gentle melodies and delicate harmonies evoke a sense of nostalgia and tranquility that helps me focus and concentrate on my work. The intricate musical structure and the subtle dynamics of the piece never fail to captivate me. Whenever I listen to "Clair de Lune," it transports me to a different world, allowing me to delve deep into my work with unwavering attention and productivity.

Overall, listening to "Clair de Lune" by Claude Debussy has been a valuable tool in helping me concentrate on my work. Its soothing melodies and calming atmosphere create an ideal environment for productivity and creativity. It is truly a masterpiece that not only enhances my focus but also provides me with a sense of joy and tranquility while studying.

   - Content: The radio has undoubtedly proven itself to be a highly valuable invention. When the radio in my father's car broke down, he turned to me for advice, assuming that my knowledge of machinery was more extensive. Uncertain about the extent of the damage, I embarked on a diligent research journey and sought the guidance of a few experts. After careful consideration, I made the challenging decision to tackle the repair myself, determined to restore it to its former functionality. Although the process was riddled with numerous difficulties, perseverance and a focused mindset ultimately allowed me to triumph over the repair task.

The successful restoration of the car radio not only brought back its desired utility but also fostered a stronger bond between my father and me. This shared experience served as a reminder of the importance of communication and problem-solving within the realm of technology. It was truly a transformative moment that deepened our understanding of each other and reinforced the significance of resourcefulness and teamwork.

In conclusion, while the radio has undeniably enhanced our lives in countless ways, we must acknowledge that technical malfunctions can occasionally impede its functioning. However, through determination and a willingness to explore new territories, we can overcome these challenges and not only bring these devices back to life but also strengthen the relationships among those involved in the restoration process.

## 13. 困难决定终成功/努力实现目标/印象深刻的谈话/重要决定 / 地点
1. [Part 4] 同学可以结合题库的具体问题，练习素材。
1. 为了更好的匹配每一道题，素材本身的字数会超过真实的考试同学们能表达字数。
2. 针对不同的问法，同学的开头和结尾需要进行调整。
3. 一定要注意表达的自然程度～必要时增加重音，表情和手势
   - Answer: 体育老师的话 (6~6.5)
   - Summary: 我清楚地记得，我全神贯注地听着体育老师的话，记住了他分享的每一条宝贵的建议。在他的指导下，我坚定地决定按照他的建议，把体育锻炼纳入我的日常生活。此外，我决心改变我的熬夜习惯。
Vivid (adj.) – 鲜明的
Gloomy (adj.) – 阴沉的
Relentless (adj.) – 持续的
Astute (adj.) – 精明的
Impart (v.) – 传授
Confines (n.) – 范围
Well-being (n.) – 健康
Disciplined (adj.) – 自律的
   - Content: There was a physical education (PE) lesson that remains vivid in my memory, leaving a lasting impression on me. It was a gloomy day, with relentless rain pouring outside, making it impossible for us to engage in our usual outdoor activities. However, our astute PE teacher seized the opportunity to impart valuable knowledge and insights within the confines of our classroom.

During the indoor session, our teacher not only educated us about the rules and strategies of various sports but also emphasized the importance of maintaining a healthy lifestyle. He enlightened us about the significance of proper nutrition and the benefits of adhering to regular sleeping patterns, thereby enhancing our overall well-being.

I vividly recall listening intently to his words of wisdom, absorbing every piece of valuable advice he shared. Motivated by his guidance, I made a firm decision to incorporate physical exercise into my daily routine, as per his recommendations. Furthermore, I resolved to break free from my late-night habits and prioritize a consistent sleep schedule.

As weeks turned into months, the effects of my disciplined lifestyle became evident. Not only did I experience a surge in my energy levels, but I also noticed improvements in my concentration and overall physical health. Through consistent exercise and a newfound commitment to balanced nutrition, I witnessed the transformation of my body into a stronger, fitter version of itself.

In summary, this remarkable PE lesson, conducted indoors due to inclement weather, resulted in an inspiring journey of personal growth.

## 15. 不喜欢并想改变的规则/对社会有贡献的人 / 人物
1. [Part 4] Describe a rule you dislike and would like to change in the future
You should say:
What it is
What it is for
Why you don't like it
And explain why you would like to change it；

Describe a person who contributes to the society
You should say:
Who the person is 
How you knew him/her
What type of work he/she does
And explain why you think he/she contributes to the society
   - Answer: 教育局长 (6~6.5)
   - Summary: 我们市教育局长非常重视体育，他规定我们每周必须上两节体育课，我很讨厌这个规定，但是多年以后发现，我们那一届学生的身体平均素质显著高于其他年级，我感觉他对我们学生身体素质的提高有很大贡献
   - Content: A rule I don't like is one regarding physical education introduced by(被…提出) the director of our city's education bureau(教育局). / I think a person who has contributed to society is the director of our city's education bureau, who brought about the reform of school sports(提出来了关于学校体育改革的事).

The city where I live is a model national education city, which means the city's education system has been widely recognized(得到广泛认可) across China. But to be honest, this recognition only regards the level of academic test scores(这个认可都在学习考试成绩的层面上). Regarding the physical ability of students, the education bureau did not pay special attention to it until the arrival of the new director. The director's surname is Zhang, and he was transferred here from another city about ten years ago. I don't know him personally, but I saw him when he came to visit our school. The first thing Director Zhang did after taking office(上任) was to stipulate(规定) that all junior high schools and high schools in the city must take physical education classes twice a week, and for PE classes to be included in the final exam. To be honest, I hated this rule at first, because firstly, I don't like sports very much. I am a relatively quiet person, and I prefer to stay in the classroom studying and reading books than exercising. Secondly, I thought PE class was just a waste of time, especially for students who were about to take high school or college entrance examinations(中考或高考). There were a lot of students who didn't like this rule, but of course we were all forced to(被迫) abide by(遵守) it. Finally, I think this rule is not suitable for all students, and I think it can be changed to arrange according to students' wishes.

But now that several years have passed, I am surprised to find that the physical ability of our students is significantly higher than that of students elsewhere. In fact, even several students from my school were admitted to pilot training school(考上了飞行员) after the college entrance examination last year, and we all know how demanding the physical fitness test to become a pilot is(我们都知道飞行员考试对考试身体素质的要求有多高)! So, despite how I initially felt, I now think Director Zhang's rule is really great, and he has made a great contribution to our city.

## 16. 一个去过的新地方/去过的乡村 / 地点
1. [Part 4] Describe a new place you visited
You should say:
Where it is
When you went there
Why you went there
And explain how you feel about the place；

Describe a countryside that you have been to
You should say:
Where it is
When you went there
Who you went there with
And explain why you went there
   - Answer: 浙江余村 (6~6.5)
   - Summary: 上个暑假我去了浙江余村，那是一个位于浙江北边的一个小山村。那是一个山峦叠嶂的地方。曾经村民们靠山吃山，毫无限制地开发资源导致环境遭受了破坏。但是现在他们改变了发展策略，通过改良环境发展起了旅游业。今年12月，浙江余村入选联合国首批“世界最佳旅游乡村”名单，他蜕变成了一个很美丽清洁的村落。
   - Content: Last month I took a holiday to Yucun in Anji county, Zhejiang province. It had just been honored as one of the "Best Tourism Villages" at the World Tourism Organization. I wondered how this small village way off the beaten track(偏远的 had achieved this, so I went there to find out.

The natural scenery there was absolutely gorgeous. However, it is hard to imagine that the green mountains, clear rivers and blue skies of that beautiful village were seriously damaged and shrouded by smog and dust just 20 years ago. Yucun once relied on cement factories and mines. Villagers got rich by selling mineral products but as a result found themselves living in a poor ecological environment. Therefore, the villagers made the decision to conserve the local environment and adjust their development planning. They began to develop leisure eco-tourism including agritainment, homestays and rafting. I lodged in a homestay run by a villager and I was stunned by his methods for promoting his business. He posted photos and videos of the beautiful scenery on his social media account and attracted more visitors to book his rooms.

All the homestays and hotels are well established and comfortably furnished. I felt as if I were staying in a five-star hotel with the most beautiful views outside the window. The days I spent in this little village were so relaxing, thanks to the fresh air and the breathtaking bamboo forest. I retain a deep respect for villagers in Yucun, with their determination and constant efforts in searching for a balance between economic development and protection of the surrounding environment. They did it and it was such a great accomplishment that I should introduce to all those who don’t know the story. From this experience, I have understood that economic development doesn’t have to be achieved at the cost of(以…为代价) destroying the environment. The ecological environment itself is the economy and all environmental protection efforts will be rewarded.

What he/she posts on social media 
And explain why you follow him/her on social media
   - Answer: 跟刘畊宏一起运动 (6.5~7)
   - Summary: 因为疫情在家，我开始跟着刘畊宏在家运动健身，他最近非常“火”，我每次打开抖音都能看到他的短视频。每天晚上7点半，我都会打开他的直播间，跟他一起运动。白天我也常常在抖音上刷他的短视频，了解健身相关的知识。自从关注他以后，我养成了运动的习惯，半个月瘦了5斤。
   - Content: I live in Shanghai. As you know, Shanghai went through a very terrible epidemic(疫情), so the whole city was in lockdown(封锁). Nobody was allowed to go out, so I was stuck at home for months. Because of the epidemic, I was really bored at home. I have finished watching the TV series and the social media of my mobile phone. I couldn't find anything to do already. At this time, a singer named Liu Genghong became popular on social media. He is a singer, but the reason for his popularity is not singing, it is his fitness videos.

I started exercising with Liu at home. He is very popular recently, and every time I open Tiktok, I can see his videos. There are also a lot of people on the Internet who started to discuss him and say that he brings a different atmosphere to Chinese social networks(给中国的社交网络带来了不一样的氛围) and made everyone fall in love with fitness. Even now, every night at 7:30, I will open his live video (直播间) and exercise with him. To be honest, for a fitness novice(新手) like me, doing his aerobics(健身操) is still really tiring. Especially at the beginning, after almost five minutes I needed to stop and take a break. However, as I started to practice more and more, I found that my energy was much better, and I was not as tired as before when I danced with him. Eventually, I was able to dance with him for half an hour or an hour before taking a break. During the day, I often swipe through his short videos(刷段视频) on Tiktok to learn about fitness-related knowledge. Since following him, I have developed the habit of (养成…的兴趣) exercising and lost 5 pounds in half a month.

## 18. 未来想一起共事的家人/传统产品 / 人物

Describe a traditional product in your country
You should say:
What it is
When you tried this product for the first time
What it is made of
And explain how you feel about it
   - Answer: 想和妈妈以后一起经营茶园 (7~7.5)
   - Summary: 茶是中国的特色饮品，是用干茶叶泡水制成，我的妈妈就在经营一个茶园。小时候我第一次尝试喝茶时，并没有立即爱上它的味道，但随着我年龄的增长，我越来越喜欢喝茶，也对其背后的茶文化越来越感兴趣，因此我也经常帮妈妈的忙，并尝试自己做茶。我非常敬佩我妈妈一丝不苟的工作态度，希望将来我能够和她一起继续将这个茶园经营下去，越做越好。
   - Content: Tea is a special drink in China. It refers to(指的是) a drink made from the leaves of the tea tree. It is mostly brewed in boiling water to drink. It can be added to food for seasoning(加入食物中调味), and can also be used in traditional Chinese medicine. Tea culture originated in(起源于) China. It is generally believed that the tea tree originated in Sichuan or Yunnan, and historically it was the main sold crop(经济作物) in humid and hilly areas(湿润丘陵地区) such as southern China. Today, tea trees are widely planted in countries all over the world.

My mother also runs a tea garden. The tea garden in my family is not very big, so it is not a very famous brand. Usually, my mother takes care of the tea garden. We only need to hire some temporary workers(临时工) when picking tea leaves. When I first tried drinking tea as a child, I didn't immediately fall in love with the taste, because I thought tea leaves were bitter, and I didn't understand why adults would like to drink such bitter water. But as I got older, I became more and more fond of drinking tea and became more and more interested in the tea culture behind it. Tea is very good for health. The caffeine(咖啡因) in tea can excite the central nervous system(兴奋中枢神经系统), help people boost their spirits(振奋精神), eliminate fatigue(消除疲劳) and improve work efficiency. In addition, tea has the effect of inhibiting arteriosclerosis(抑制动脉硬化) and is antibacterial(抗菌). I often do my mom a favor and try to make my own tea. I admire my mother's meticulous work attitude(一丝不苟的工作态度) very much. I hope that I can continue to run this tea garden with her in the future and make it better and better.

## 19. 交通拥堵/用手机做重要事情 / 事物

What happened
When it happened
How important the cellphone was
And explain how you felt about the experience
   - Answer: 堵车路上用手机完成工作 (7~7.5)
   - Summary: 去年的国庆节我出去旅游了，在回家的高速路上发生了严重的堵车，结果这个时候我的上司突然给我安排了一项紧急的工作，让我快速完成。但我出门的时候并没有带笔记本电脑，无奈之下，我只能用手机开始工作，幸亏手机上的办公软件还算好用，我有惊无险地按时完成了工作。如果没有堵在路上，我可能反而腾不出手来完成工作，算是因祸得福了。
   - Content: I have worked very hard for the past few years without a vacation. So last year's National Day, I arranged a family reunion (久违的) with the whole family. We didn't go very far, just drove to the capital city in my province(省会城市) and spent six days there. On the last morning of the National Day holiday, we drove home. To my surprise, there was a serious traffic jam on the highway home. If I remember correctly, there had been a serious crash on the highway ahead of us. One of the trucks rolled over(侧翻) and it blocked the entire highway, making it impossible for all traffic to pass.

Just as we were doing nothing on the motorway, my boss suddenly assigned me an urgent job(安排了一个紧急工作) that I had to do quickly, and needed to submit to a client within two hours. But I didn't take my laptop with me when I went out, because I didn't expect my boss to arrange work for me between vacations. In desperation(无奈之下), I could only use my mobile phone to start work. Fortunately, the office software on the mobile phone was easy to use, and I also remembered all the data and materials at work, so I completed the work on time without any mistakes . Looking back now(现在回想起来), it was a blessing in disguise(因祸得福) that if I hadn't been stuck in the road, I might have had no time to do my work.

## 20. 重要的河流&湖泊/安静的地方 / 地点
1. [Part 4] Describe an important river/lake in your country 
You should say: 
Where it is located 
How big/long it is 
What it looks like 
And explain why it is important

Describe a quiet place 
You should say: 
Where it is 
How you knew it 
How often you go there 
What you do there 
And explain how you feel about the place
   - Answer: 星空下的青海湖 (7~7.5)
   - Summary: 我想说的是青海湖，它坐落在青藏高原上，面积超过4000平方公里，像一块宝石镶嵌在高原之上。它风景秀美，也是一个重要的生态区，许多鸟类和动物的生存都依赖于它。我去旅游的时候曾在青海湖旁住过一晚，晚上的时候我和朋友裹着被子在客栈的露台上看星星，四周安静得只有风声，世界上好像只剩下星星、湖水和我们，我永远也忘不了这一晚的青海湖。
   - Content: I would say Qinghai Lake, which is very quiet, but one of the most important lakes in China. Qinghai Lake is located in the northeastern part of the Qinghai-Tibet Plateau(青藏高原) in Qinghai Province, China. It is the largest lake and the largest saltwater lake(咸水湖) in China. Qinghai Lake covers an area of(占地面积达…) ​​more than 4, 000 square kilometers and is surrounded by mountains, like a gem set on the plateau(像一块宝石镶嵌在高原之上). It has beautiful scenery and is also an important ecological area(生态区). The survival of many birds and animals depends on it. For example, there are more than 100, 000 migratory birds(候鸟) inhabiting(栖息) it in spring and summer, and the fish resources are also very rich.

When I traveled to Qinghai two years ago, I stayed by Qinghai Lake for one night, but that night made me fall in love with this quiet lake completely. In the evening, my friends and I were wrapped in quilts(裹着棉被) and stared at the stars on the terrace of the inn. I am a person who grew up in the city. From my impression(在我的印象里), there were not many stars in the sky since I was a child. So, when I saw the sky full of stars in Qinghai Lake, I was so surprised that I opened my mouth and didn't even dare to breathe(不敢呼吸), for fear of destroying this beautiful thing(生怕破坏了这美好的一切). All around me was so quiet, there was only the sound of the wind, and it seemed that only the stars, the lake and us were left in the world. The beauty of the entire starry sky and the silent lake took my breath away. . I will never forget Qinghai Lake that night.

## 21. 有趣的邻居/受欢迎的名人 / 人物
1. [Part 4] Describe a neighbor you are interested in 
You should say:

How you knew him/her 
What you do together 
And explain why you are interested in him/her

Describe a popular well-known person in your country 
You should say: 
Who this person is 
What he/she has done 
Why he/she is popular 
And explain how you feel about this person
   - Answer: 全国优秀教师张老师 (6.5~7)
   - Summary: 我想说说住在我们小区里的张老师，她是我们小区的“明星”，听说她在很多年前就被评为了“全国优秀教师”，我在报纸上还看到了关于她的报道，也经常看到很多她以前的学生来拜访她。现在她退休了，在小区里义务开办了科学兴趣小组，带小朋友们一起做小发明，我假期里有时候会去当她的助手，因为我很想了解一个优秀的科学教师是怎么上课的，她的激情和智慧也确实了我很多启发。
   - Content: I want to talk about Teacher Zhang who lives in my community. I heard that she was named "National Excellent Teacher(全国优秀教师)" before . I remember reading about her in the newspaper three years ago. The report mainly talked about her teaching career and also described her life after retirement. Originally, I didn't know that she was the Teacher Zhang that lived in my community. Later, when I saw her downstairs, I realized that she was the "celebrity" reported in the newspaper.

Now I often see many of her former students visit her, especially on Teacher's Day and Chinese New Year. There are many of her students, and some of them have become top leaders in our city. They bring a lot of gifts and fruits every time they come to see her, and Teacher Zhang is always happy to see her former students. Now she is retired, but Teacher Zhang is not idle (没闲下来). She set up a science interest group(开办了科学兴趣小组) in the community, and helps children make small inventions together. This interest class is free, as long as children can come to participate. There are many children who sign up(报名), and there are about dozens of people in each class. My own dream is to be an excellent teacher in the future, so I sometimes go to be her assistant during the holidays, because I really want to know how a good science teacher teaches. Her classes are very interesting, her life is lively and attractive, and children like her very much. Teacher Zhang's passion and wisdom have indeed inspired me a lot(激情和智慧确实给了我很多启发) and made me yearn for the teaching profession even more(让我对教师的职业更向往了).

## 22. 庆祝过的活动/花费甚少的外出日 / 事物
1. [Part 4] Describe an important event you celebrated 
You should say: 
What the event was 
When it happened 
Who attended the event 
And explain how you feel about the event

Describe a special day out that cost you little money/didn’t cost you much 
You should say: 
When was the day 
Where you went 
How much you spent 
And explain how you feel about the day
   - Answer: 免费参加端午节活动 (6.5~7)
   - Summary: 我想分享的是我的家乡在去年端午节的时候举办的赛龙舟活动，我们全家都去了。活动在我们家附近的一个码头举行，我们和别的家庭组成一个参赛队伍，最终我们取得了第三名的成绩，获得了一个粽子礼盒。我们全家都特别开心，因为活动不仅没有收取任何费用，我们还带了礼物回家。
   - Content: What I want to share is the dragon boat race held in my hometown during the Dragon Boat Festival last year. The Dragon Boat Festival, the Spring Festival, the Ching Ming Festival and the Mid-Autumn Festival are known as the four traditional Chinese festivals. The Dragon Boat Festival has a big influence all over the world(在世界上影响广泛), and some countries and regions in the world also have activities to celebrate the Dragon Boat Festival. Every year on the fifth day of the fifth lunar month(农历), China celebrates this Festival.

During the Dragon Boat Festival last year, my whole family went to the dragon boat race in my city. The event was held at a marina(码头) near our house, and everyone could sign up for the competition(报名参加比赛), with prizes for the top three(前三名还有奖品可以拿). My family and other families formed a team. To be honest, this was the first time my family had participated in a dragon boat race. My family and I had never rowed before, so I was very excited. I thought we would not win the prize , but as long as everyone participated happily it would be worth it. To my surprise, the other family we teamed with(和我们一起组队的另一个家庭) played this game every year , so they were very experienced. In the end, we got the third place and got a zongzi gift box. This was really beyond our expectations(出乎我们的意料). Our whole family had a great time because not only was there no charge for the event, but we also brought gifts home.

## 23. 喜欢一起聊天的朋友/学习、工作中的积极建议 / 人物
1. [Part 4] Describe a friend you like to talk with 
You should say 
Who he/she is 
What you like to talk about 
Why you like to talk with her 
And explain how you feel about him/her

Describe an occasion when someone gave you positive advice or suggestions about your work/study 
You should say: 
Who the person is 
What he/she said 
How the advice/suggestion affected you 
And explain how you felt about the advice/suggestion
   - Answer: 给我工作建议的大学同学Nancy (6.5~7)
   - Summary: 大学室友Nancy是我多年的挚友，她耐心聪慧如师长。初入职场时，我因效率低下被领导批评，Nancy建议用每日表格追踪进度、按重要性排序任务。这些方法让我工作效率大幅提升，重燃工作热情。
Encounter difficulties 遇到困难
Overwhelmed by tasks 被任务压垮
Frustrated 沮丧的
Track progress 追踪进度
Sort by importance 按重要性排序
Work efficiency 工作效率
Enthusiasm came back 重燃热情
   - Content: This topic reminds me of my friend Nancy. She was my classmate in the same major in college. We lived in the same dormitory for four years, and we were best friends in college. Now that we both work, we are still best friends even though we are not in the same city, and we are in touch(保持联系) almost every day.

Nancy is a very patient and very smart person. I often feel like she is a teacher, or a big sister who is much older than me, because she always has so much life experience to share with me. I always like to chat with her when I encounter difficulties(遇到困难) at work, and she always gives me a lot of useful suggestions. I am very grateful for her. I remember when I first entered the workplace, and because I was unfamiliar with the job, I always felt that it was difficult to get started. I wasn't very productive at that time because I was always overwhelmed by all sorts of little tasks(被各种各样的小事情所耽搁). My leader even criticized me a few times for this, which made me very frustrated(沮丧). I told Nancy about it, and even though she was just starting work at the time, she immediately advised me on(在…问题上提出建议) my problems. She told me that I could make a daily table to track my progress(追踪工作进度), and that I could also sort tasks by importance(按照任务的重要程度进行排序), so, I knew exactly what I should do first and what I could do later.

After doing what she said, I found that my work efficiency increased rapidly, and the enthusiasm for my work came back(工作的热情又回来了). I really love her so much.

## 24. 丢东西的经历/惊喜之事 / 事物
1. [Part 4] Describe an occasion that you lost something 
You should say: 
What you lost 
When and where you lost it 
What you did to find it 
And explain how you felt about it

Describe something that surprised you 
You should say: 
what it is 
How you found out about it 
What you did 
And explain whether it made you happy
   - Answer: 手机落在出租车上被朋友捡到 (6.5~7)
   - Summary: 我想分享最近我的手机差点不见的故事。上周我打车去市中心的商场，但是下车后我突然发现我的手机好像落在车上了。我给我的手机打电话试图联系司机，没想到接电话的却是我的一个朋友，原来我刚下车不久，他就上了同一辆车，当天晚上他就把手机给我送回来了。我觉得这件事真是太巧合了，同时我也觉得手机能够失而复得我实在太幸运了。
   - Content: Speaking of which, I have a hilarious yet magical thing to share with you, and this is the story of the recent “lost and found” of my phone.

Last week I went to the mall with my high school classmates to watch a movie, so on Sunday I took a taxi to the mall in the city center. I vividly remember(清晰地记得) that I was texting with my friends on my phone while in the car, but when I got out of the car, I suddenly realized that my phone was gone. I was very anxious at that time, because not only was the contact information of my friends on there, but also many precious photos were on my phone. I was afraid that if the phone was lost, these precious things would be gone(手机掉了之后，这些宝贵的东西就会不见了). So, I immediately recalled where the phone had been dropped. I realized that my phone seemed to be in the taxi. So, I immediately walked into a coffee shop, explained the situation to the clerk, and asked him to lend me his cell phone. I called my cell phone to try to contact the driver. The call was connected, but it was not the driver who answered(不是司机接的电话). To my great surprise, the person who answered the phone was another friend of mine. It turned out that(原来是) shortly after I got out of the car, he got into the same taxi and found a mobile phone in the back seat. My friend gave me the phone that night.

I think it's such a coincidence, and at the same time I think I'm so lucky and happy to have my phone back.

## 25. 送朋友的礼物/别人给你的衣服 / 事件
1. [Part 4] 送朋友的礼物
Describe a gift you gave to a friend
You should say:
When it happened
What gift it was
Who you gave it to 
And explain why you chose that gift
别人给你的衣服
Describe an item of clothing that someone gave you 
You should say:
What the clothing was
Who gave it to you 
When you got it 
And explain why this person gave you the clothing
   - Answer: 汝之蜜糖，彼之砒霜 (6.5~7)
   - Summary: 别人送了我一件衣服（what、who、when、why），我因为不喜欢一直没穿，但我的朋友偶然看到觉得非常适合他，就送给朋友当作礼物了（when、what、who 、why）
   - Content: On my birthday the year before last, my godmother gave me a dress as a birthday gift. Although I pretended to be very happy when I got the dress, I honestly didn't like the gift at all. The dress is dark blue, but a very old-fashioned(老气的) dark blue that looks like something my grandma would like. The dress is a long skirt that reaches all the way down to my feet(脚背). How was I expected to wear a dress this long as a 20 year old? Besides, the pattern on the front also looks very vintage with a red rose print on the chest of the dress. I was really speechless. I was pretty sure even my mother wouldn’t be seen dead wearing such a dress. To be honest, I really don't know why my godmother chose this dress for my 20th birthday.

I've never worn this dress, so it's been sitting in my closet the whole time. Three months ago, when a friend of mine came to my house and saw this dress in the closet, I was surprised to hear that she actually liked it. To be honest I didn't understand why she liked it. She is about the same age as me, so I couldn’t understand what she saw in it. In Chinese there is a saying that goes “my honey, and the other's arsenic (汝之蜜糖，彼之砒霜)”, which means one man’s meat is another man’s poison. In short, seeing that she liked this dress so much, and the size was just right for her, I gave it her on the spot(当场). My friend was so happy that as soon as she got home she took a selfie of herself in the dress and sent it to me. Anyway, this dress has finally found a suitable owner(这条裙子总算是找到了适合它的主人), and it has made my friend happy.

So this is the gift I gave to a friend. / So, this ugly dress is the item of clothing that.

## 27. 别人讲述的故事/收到特殊蛋糕 / 事件
1. [Part 4] 别人讲述的故事
Describe a story someone told you and remember
You should say:
What the story was about
Who told you this story
Why you remember it
And how you feel about it
收到特殊蛋糕
Describe a special cake you received from others 
You should say
When it happened
Where it happened
Who you got the cake from
And explain why it’s a special cake
   - Answer: 别人讲述了一个收到特殊蛋糕的故事 (6.5~7)
   - Summary: 在去年的一次同学聚会上，我碰到了因为去山区支教一年多不见的老朋友，她给我们分享了一个非常动人的故事。支教的山区条件艰苦，学生基础很差，但是她依然非常尽心尽力地去做自己能做的事情帮助那里的学生，在她快要离开的时候，正好赶上她的生日，她急匆匆去上课，推开门，学生们送给了她一个用糯米做成的蛋糕并祝她生日快乐。就像是苏格拉底所说的那样，教育是点燃火焰。我感觉孩子们的火被她点燃了。
   - Content: At a class reunion(同学聚会) last year, I met an old friend who I hadn't seen for over a year because she went to teach in the mountains and had missed the previous get together. It was great to have a catch up with her and to share some interesting stories. My friend shared a particularly moving story that left a deep impression on the people who heard it.(在场所有的人听了之后都不禁为之动容).

My old friend majored in(专业是…) teaching. After graduating from college, she decided to pay back some of her debt to society by volunteering as a teacher for underprivileged children in a rural area.(报答社会) So, she joined a charity organization and they sent her to teach as a volunteer in western China for three weeks(她跟着一个慈善组织去了中国西部的一个小农村里做志愿者支教三周). The conditions in the mountainous areas where she went were quite harsh(非常艰苦), and most of the students were left-behind children(留守儿童. This meant that the parents of these children had to go out to work to make a living(为了生计), while the children were either left at home alone, or in the care of an elderly grandparent. Some children were even left to take care of younger siblings(兄弟姐妹) on their own. In addition, the teaching conditions were not up-to-date and were very poor, but my friend was still very dedicated to doing what she could to help the students there (但是我这个朋友依然非常尽心尽力地去做自己能做的事情帮助那里的学生). The day before she was about to leave happened to be her birthday. She hurried to class and upon opening the door saw that her students had made her a cake made of glutinous rice(糯米. As soon as she walked in, they started singing and dancing around her, wishing her a happy birthday. Upon beholding this sight, tears immediately started to stream down her face. She had no idea that these children would know about her birthday and make her a cake under such miserable conditions. As Socrates(苏格拉底) said, education is the kindling of fire(教育是点燃火焰). I felt that the children's fire was lit by her, and at the same time, she was also lit by the fire of these innocent and lovely children(孩子们的火被她点燃了，同时她也被这群天真可爱的孩子们的火焰点燃了).

## 28. 语言学习/向长者学习技能 / 事物
1. [Part 4] 语言学习
Describe something that helped you learn a language
You should say 
What it is 
What language you learned
How it helped you learn the language
And how you felt about it
向长者学习技能
Describe a skill that you can learn from older people
You should say:
Why the skill can be learned from older people
How you will learn the skill from older people
And explain how you will feel if you master the skill
   - Answer: 向长者学习语言 (6.5~7)
   - Summary: 我的奶奶是俄语专业毕业的，在他们哪个年代，俄语在中国有非常广泛的应用，我和奶奶相处的时候，她就会教授给我一些常用的俄语词汇，并且和我用俄语对话，比如乌拉，达瓦里希之类的，这是我第一次学习外语，一种与中文截然不同的语言从我嘴里讲出来，我感觉十分的奇妙。
   - Content: My grandma came from a scholarly family (书香世家). In China at that time, very few girls were sent to school for education. However, my grandmother not only excelled at school but also went on to graduate from university with a degree in the Russian language. Her academic success was rewarded upon graduation when she was sent to Russia by the government. Of course at that time Russia was the major constituent part of the Soviet Union(前苏联. After returning to China, she became a translator of Russian for the Chinese Government.

Back then, Russian was widely used in China, because the former Soviet Union was like a big brother to China and offered us a lot of help. When I was a child, I got along with my grandmother, and she would teach me lots of common Russian vocabulary and try to converse with(和…交谈) me in the language. One phrase I remember is ура, товарищи, and there are others. For me as a child, this was the first time I had come into contact with(接触到) a foreign language, and it felt amazing to be able to produce words in this strange and foreign language.(一种与中文截然不同的语言从我嘴里讲出来，我感觉十分的奇妙). From these first steps, I continued my journey with the Russian language under my gran’s guidance(在奶奶的指导下). During the summer vacation three years ago, I accompanied my grandma on what might be her last trip to Russia. She was particularly moved during a trip to the old university where she had studied. Looking at the happy smile on her face, I too was also deeply touched. In this moment, I learned that language learning can bring us benefits of immeasurable value. For me, it's not just a language, it's something that can be used to survive, to create memories, to enhance our life-experience(而是一门可以用来生存的，用来创造价值的东西). I plan to choose Russian as a major when I go to university. I want to continue studying Russian, and strive to(争取) study in Russia in the future. After the completion of my time abroad, I want to follow in my grandmother’s footsteps by becoming a professional Russian translator and, in the process, contributing to my motherland.

So my grandmother helped me learn a language. / So this is the skill that I can learn from older people, namely my grandmother.

## 29. 童年玩具/生活中离不开的东西 / 事件
1. [Part 4] 童年玩具
Describe the toy you played with as a child
You should say:
What it was
What it was like
How you played with it
And explain why you played with it
生活中离不开的东西
Describe something that you can't live without (not a computer/phone)
You should say:
What it is
What you do with it
How it helps you in your life
And explain why you can't live without it
   - Answer: 离不开的大熊玩偶 (6.5~7)
   - Summary: 我有一只大熊玩偶，他从我小时候就一直陪伴着我，非常可爱，浑身是棕色的毛发，我每天都会抱着它睡觉，这只大熊能够带给我安心的感觉。现在他已经很旧了，我生活的也很痛苦，因此每天晚上睡觉必须要依靠它给我带来的安全感。我的生活已经离不开它了。
   - Content: I have been particularly interested in bears since I was a child, whether it’s brown bears, polar bears(北极熊) or black bears. Although bears are ferocious wild animals, they are fluffy and when they walk, they look very funny and cute. Bears are very smart, and their intelligence levels are very high when compared to other animals(智商在动物里面算是非常高的了). So for my 8th birthday, my aunt bought me a big bear doll as my birthday present. This bear is half the height of a human being. When I first received it, at the age of 8, it was taller than me. Now the bear doll has been with me for over 10 years.

With its brown fur and cowboy hat, I think it looks really cute, and also quite cool in its own way. Ever since I received this gift, it has maintained pride of place on my bedside table. I sleep with it every day, and this big bear brings me peace of mind(带给我安心的感觉). Sometimes I tell my secrets and troubles to it, and I always feel that it can understand me. With age and countless washes, some of the limbs have become loose and in parts it is quite threadbare. I have repaired it but it is still cracked(但是还是裂开了). My life is like this doll, miserable and unfixable(悲惨却又无法修补). I can’t do my work correctly, I can’t get along well with(和…相处得好) my colleagues, and I can’t even bear(忍受) to stay in the same room with my boss. I just broke up with my boyfriend recently, and just like the bear, my life has holes in many places(我的生活也到处脱线了), so I have to rely on the security it gives me every night to sleep(每天晚上我睡觉必须要依靠它给我带来的安全感). We keep each other warm and it reminds me that life is not so bad. It may seem strange but I feel me and this bear have become inseparable.

So this is the toy I played with as a child. / So this bear doll is something that I can’t live without.

## 30. 远距离步行/想共度时光的人/计划多人活动/照片/美丽天空/户外运动的地方 / 人物
1. [Part 4] 远距离步行/想共度时光的人/计划多人活动/照片/美丽天空/户外运动的地方
Describe an outdoor sport you would like to do
Describe a photo that you enjoy looking at 
Describe a time when you and some other people made a plan to do an activity
Describe a beautiful sky you enjoyed seeing
Describe a place you went to and an outdoor activity you did there
   - Answer: 和家人一起计划了远距离步行，看到了美丽的日落并拍照 (6.5~7)
   - Summary: 我想尝试的一个户外徒步活动，我邀请我的家人朋友一起，并且在徒步的过程中看到了美丽的日落，并照下了我最喜欢的一张照片。
户外徒步活动 - outdoor trekking; 徒步 - hiking; 日落 - sunset; 照片 - snapshot; 山谷 - valley; 峰顶 - peak; 色彩斑斓的 - vibrant; 愉悦的 - heartening; 难以磨灭 - indelible; 探索 - exploration.
   - Content: I have always yearned to try trekking as an outdoor activity to immerse myself in nature and challenge my physical endurance. Last summer, I decided to organize a hiking trip along a picturesque trail with my family and a few close friends. Setting off early in the morning, we were greeted by the tranquil sounds of the forest and the crisp mountain air.

As we ascended, the panoramic views unfolded before us, showcasing lush valleys and majestic peaks stretching as far as the eye could see. The camaraderie among us grew stronger, filled with shared laughter and encouraging words to conquer steep inclines. It was heartening to witness everyone pushing their limits and offering support along the way.

As the sun began its descent, casting a warm glow over the landscape, we reached a clearing overlooking a serene lake. The sky transformed into a canvas of vibrant hues - streaks of orange, pink, and gold painted across the horizon, creating a breathtaking sunset. Mesmerized by the ethereal beauty before us, I captured the moment with my camera, preserving it as my favorite snapshot from the trek.

The experience of witnessing such a stunning sunset amidst the company of loved ones left an indelible mark on my heart. It not only strengthened our bonds but also instilled a profound appreciation for the wonders of the natural world. This unforgettable hiking adventure will forever hold a special place in my memory, reminding me of the joy found in exploration and shared moments of beauty in the great outdoors.

## 31. 给别人建议 + 擅长做计划的人 + 乐于助人的人+ 鼓励保护自然的人 / 人物
1. [Part 4] 同学可以结合题库的具体问题，练习素材。
1.为了更好的匹配每一道题，素材本身的字数会超过真实的考试同学们能表达字数。
2.针对不同的问法，同学的开头和结尾需要进行调整。
3.一定要注意表达的自然程度~必要时增加重音，表情和手势
   - Answer: 一位环保引路人的言传身教 (6~6.5)
   - Summary: 我的环境科学教授陈博士。她展现规划才能的具体表现是精心设计课程大纲并完美组织湿地考察，确保每个教学环节都高效利用。她乐于助人的本质体现在课后花费额外时间耐心指导学生处理复杂数据分析。正是某次湿地考察中，她指着芦苇间的塑料残骸，将抽象环保概念转化为具体行动号召，成为激励我保护自然的关键人物。这一鼓励直接促使我在家庭聚会上劝阻叔叔铺平花园的计划，通过解释生态价值并建议替代方案，最终使他改变决定。这段经历完整呈现了优秀规划能力、真诚助人精神与有效环保倡导如何形成影响闭环。
   - Content: The person who seamlessly connects these topics is my environmental science professor, Dr. Chen, a master planner and inherently helpful individual. Her meticulously structured syllabus and flawlessly executed field trips to ecosystems like local wetlands demonstrated exceptional organizational skill, ensuring every educational moment was maximized.

Her willingness to spend extra hours after class, patiently guiding students through complex data analysis, truly defined her helpful nature. It was during one such wetland visit that she became my pivotal encourager for protecting nature. Pointing at plastic debris amidst the reeds, she made the abstract concept of conservation tangibly urgent, urging us to adopt sustainable daily habits.

This inspiration directly led to my own act of giving advice. At a family gathering, when my uncle planned to pave over his garden, I advised against it, explaining its ecological value and suggesting permeable alternatives. Influenced by Dr. Chen’s teachings, my reasoning resonated with him, and he revised his plans. This experience highlighted how a planner’s structure, a helper’s support, and an encourager’s spark can collectively empower one to advocate for positive change, completing a meaningful cycle of influence.

## 32. 自行车/摩托车/汽车旅行 + 外国的短期停留 + 想见的名人 + 花费超过预期的物品 / 事物

1.为了更好的匹配每一道题，素材本身的字数会超过真实的考试同学们能表达字数。
2.针对不同的问法，同学的开头和结尾需要进行调整。
3.一定要注意表达的自然程度~必要时增加重音，表情和手势
   - Answer: 骑行、旅行与未竟的梦想清单 (6~6.5)
   - Summary: 我一直梦想骑摩托车穿越德国的黑森林，感受蜿蜒山路与古老城堡的魅力。之后，我将短暂停留奥地利的萨尔茨堡，沉浸在其浓厚的音乐氛围与阿尔卑斯风光中。我渴望见到的名人是指挥家古斯塔沃·杜达梅尔——虽然相遇机会渺茫，但他的艺术激情正是我探访这座音乐之城的缘由。而整个旅程中，令我花费远超预期的，是在萨尔茨堡老城一眼相中的手工雕刻音乐盒。它奏着莫扎特《魔笛》的旋律，其精美工艺让我毫不犹豫地超出了预算，但它也因此成为融合了旅途冒险、文化共鸣与艺术灵感的最佳纪念。
   - Content: I'd love to take a motorbike trip through Germany's Black Forest, following winding roads past villages and castles. After this ride, I'd cross into Austria to stay briefly in Salzburg, drawn by its musical heritage and alpine scenery.

Interestingly, the famous person I most want to meet, conductor Gustavo Dudamel, connects to this. While I know meeting him is unlikely, his passion is why I'd visit Mozart's birthplace—to feel that artistic energy.

The item I bought that cost more than expected ties this together. In Salzburg, I’d find a beautifully hand-carved music box playing a tune from Mozart’s The Magic Flute. Initially, I’d budget for a simple souvenir, but the craftsmanship would convince me to spend far more—a tangible reminder of the journey, the place, and the inspiration from artists like Dudamel. This trip blends adventure, culture, admiration, and a personal, though costly, keepsake.

## 33. 喜欢画画的孩子 + 最近读过的故事 + 有趣的建筑 + 不享受的音乐活动 / 事件
1. [Part 4] 同学可以结合题库的具体问题，练习素材。

3.一定要注意表达的自然程度~必要时增加重音，表情和手势
   - Answer: 一次多维艺术之旅 (6.5~7)
   - Summary: 我八岁的侄女莉莉，她想象力丰富，酷爱画画。她的画作充满童趣，最近还根据她读的一个关于月宫玉兔的中国童话创作了一系列素描。我受此启发也读了那个故事，其中蕴含的善良与冒险精神令我回味无穷。这让我联想到上海一座造型奇特、形似兔耳的“月兔塔”现代美术馆，其建筑巧妙融合传统与未来元素。然而，上个月我参加的一场前卫音乐活动却令人失望——实验性的不和谐音效显得杂乱无章，让我深感艺术表达需与观众建立真挚联结。这些经历共同印证了真正打动人心的艺术所具有的感染力。
   - Content: The child I’d like to describe is my eight-year-old niece, Lily, who has a vivid imagination and loves drawing more than anything. Her sketches are not just simple pictures; they are windows into her playful mind. Recently, she showed me a series of drawings inspired by a story she’d read—a Chinese folk tale about a magical rabbit living in a moon palace. I was so intrigued that I decided to read the story myself. It was a beautiful narrative about kindness and adventure, which lingered in my thoughts long after I finished it.

Interestingly, that tale reminded me of an unusual building I once visited in Shanghai—the “Moon Rabbit Tower,” a modern art museum with a distinctive, curved design that resembles a rabbit’s ear. Its architecture blends traditional motifs with futuristic elements, making it stand out in the city’s skyline. I recalled wandering through its exhibits, marveling at how stories and structures can intertwine to create something truly captivating.

Last month, however, I attended a musical activity that didn’t resonate with me at all. It was an avant-garde performance where the musicians experimented with dissonant sounds and random noise, claiming it was “artistic innovation.” While I appreciate creativity, the experience felt chaotic and lacked the harmony I enjoy. It made me reflect on how art, whether through a child’s drawing, a timeless story, or an interesting building, should connect with people on a deeper level. Unlike Lily’s joyful sketches or the enchanting Moon Rabbit Tower, that musical event left me feeling disconnected, underscoring the importance of authenticity in artistic expression.

In summary, from Lily’s inspiring drawings to the folk tale and the imaginative building, these experiences highlight the beauty of art that speaks to the heart. The disappointing musical activity, in contrast, served as a reminder that not all creative endeavors succeed in forging that emotional bond.

## 34. 朋友学的技能 + App/程序 + 机智解决问题的人 + 鼓励别人做不愿做的事 / 人物
1. [Part 4] 同学可以结合题库的具体问题，练习素材。
1.为了更好的匹配每一道题，素材本身的字数会超过真实的考试同学们能表达字数。
2.针对不同的问法，同学的开头和结尾需要进行调整。
3.一定要注意表达的自然程度~必要时增加重音，表情和手势
   - Answer: 技能学习与鼓励 (6.5~7)
   - Summary: 我想分享朋友Leo自学Python编程的经历。起初他为自动化工作而学，后来却深深入迷。上月我们团队遇到数据处理难题，需手动分析庞大而复杂的数据集，耗时且易错。

同事David提出了巧妙方案：建议使用“Automate”应用程序，并结合Leo的编程技能，设计了高效工作流。然而，Leo因信心不足不愿主导编码。我鼓励他接受挑战，强调这是检验学习成果的良机。

最终，Leo鼓起勇气完成了脚本，成功解决问题。这件事让我看到，一项技能、一个实用程序、一次机智解难和适时鼓励如何串联，将犹豫转化为实实在在的成就。
   - Content: I’d like to talk about my friend Leo, who recently taught himself Python programming through online courses. Initially, he just wanted to automate some repetitive tasks at work, but he soon became fascinated with its potential. His new skill turned out to be incredibly useful when our team faced a major data processing issue last month. We had to compile and analyze a huge dataset manually, which was extremely time-consuming and prone to errors.

That’s when my colleague, David, demonstrated a clever solution. Instead of following the tedious manual process, he suggested we could use a specific app called “Automate” to handle the task. This program allows users to create custom workflows without deep coding knowledge. David, however, combined it with Leo’s Python skills in a brilliant way. He designed a simple interface in “Automate” to pre-process the files, then used Leo’s Python script to perform the complex analysis automatically. It was a stroke of genius that saved us days of work.

Interestingly, Leo was hesitant to take the lead on the coding part at first, feeling his skills weren’t professional enough. Seeing his self-doubt, I encouraged him to embrace the challenge. I reminded him of how far he’d come on his own and assured him that this real-world problem was the perfect chance to apply his knowledge. After some persuasion, he agreed. We worked together, with me supporting him on the logical flow while he wrote the script.

The result was a great success. Not only was the problem solved efficiently, but Leo’s confidence soared. This experience showed me how a learned skill, a useful app, and clever problem-solving can intertwine. More importantly, it highlighted the power of encouragement—sometimes, all someone needs is a little push to unlock their potential and turn reluctance into achievement.

## 35. 商场 + 禁用手机的场合 + 微笑的场合 + 近期观影 / 地点

3.一定要注意表达的自然程度~必要时增加重音，表情和手势
   - Answer: 商场影院的温馨时光 (6.5~7)
   - Summary: 我常去的"银河广场"购物中心顶楼有家影院，我最近在那里观看了温情电影《最后的信》。这部影片讲述90年代书信传递亲情的故事，与数字时代形成鲜明对比。观影时影院严禁使用手机，这种"数字戒断"起初令人不安，却让我更投入剧情。最打动我的是观察周围观众——在动人场景时，许多人脸上浮现出会心的微笑，那是种基于共情的真诚表达。这次经历让我思考，即便在商业科技空间，我们仍能找到真实的人际联结与情感共鸣。
   - Content: The shopping mall I frequent is the "Galaxy Plaza" near my home, a sprawling complex that combines retail therapy with leisure activities. What makes it special is its rooftop cinema, where I recently watched a heartwarming film called "The Last Letter." This Chinese drama, set in the 1990s, explores family bonds through handwritten correspondence—a poignant contrast to our digital age.

The cinema experience itself provided the perfect occasion when phone use was strictly prohibited. Before the movie started, clear announcements and signs reminded us to silence our devices, and ushers politely ensured compliance. Initially, I felt that familiar twinge of anxiety being disconnected, but this digital detox soon became liberating. It allowed me to be fully immersed in the film’s emotional journey without the constant pull of notifications.

The most memorable moment, however, was observing the audience around me. In the dim light, I noticed subtle smiles spreading across people’s faces during particularly tender scenes—a grandfather reading a letter to his granddaughter, a moment of reconciliation between siblings. These weren’t broad, dramatic smiles, but gentle, genuine expressions of empathy and recognition. It was a powerful reminder of cinema’s unique ability to create shared emotional experiences.

Leaving the mall that evening, I carried with me more than just the film’s storyline. I reflected on how a simple trip to a familiar mall had offered such a rich tapestry of experiences: the anticipation of entertainment, the unusual quiet of being phoneless, and the beautiful, silent communion of strangers smiling together in the dark. It highlighted how even in our commercialized, tech-driven spaces, there remains room for authentic human connection and reflection.

## 36. 完美工作 + 想拥有的科技产品 + 擅长做计划的人 + 发挥想象力 / 事物

   - Answer: 理想中的工作 (6~6.5)
   - Summary: 我的理想职业是未来城市或智能生活系统的概念设计师，在创意与科技的交汇处工作，核心在于发挥想象力去构想未来的生活方式。为了实现它，我渴望拥有一台先进的全息增强现实头盔，它能将抽象概念转化为可交互的三维原型。我的表姐安娜则是一位善于规划的典范，她能把我天马行空的想法分解为可行的步骤。一次我与她畅谈关于自给式森林社区的奇幻构想，我的想象力自由驰骋，而她的规划思维则帮助我将幻想提炼为更成熟的愿景。这让我明白：想象力点燃梦想，而规划则为实现梦想搭建桥梁。
   - Content: My ideal job has always been something at the intersection of creativity and technology—perhaps a concept designer for future cities or smart living systems. In this role, I wouldn't just design buildings or products; I’d craft holistic experiences, imagining how people will live, work, and connect in tomorrow's world. The core of this work would be pure imagination, envisioning possibilities beyond current constraints.

To truly excel in such a forward-thinking field, there's a technological product I’ve longed to own: an advanced augmented reality (AR) headset with full holographic capabilities. Imagine being able to visualize and manipulate 3D models of your ideas in real space, turning abstract concepts into tangible, interactive prototypes. This tool wouldn't just be a gadget; it would be an extension of my creative mind.

My cousin Anna, a project manager for a major tech firm, embodies the perfect counterpart to this imaginative work. She is exceptionally skilled at planning, able to break down even the most visionary ideas into logical, actionable steps. I remember describing my dream job to her once—a whimsical concept about self-sustaining forest communities. While I got lost in the fantastical details, she immediately began sketching a phased development plan, considering resources, timelines, and potential challenges. Her ability to ground dreams in reality is truly inspiring.

This conversation with Anna was itself a time when I used my imagination vividly. As I described those floating garden pods and communal learning hubs, my mind raced with possibilities. Yet, through Anna’s structured questions, my imagination was channeled and refined, moving from pure fantasy to a more considered vision. It was a powerful lesson: imagination sparks the dream, but planning builds the bridge to reach it. Ultimately, my ideal career combines these two forces—using tools like the AR headset to fuel boundless creativity, while relying on the mindset of planners like Anna to bring those visions meaningfully to life.

## 37. 让你骄傲的家人 + 对家庭重要的东西 + 鼓励你保护自然的人 + 乐于助人的人 / 人物
1. [Part 4] 同学可以结合题库的具体问题，练习素材。
1.为了更好的匹配每一道题，素材本身的字数会超过真实的考试同学们能表达字数。
2.针对不同的问法，同学的开头和结尾需要进行调整。
3.一定要注意表达的自然程度~必要时增加重音，表情和手势
   - Answer: 家庭骄傲与自然守护的故事 (6~6.5)
   - Summary: 最让我骄傲的家人是我年过八旬的祖母。她五十多年来悉心照料着庭院里的一株茶树，这株活着的传家宝象征着耐心、坚韧与土地的联结，是我们家族重要的精神图腾。祖母也是我环保意识的启蒙者，她以自然农法养护茶树，教我“向大地借用，必以照料偿还”的道理。她更是我认识的最乐于助人的人，经营的小店成为社区枢纽，默默帮助邻里。在她身上，养护植物、保护自然与帮助他人实现了统一，都源于同样的尊重与关怀。她的传承不仅是茶香，更是一种自觉、互助的生活态度。
   - Content: The family member who makes me immensely proud is my grandmother. Now in her eighties, she has nurtured a tea plant in our courtyard for over fifty years—a living heirloom that represents something profoundly important to our family. More than just a plant, it symbolizes patience, resilience, and our connection to the land. Every spring, our family gathering to pick its leaves is a cherished ritual, grounding us in shared history and simple values.

This tea plant is also at the heart of how I learned to protect nature. My grandmother was the first person who encouraged me to see the natural world not as a resource to be used, but as a partner to be respected. As a child, I watched her care for this plant without chemicals, explaining how healthy soil and balanced ecosystems mattered more than quick yields. "We borrow from the earth," she would say while teaching me to compost kitchen scraps for the plant, "so we must return the care." Her gentle lessons turned my childhood curiosity into a lifelong commitment to environmental stewardship.

Her ethos of care extends beyond nature to people. My grandmother is, fundamentally, the most helpful person I know. Her small grocery shop in our village has been a community hub for decades. She remembers every family's needs, delivers groceries to elderly neighbors without being asked, and uses her tea gatherings to mediate minor disputes or offer quiet comfort. Her help is never grandstanding; it's woven into the daily fabric of life, showing that protecting nature and helping people are two sides of the same coin—both rooted in respect and sustained care.

In her, I see a powerful unity: the tea plant she nurtures, the environmental values she instilled, and the community she sustains are all expressions of the same principle. She taught me that what makes our family proud isn’t grand achievements, but how we tend to the living world—both the plant in our courtyard and the community around us. Her legacy isn't just in the tea we drink, but in the conscious, helpful life she inspired me to lead.

## 38. 二手物品网站/商店/购物服务/见过产品的广告 / 事件
1. [Part 4] 同学可以结合题库的具体问题，练习素材。
1. 为了更好的匹配每一道题，素材本身的字数会超过真实的考试同学们能表达字数。
2. 针对不同的问法，同学的开头和结尾需要进行调整。
3. 一定要注意表达的自然程度～必要时增加重音，表情和手势
   - Answer: 和朋友一起在伦敦逛商店 (6.5~7)
   - Summary: 好的，我想分享一次在伦敦旅行的购物经历。当时我和朋友在科文特花园附近一条迷人的小巷里，偶然发现了一家迷人的中古店，由于我对古董手表有浓厚兴趣，便立刻被吸引。

这家店出售各类复古钟表物品，例如经典怀表、老式制表工具和复古广告海报。商品保存状况极佳且独具魅力，让我驻足良久。其中一枚劳力士手表尤为引人注目，这个品牌以卓越品质闻名。我曾看过其1960年代的一则广告，内容描绘探险家与成功人士，将手表与精准耐用特性相关联，这则广告令我印象深刻，也让我对该产品更加青睐。
   - Content: Well, I want to talk about a time during a trip to London with a friend. At that time, I visited a a second hand shop because I have a keen interest in vintage watches, I remember we stumbled upon a fascinating vintage store in a charming alley near Covent Garden.
I could recall the store sold a variety of vintage horological items, such as classic timepieces, old watchmaking tools, and antique advertising posters. I was captivated for a long time because the products were in remarkably good condition and had a unique charm.
One item, in particular, caught my eye: a watch from Rolex, a brand renowned for its quality. I had previously seen a memorable advertisement for Rolex from the 1960s, which featured explorers and achievers, associating the watch with precision and endurance. I was deeply impressed by that ad, which made me appreciate the product even more.
Furthermore, the store service was excellent. The staff was exceptionally knowledgeable and patient, offering detailed histories of each piece without being pushy. After much deliberation, I ended up spending a significant amount of money and purchased a classic, elegant Omega Seamaster from the 1970s and a beautifully aged leather watch box. It was a truly rewarding shopping experience that combined my passion with history.

词汇与搭配总结.

Keen interest	浓厚的兴趣	/kiːn ˈɪntrəst/.
Stumbled upon	偶然发现	/ˈstʌmbld əˈpɒn/.
