Horological items	钟表类物品	/ˌhɒrəˈlɒdʒɪk(ə) l ˈaɪtəmz/.
Classic timepieces	经典时计	/ˈklæsɪk ˈtaɪmpiːsɪz/.
Remarkably good condition	保存极佳	/rɪˈmɑːkəbli ɡʊd kənˈdɪʃ(ə) n/.
Unique charm	独特的魅力	/juˈniːk tʃɑːm/.
Caught my eye	吸引了我的目光	/kɔːt maɪ aɪ/.
Renowned for	以...闻名	/rɪˈnaʊnd fɔː(r)/.
Memorable advertisement	令人难忘的广告	/ˈmem(ə) rəbl ədˈvɜːtɪsmənt/.
Precision and endurance	精准与耐用	/prɪˈsɪʒ(ə) n ənd ɪnˈdjʊərəns/.
Exceptionally knowledgeable	知识非常渊博	/ɪkˈsepʃənəli ˈnɒlɪdʒəbl/.
Without being pushy	不强求推销	/wɪˈðaʊt ˈbiːɪŋ ˈpʊʃi/.
After much deliberation	经过深思熟虑	/ˈɑːftə(r) mʌtʃ dɪˌlɪbəˈreɪʃ(ə) n/.
Rewarding experience	有收获的经历	/rɪˈwɔːdɪŋ ɪkˈspɪəriəns/.
Charming alley	迷人的小巷	/ˈtʃɑːmɪŋ ˈæli/.
Antique advertising posters	复古广告海报	/ænˈtiːk ˈædvətaɪzɪŋ ˈpəʊstəz/.
Deeply impressed	印象非常深刻	/ˈdiːpli ɪmˈprest/.
Classic and elegant	经典而优雅	/ˈklæsɪk ənd ˈelɪɡənt/.
Combining passion with history	将热情与历史结合	/kəmˈbaɪnɪŋ ˈpæʃ(ə) n wɪð ˈhɪst(ə) ri/.

## 39. 想再看的电影/奇装异服的人/熊孩子/搞笑电影/有趣小说or故事 / 事件
1. [Part 4] 同学可以结合题库的具体问题，练习素材。
1. 为了更好的匹配每一道题，素材本身的字数会超过真实的考试同学们能表达字数。
2. 针对不同的问法，同学的开头和结尾需要进行调整。
3. 一定要注意表达的自然程度～必要时增加重音，表情和手势
   - Answer: 看流浪地球遇到熊孩子 (6.5~7)
   - Summary: 我想讨论的电影是《流浪地球2》，这部国产科幻巨制的前传。我在首映周末于本地IMAX影院观看了这部由导演郭帆执导的科幻史诗。
影片不仅以发人深省的剧情吸引我，更以沉浸式视听效果令人折服——震撼的音效与逼真的视觉呈现让巨型发动机触手可及，如此极致的体验让我决定流媒体上线后要二刷。

不过观影过程有个小插曲：前排身着全套宇航服的小影迷在精彩场景时不断惊叫，屡次打破我的沉浸感。虽然我选择克制现场争执以免影响他人，但始终认为家长有责任约束孩子在公共场合的行为，这是对他人观影体验的基本尊重。
   - Content: The film I'd like to talk about is "The Wandering Earth II," a prequel to the famous Chinese sci-fi movie. I watched it during its opening weekend in a local IMAX cinema.
The film is a produced by a talented director called Guo Fan, and it's a grand-scale science fiction epic. The movie is about humanity's monumental effort to build enormous engines to propel the Earth out of the solar system to escape an expanding sun. It brilliantly explores themes of global unity, sacrifice, and survival against impossible odds.
I found it so compelling not just for its thought-provoking plot but also for the immersive audiovisual experience. The sound design was powerful, and the visual effects were stunningly realistic, making the colossal planetary engines feel tangible. I was so satisfied with the experience that I plan to rewatch it once it's available on streaming platforms.
However, the viewing experience was slightly marred by a small incident. A young boy, who was also a huge fan, was sitting a few rows ahead. He was wearing a detailed astronaut costume, complete with a helmet, which was quite noticeable. Throughout the film, he kept exclaiming loudly at exciting moments. I was incredibly annoyed, as it constantly broke my immersion. I handled it by refraining from confronting him during the movie, believing it would cause a bigger disturbance. But I strongly felt that the child's parents had an obligation to manage their child's behavior in a public setting to ensure it didn't detract from others' enjoyment.

词汇与搭配总结.
Science fiction epic	科幻史诗	/ˈsaɪəns ˈfɪkʃ(ə) n ˈepɪk/.
Monumental effort	巨大的努力	/ˌmɒnjuˈmentl ˈefət/.

Immersive audiovisual experience	沉浸式的视听体验	/ɪˈmɜːsɪv ˌɔːdiəʊˈvɪʒuəl ɪkˈspɪəriəns/.

## 40. 有用的书/别人向你道歉/演讲经历/告诉朋友实情/朋友的争执/印象深刻的谈话/感兴趣的科学领域/有趣老人/学科 / 事物
1. [Part 4] 同学可以结合题库的具体问题，练习素材。
1. 为了更好的匹配每一道题，素材本身的字数会超过真实的考试同学们能表达字数。
2. 针对不同的问法，同学的开头和结尾需要进行调整。
3. 一定要注意表达的自然程度～必要时增加重音，表情和手势
   - Answer: 和同样喜欢人工智能的朋友讨论 (6.5~7)
   - Summary: 我想谈谈对人工智能的兴趣。在学校图书馆读到斯图尔特·罗素所著的《人类兼容》后，我的探索欲被真正点燃。并和朋友进行讨论。
   - Content: I’d like to discuss my interest in Artificial Intelligence. My fascination truly deepened after I read a book called "Human Compatible" by Stuart Russell, which I got in my school library.
One of my professor introduced this book to me, this book was incredibly enlightening because it clarified many misconceptions I had. It argues that the common goal of building AI to simply optimize a fixed objective is flawed and potentially dangerous. Instead, it proposes a new foundation for AI where machines are designed to be inherently uncertain about human preferences, thus prioritizing human oversight.
This knowledge played out during a casual conversation with a group of friends. We were discussing AI's future, and one friend confidently stated that superintelligent AI would inevitably be benevolent by default. Remembering the book's core argument, I immediately correcting him, explaining that without careful design, an AI optimizing a poorly-specified goal could lead to unintended catastrophic consequences. I elaborated in detail on what I had learned.
afterwards I felt quite conflicted. My friend was visibly embarrassed and somewhat angry, feeling I had shown him up in front of others, and we had a brief argument. The situation was resolved, he apologized to me later that evening for his overreaction. I also apologized for my somewhat pedantic tone and for not being more tactful. Although there was a minor conflict, the incident left a deep impression on me because of the intense stimulation and freshness that came from that intellectual discussion and collision of ideas. Even though we almost had a big quarrel, still, I enjoy the process of exchanging ideas and personal opinions.

词汇与搭配总结.
Fascination deepened	兴趣加深	/ˌfæsɪˈneɪʃ(ə) n ˈdiːpənd/.
Incredibly enlightening	非常有启发性	/ɪnˈkredəbli ɪnˈlaɪtnɪŋ/.
Clarified misconceptions	澄清了误解	/ˈklærəfaɪd ˌmɪskənˈsepʃ(ə) nz/.
Optimize a fixed objective	优化一个固定目标	/ˈɒptɪmaɪz ə fɪkst əbˈdʒektɪv/.
Flawed and dangerous	有缺陷且危险	/flɔːd ənd ˈdeɪndʒərəs/.
Proposes a new foundation	提出一个新的基础	/prəˈpəʊzɪz ə njuː faʊnˈdeɪʃ(ə) n/.
Inherently uncertain	本质上是不确定的	/ɪnˈherəntli ʌnˈsɜːtn/.
Prioritizing human oversight	优先考虑人类监督	/praɪˈɒrətaɪzɪŋ ˈhjuːmən ˈəʊvəsaɪt/.
Casual conversation	随意交谈	/ˈkæʒuəl ˌkɒnvəˈseɪʃ(ə) n/.

Unintended consequences	意想不到的后果	/ˌʌnɪnˈtendɪd ˈkɒnsɪkwənsɪz/.
Showed him up	让他难堪	/ʃəʊd hɪm ʌp/.
Pedantic tone	卖弄学问的语气	/pɪˈdæntɪk təʊn/.
Being more tactful	更委婉一些	/ˈbiːɪŋ mɔː(r) ˈtæktfl/.
Intellectual discussion	智力讨论	/ˌɪntəˈlektʃuəl dɪˈskʌʃ(ə) n/.
Collision of ideas	思想的碰撞	/kəˈlɪʒ(ə) n əv aɪˈdɪəz/.
Left a deep impression	留下深刻印象	/left ə diːp ɪmˈpreʃ(ə) n/.
Visible embarrassed	明显尴尬	/ˈvɪzəbl ɪmˈbærəst/.
Core argument	核心论点	/kɔːr ˈɑːɡjumənt/.

## 41. 有好习惯的朋友/经营家族企业的人/重要的好朋友/聪明的人/钦佩的创作者/喜欢的歌手或乐队/爱唱歌的朋友 / 人物
1. [Part 4] 同学可以结合题库的具体问题，练习素材。
1. 为了更好的匹配每一道题，素材本身的字数会超过真实的考试同学们能表达字数。
2. 针对不同的问法，同学的开头和结尾需要进行调整。
3. 一定要注意表达的自然程度～必要时增加重音，表情和手势
   - Answer: 我的一个喜欢说唱的朋友 (6.5~7)
   - Summary: 我要介绍的是我十分敬佩的朋友Leo。我们相识于大学时代，他来自一个以小型制造业闻名的城市。

令我印象深刻的是，他家族经营着一项专门生产各类扑克牌的生意，这份产业由他父亲传承下来。大学毕业后，Leo接手了家族企业。我钦佩他并非因为家业，而是他能在兼顾生意之余，始终坚持着作为说唱歌手的梦想。

最让我叹服的是他的经营智慧。当桌游在年轻人中兴起时，他敏锐地开辟了定制卡牌的新业务线，成功吸引了大量年轻客户。与此同时，他的说唱事业也风生水起，不仅在社交媒体拥有大量粉丝，还经常进行周末巡演。
   - Content: I’m going to talk about my friend, Leo, whom I truly admire. I first met him during our university days. He's from a city known for its small manufacturing industries.

I remember he told me that his family runs a specialized business producing all kinds of playing cards, a trade passed down from his father. After graduating, Leo took over the business. I really admire him not because of his family business, but because of his remarkable ability to balance this responsibility with his passion for being a rap artist.

What impressed me the most was his ingenuity. For instance, how he revitalized the business was by capitalizing on the trend of tabletop games among young people. He launched a new line of custom-designed card games for these games, which attracted a wave of new orders. Simultaneously, his rap career is thriving; he has a substantial following on social media and frequently goes on weekend tours.

He manages this demanding schedule is through meticulous time management and unwavering discipline. He dedicates his mornings to factory management and his evenings to writing lyrics and recording. When I attend his live performances is immense pride. His creativity and determination to succeed in both arenas are truly inspirational. Although he must be exhausted, his daily perseverance is a testament to his strong character.

词汇与搭配总结.

Truly admire	非常钦佩	/ˈtruːli ədˈmaɪə(r)/.

Substantial following	大量的粉丝	/səbˈstænʃl ˈfɒləʊɪŋ/.
Meticulous time management	精细的时间管理	/məˈtɪkjələs taɪm ˈmænɪdʒmənt/.

## 42. 和亲友享受的晚餐/社交媒体趣事/家中老物件/突然停电/传统故事 / 事物
1. [Part 4] 同学可以结合题库的具体问题，练习素材。
1. 为了更好的匹配每一道题，素材本身的字数会超过真实的考试同学们能表达字数。
2. 针对不同的问法，同学的开头和结尾需要进行调整。
3. 一定要注意表达的自然程度～必要时增加重音，表情和手势
   - Answer: 春节停电 (6.5~7)
   - Summary: 我们在灯光下共进晚餐，温暖的烛光反而营造了格外亲密温馨的氛围。我将这个独特的经历拍成视频分享到社交媒体，使这个意外之夜变得比往常更加特别和难忘。
   - Content: I’d like to share my experience of celebrating the Spring Festival, also known as Chinese New Year, which occurred last year at my grandparents' house. It happened on New Year's Eve, the most important time for family reunions. We were in my grandparents' cozy apartment in my hometown.

I had a wonderful reunion with my close families. The celebration is rooted in a fascinating traditional legend about a monster named Nian, who was said to appear at the end of the year to terrorize villagers. People discovered that Nian was afraid of the color red, bright lights, and loud noises, which is why we now have customs like pasting red couplets, setting off firecrackers, and giving money in red envelopes.

We were celebrating by preparing and enjoying a lavish feast with traditional dishes like fish, symbolizing surplus, and dumplings, representing wealth. However, in the middle of dinner, the power went out. It wasn't just our building; the entire district experienced a blackout due to a malfunction at the local power plant. We waited for a long time, but the power wasn't restored.

My grandmother solved the problem by retrieving a family heirloom, an old but remarkably durable flashlight that belonged to her father. It had a long history but was still fully functional. We ended up finishing our dinner by flashlight. I felt that this unexpected event made the evening even more special and memorable than usual. The warm, flickering light created an incredibly intimate atmosphere. We even shared the story with friends via WeChat and recorded a short video of our unique celebration to post on social media. It turned a potential inconvenience into a uniquely heartwarming experience.

词汇与搭配总结.
Family reunions	家庭团聚	/ˈfæməli ˌriːˈjuːnjənz/.
Rooted in	根源于	/ˈruːtɪd ɪn/.

Lavish feast	丰盛的大餐	/ˈlævɪʃ fiːst/.

Representing wealth	代表财富	/ˌreprɪˈzentɪŋ welθ/.
Took an unexpected turn	发生意想不到的转折	/tʊk ən ˌʌnɪkˈspektɪd tɜːn/.
Power went out	停电了	/ˈpaʊə(r) went aʊt/.
Experienced a blackout	经历停电	/ɪkˈspɪəriənst ə ˈblækaʊt/.
Malfunction	故障	/ˌmælˈfʌŋkʃn/.
Family heirloom	传家宝	/ˈfæməli ˈeəluːm/.
Remarkably durable	非常耐用	/rɪˈmɑːkəbli ˈdjʊərəbl/.
Fully functional	功能完好	/ˈfʊli ˈfʌŋkʃənl/.
By candlelight	借着烛光	/baɪ ˈkændllaɪt/.
Flickering light	闪烁的光	/ˈflɪkərɪŋ laɪt/.
Intimate atmosphere	亲密温馨的氛围	/ˈɪntɪmət ˈætməsfɪə(r)/.
Potential inconvenience	潜在的不便	/pəˈtenʃl ˌɪnkənˈviːniəns/.
Heartwarming experience	暖心的经历	/ˈhɑːtwɔːmɪŋ ɪkˈspɪəriəns/.
Immediate family	直系亲属	/ɪˈmiːdiət ˈfæməli/.
Cozy apartment	舒适的公寓	/ˈkəʊzi əˈpɑːtmənt/.

## 43. 自然之地/想去的多树之地/想了解更多的野生动物/迷路/想再去的旅行/第一次用外语/远行/旅途中的有趣建筑/美丽天空/等待特别事情/想再去一次的城市/决意等待/计划多人活动/户外活动之地 / 事物
1. [Part 4] 同学可以结合题库的具体问题，练习素材。
1. 为了更好的匹配每一道题，素材本身的字数会超过真实的考试同学们能表达字数。
2. 针对不同的问法，同学的开头和结尾需要进行调整。
3. 一定要注意表达的自然程度～必要时增加重音，表情和手势
   - Answer: 我去英国徒步旅行 (6.5~7)
   - Summary: 我想描述一次几年前与朋友计划的难忘徒步旅行。那是在我大学最后一年的秋天，我们去了位于英国贝克韦尔古镇附近的峰区国家公园。
   - Content: I'm going to describe a memorable hiking trip I planned with a friend a couple of years ago. It took place during the autumn of my final year at university. We went to the Peak District National Park, which is situated near the quaint town of Bakewell in the UK.

I went there with my best friend Tom. We embarked on this adventure by meticulously planning a route through the stunning countryside. The natural environment was breathtaking; rolling hills were covered in purple heather, and deep valleys were carved by ancient rivers. The ecosystem was thriving – we spotted adorable mountain hares and a variety of birds of prey soaring overhead, many of which I couldn't identify and desperately wished for a guide.

The situation unfolded when I became so engrossed in exploring the unmarked paths and beautiful local flora that I inadvertently strayed from the main trail and got completely lost. I felt a wave of panic. Fortunately, I soon encountered a group of local hikers. I mustered up the courage to explain my predicament and asked if I could tag along with them. After a brief chat, their leader kindly agreed.

I remember our journey continued, we came across the ruins of an ancient manor house. It looked both majestic and eerie, sending a shiver down my spine. While some of us felt a tad frightened, there was a collective curiosity to explore it. However, the leader, exercising caution, insisted that our immediate priority was to get back before dusk. He suggested we could plan a proper return visit, which I readily agreed to.

True to his word, three days later on a clear and sunny afternoon, we reconvened to explore the ruins. I felt a mix of trepidation and excitement. The place was indeed slightly spooky, but it had a perfect rooftop terrace for watching the sunset. We waited until past six o'clock and were rewarded with the most magnificent sunset I've ever seen. The sky was ablaze with hues of orange, pink, and gold, casting a warm glow over the entire valley. It was an absolutely unforgettable experience that I've longed to repeat ever since.

词汇与搭配总结.
Memorable hiking trip	难忘的徒步旅行	/ˈmem(ə) rəbl ˈhaɪkɪŋ trɪp/.

Inadvertently strayed	不经意间迷路	/ˌɪnədˈvɜːt(ə) ntli streɪd/.

Sky was ablaze with	天空被...映红	/skaɪ wɒz əˈbleɪz wɪð/.
Casting a warm glow	投射出温暖的光芒	/ˈkɑːstɪŋ ə wɔːm ɡləʊ/.

## 44. 健康文章/童年的玩具/弄坏东西/别人帮忙下做的决定水上运动/教别人的技能/近期日常改变/第一次尝试的兴奋活动/想提升的天赋/想看的体育赛事/钦佩的运动员/激励你做有趣事情的人/天空/发小 / 事件
1. [Part 4] 同学可以结合题库的具体问题，练习素材。

   - Answer: 游泳 (6.5~7)
   - Summary: 我想谈谈游泳这项让我又爱又恨的运动。小时候我就对游泳产生了浓厚的兴趣，父母还给我买了个明黄色的充气游泳圈。

转机出现在大学时期。我的一位痴迷游泳的好友不断鼓励我重新尝试。在我20岁生日那天，他送了本名为《全浸式游泳》的书籍，里面深入探讨了游泳技巧。

他还带我去观看全国游泳锦标赛。我尤其被孙杨这位运动员所折服，他在泳池中的卓越表现与赛后采访时的谦逊态度相得益彰。他的坚韧精神深深激励了我
   - Content: I'd like to talk about swimming, a sport I've had a love-hate relationship with. When I was a child, I developed a strong fondness for it. My parents even bought me a bright yellow inflatable rubber ring, which was my favourite toy. Tragically, I accidentally punctured it one day, and I was utterly heartbroken. That incident made me give up on swimming entirely for years.

The turning point came when I was in university. A close friend of mine, who is an avid swimmer, he persistently encouraged me to give it another shot. On my 20th birthday, he gave me a book called "Total Immersion," which delves into swimming techniques. It explained fascinating concepts like reducing drag by improving body position and maximizing propulsion through efficient arm pulls. Reading it rekindled my childhood passion.

He also took me to watch national swimming competitions. I was particularly impressed by an athlete named Sun Yang. His exceptional performance in the pool was matched only by his humility during post-race interviews. His perseverance deeply inspired me. I felt motivated to emulate his dedication. I started going to the local pool regularly, swapping my sedentary habits for a healthier lifestyle. I soon experienced significant health benefits, such as enhanced cardiovascular fitness and improved muscle tone across my entire body. The sense of achievement after completing my first proper lap was incredible; I felt an overwhelming pride and joy. That initial success fueled my determination to keep improving.
我想谈谈游泳这项让我又爱又恨的运动。小时候我就对游泳产生了浓厚的兴趣，父母还给我买了个明黄色的充气游泳圈。.

他还带我去观看全国游泳锦标赛。我尤其被孙杨这位运动员所折服，他在泳池中的卓越表现与赛后采访时的谦逊态度相得益彰。他的坚韧精神深深激励了我.

   - Summary: 我喜欢 Lady gaga, 她不但有完美的歌声和超强的创造力，而且在服装搭配上非常独树一帜，她的风格总是能和她的风格，音乐有机地结合在一起，我非常希望能见到她

I first discovered Gaga in 2009 when her hit song "Poker Face" (成名曲《Poker Face》) was everywhere. Her powerful voice immediately caught my attention. But what really amazed me was her bold fashion style (大胆的时尚风格) - who could forget her iconic meat dress (经典的"肉片装") or the 10-inch heels she wore to awards shows?

Gaga's music style is mainly pop (流行风格), but she mixes in electronic, dance and even jazz elements (电子、舞曲和爵士元素). Her songs like "Bad Romance" and "Born This Way" have unforgettable melodies (难忘的旋律) and meaningful lyrics (有意义的歌词).

What I admire most is her dedication to art (对艺术的奉献). She once said: "I don't care if people think I'm weird." This confidence inspires me to be myself. Though I'll probably never meet her, I'll always be a little monster (她的粉丝昵称) at heart.

## 46. 难用的科技产品/见过产品的广告/商店/二手物品网站/信息搜索/ / 事件

Describe a piece of technology you own that you feel is different to use
Describe an advertisement which introduced a product you have seen.
Describe a shop/store you enjoy visiting.
Describe a website that sells second - hand items.
Describe a time when you needed to search for information
   - Answer: 想买一个跑步机 (6~6.5)
   - Summary: 我想买一个跑步机来减肥，因为有天看到了一个广告，非常吸引我，而且我有在健身房体验过这个跑步机，所以想买一个，但是预算有限，所以上网各种搜索找到了一家靠谱的二手网站，但是买了之后发现它非常占用空间，而且我也很难坚持使用，最后还是闲置了
Sleek – 时尚的
Effortless – 毫不费力的
Budget – 预算
Niche – 小众的
Haggling – 讨价还价
Reality hit hard – 现实很残酷
Overpriced – 价格过高的
Guarantee – 保证
   - Content: Last winter, I became obsessed with buying a treadmill after seeing an advertisement that promised "effortless weight loss at home." The ad showed a sleek, high-tech machine with a built-in TV screen—it looked perfect! I even tried a similar model at my gym and loved how smooth it felt.

But with a limited budget, I needed to find a cheaper option. So I spent weeks searching online for second-hand treadmills. I checked e-commerce platforms (电商平台) like Taobao first, but most were too expensive. Then I dug deeper into niche second-hand websites (小众二手网站) and fitness forums, comparing prices, reading user reviews, and even messaging sellers to ask about the treadmill’s condition.

Finally, I found a "barely used" model on a local second-hand app. The seller claimed it was only used a few times—which seemed believable because the photos looked clean. After some price haggling (讨价还价), I bought it.

But reality hit hard: the treadmill was HUGE, turning my living room into a gym. Worse, I barely used it after the first month—turns out, running at home is way more boring than at the gym! Now it’s just an overpriced clothes rack (昂贵的晾衣架).

This experience taught me that thorough research (充分调研) doesn’t guarantee a good decision—sometimes, you don’t know what you really need until it’s too late.

## 47. 想参观的不寻常建筑/看见动物的地方 / 地点
1. [Part 4] 同学可以结合题库的具体问题，练习素材。
1. 为了更好的匹配每一道题，素材本身的字数会超过真实的考试同学们能表达字数。
2. 针对不同的问法，同学的开头和结尾需要进行调整。
3. 一定要注意表达的自然程度～必要时增加重音，表情和手势
   - Answer: 想参观的不寻常建筑/看见动物的地方 (6.5~7)
   - Summary: 一个很吵闹的，建筑很不寻常的动物展示区域，它类似一个沙漠里的帐篷，人们可以看到各种各样的爬行动物。
Reptile exhibition - 爬行动物展
Hissing sound effects - 嘶嘶音效
Unconventional design - 非常规设计
Shed snakeskin - 蛇蜕皮
Deafening screams - 震耳欲聋的尖叫
Rattling walkways - 嘎吱作响的步道
Amplified sounds - 被放大的声响
   - Content: One of the noisiest places I’ve ever visited was a reptile exhibition(爬行动物展) in a huge tent-like structure(帐篷式建筑) that looked like something out of a desert adventure movie. The whole place had a wild, unconventional design(不寻常的设计)—colorful fabrics stretched over metal frames, with rattling(嘎嘎作响的) wooden walkways and hissing(嘶嘶声的) sound effects playing through hidden speakers to make it feel like a real oasis(绿洲) full of exotic creatures.

I went there last summer with my nephew, who’s crazy about snakes and lizards. Inside, the noise was overwhelming(让人受不了的)—kids shrieking every time a python moved, parents yelling warnings like "Don’t tap the glass!", and staff members shouting fun facts over the crowd. At one point, a mischievous(调皮的) macaw parrot (which somehow lived there too) started squawking(尖声大叫) "Hello! Hello!" nonstop, making everyone laugh but adding to the chaos.

What made it even noisier was the interactive area(互动区), where children could hold small turtles or touch a shed snakeskin(蛇蜕的皮). The excitement—and terrified screams—were deafening(震耳欲聋的). At first, I just wanted to escape, but then I noticed how much joy the noise represented. The strange tent amplified(放大) every sound, turning it into a vibrant(热闹的), unforgettable experience. By the end, even I was laughing and shouting over the din to ask the keeper questions about venomous(有毒的) frogs.

## 48. 想退的货/智力游戏 / 人物
1. [Part 4] Describe something you bought that you really
wanted to return

When and where you bought itWhy you wanted to return it
And explain whether you returned it in the end；
Describe a(jigsaw, crossword, etc)puzzle you have played
You should say:
What it is like
How easy or difficult it is
How long it takes you to solve
And how you feel about it
   - Answer: 魔方 (6~6.5)
   - Summary: 我想谈谈我对魔方的终生迷恋——这段旅程既激动人心又令人沮丧，教会了我耐心和信任可靠卖家的重要性。
   - Content: I’d like to talk about my lifelong fascination with Rubik’s Cubes—a journey that’s been equal parts thrilling and frustrating, teaching me patience and the importance of trusting reliable sellers.

My obsession began at age 10 when I received a classic 3x3 cube as a birthday gift. Initially, I couldn’t solve even one side without peeling off the stickers (yes, I cheated)!. Then I stumbled upon a YouTube tutorial by a speedcuber who broke down algorithms like “F2L” and “OLL.” For weeks, I carried that cube everywhere—during meals, on school buses—muttering acronyms like “R U R’ U’” like magical incantations. The day I finally aligned all six colors remains etched in my memory; I ran around the house screaming, convinced I’d cracked the Da Vinci Code of toys.

Fast-forward to last month. Browsing an online marketplace late at night, I spotted a “professional-grade magnetic speed cube” with glowing reviews and rainbow-lit promotional photos. Seduced by claims of “buttery smooth rotation” and “world championship-approved design,” I clicked “buy” instantly.

When it arrived, reality bit hard. The plastic felt cheap and squeaky, lightyears from the promised silkiness. The stickers—advertised as “smudge-proof”—started peeling within minutes. Worst of all, the magnets meant to stabilize turns were so weak, the cube practically disintegrated during my first attempt at a T-perm algorithm. I felt cheated, like ordering a gourmet steak and getting a shoe sole.

After filming unboxing evidence, I confronted the seller. Their response was classic dodgy vendor: “Maybe you used too much force?” and “All cubes have slight flaws.” I shot back with screenshots of their misleading ads and threatened a platform dispute. They finally caved, offering a refund if I paid return shipping—a partial victory.

This experience taught me two things: First, childhood passions evolve but never fade—I’ve since bought a genuine Moyu cube from a certified store, and its flawless clicks bring back that original joy. Second, online shopping is a minefield where sparkly photos often hide plastic disappointments. Now, I check serial numbers like a detective and read reviews with Sherlock-level skepticism.

Maybe next time, I’ll just stick to solving puzzles rather than navigating return policies!

## 49. 最喜欢的运动/仰慕的运动员或体育队 / 人物

And explain why you admire the athlete/sports team；

You should say:
What it is
How often you do it
How you learned to do it
And explain why you like it
   - Answer: 乒乓球 (6~6.5)
   - Summary: 我想谈谈中国乒乓球运动员徐昕，他彻底改变了我对体育的看法——不仅仅是一项比赛，而是一种艺术形式。他的创造力和天赋使像我这样的普通观众变成了一个狂热的乒乓球爱好者。
   - Content: I’d like to talk about Xu Xin, the Chinese table tennis player who completely changed my perspective on sports—not just as a competition, but as an art form. His creativity and flair turned a casual viewer like me into an avid ping-pong enthusiast.

I first noticed Xu during the Tokyo Olympics mixed doubles final. While others played textbook strokes, he stood out with his unorthodox techniques—like executing a "phantom spin" serve that left opponents frozen, or pulling off improvisational shots mid-air that defied physics. Commentators called him "The Showman", and rightfully so. One rally, in particular, hooked me: he lobbed the ball diagonally across the table, then spun 180 degrees to smash it backward without even looking. The crowd erupted, and I thought, "This isn’t just sport; it’s poetry in motion!".

Inspired, I signed up for weekly ping-pong classes. My first session was humbling—I couldn’t even grip the paddle properly! My coach laughed, saying, "Trying to imitate Xu Xin? Start by keeping the ball on the table first!" For months, I drilled footwork and basic spins until my legs ached. But what kept me going was recreating Xu’s signature moves during practice. My "reverse pendulum serve" initially flew into walls, but gradually, muscle memory kicked in.

The real joy, though, comes from weekend matches with friends. We’ve turned our garage into a makeshift arena, complete with LED lights and a chalkboard scorekeeper. Last month, mimicking Xu’s famous "behind-the-back" shot, I accidentally smashed a lamp—but we laughed so hard we postponed the game. Through these chaotic rallies, I’ve bonded with friends who now share my admiration for Xu’s genius.

Xu Xin taught me that mastery isn’t just about precision—it’s about personality. Every missed shot now feels like a step toward unlocking my own style. Who knows? Maybe one day I’ll nail that no-look smash... or at least stop breaking lamps.

   - Answer: 披萨 (6.5~7)
   - Summary: 我想谈谈我对披萨的终生热爱——这道菜对我来说不仅仅是食物，而是连接童年记忆、友谊和美食冒险的线索。
Wood-fired - 柴火烤制的
Gooey mozzarella - 拉丝马苏里拉
Culinary school - 烹饪学校

Caramelized onions - 焦糖洋葱
Edible language - 可食用的语言
Lopsided dough - 不规则面团
Brick oven - 砖砌烤炉
   - Content: I’d like to talk about my lifelong love for pizza—a dish that’s not just food to me, but a thread connecting childhood memories, friendship, and culinary adventures.

My obsession began when I was eight. My parents, wanting to broaden my picky eating habits, took me to an Italian restaurant downtown. The moment the wood-fired Margherita pizza arrived—its crispy crust, gooey mozzarella, and basil aroma—I was hooked. From then on, Friday nights became “pizza nights” in our family, rotating between pepperoni feasts and Hawaiian controversies (yes, I’m team pineapple)!.

But the real twist came through my friend Lisa. Last summer, during a pizza-themed movie night at my place, she casually mentioned enrolling in a week-long pizza-making course at a culinary school. “I’m tired of just eating it,” she declared. “I want to create magic!”.

Curious, I visited her final class. The workshop was chaos incarnate—flour-dusted counters, students frantically stretching dough, and a fiery brick oven roaring in the corner. Lisa, usually meticulous, embraced the mess. She explained how temperature affects yeast activity while kneading dough, and why San Marzano tomatoes are considered the “gold standard” for sauce.

The highlight came when she pulled her creation from the oven: a rustic pizza topped with roasted garlic, caramelized onions, and local honey. One bite transported me—the sweetness balancing the savory, the crust crackling like autumn leaves. “This beats any chain restaurant,” I mumbled through a full mouth.

What makes this special isn’t just the taste. Through Lisa’s journey, I’ve gained respect for pizza as both art and science. We’ve since hosted DIY pizza nights, laughing over lopsided dough shapes and accidental ingredient combos (kimchi and chocolate? Not recommended). It’s become our edible language of friendship.

Now, whenever I bite into a pizza slice, I taste layers beyond cheese and sauce—the warmth of family traditions, the joy of shared experiments, and proof that passion, when baked at 450°F, creates something unforgettable.

## 51. 环保人士 /想去的多树之地 / 人物
1. [Part 4] Describe a person who helps to protect the environment
You should say:
Who this person is
When this person does this
What has the person done
And explain why you think this person does this；
Describe a place with a lot of trees that you would like to visit(e.g. a forest, oasis)
You should say:
Where it is
How you knew this place
What it is like
And explain why you would like to visit it
   - Answer: 护林员 (6~6.5)
   - Summary: 我想谈谈我的叔叔，他是一名护林员，他对环境保护的奉献精神深深地激励了我。他的故事不仅仅是一份工作，而是对治愈我们称之为家的土地的毕生承诺。
   - Content: I’d like to talk about my uncle, a forest ranger whose dedication to environmental protection has deeply inspired me. His story isn’t just about a job—it’s a lifelong commitment to healing the land we call home.

My uncle has worked as a guardian of the mountains in my hometown for over 20 years. Every dawn, rain or shine, he hikes through dense forests to inspect trails, monitor wildlife, and clear invasive plants. His routine might sound repetitive, but as I learned during my recent summer visit, it’s anything but ordinary.

I joined him on his patrol one morning at his mountain cabin. Wearing his faded green uniform and carrying a weathered backpack, he pointed out subtle signs of ecological recovery: a family of pheasants nesting in shrubs that were once trampled by illegal loggers, crystal streams revived after his team removed plastic waste dams. “Twenty years ago,” he said, “this slope was bald from wildfires. Now look—the oaks are taller than me!” His pride was palpable.

What amazed me most was his innovative approach. Instead of just enforcing rules, he collaborates with villagers. He convinced farmers to replace chemical pesticides with natural solutions, turning former poachers into volunteer forest monitors. Thanks to these efforts, the mountain has become a biodiversity hotspot, with rare species like leopard cats reappearing after decades.

This trip reshaped my perspective. As a child, I saw my uncle’s job as lonely and tough. Now, I realize it’s a quiet revolution. Seeing villagers greet him with homemade snacks during our patrol—their way of thanking him—made me tear up. The mountain isn’t just greener; the community’s mindset has blossomed too.

Leaving his cabin, I took one last glance at the misty peaks. They stood as a testament to what one person’s perseverance can achieve. My uncle may never trend on social media, but in every birdsong and rustling leaf here, his legacy lives on.

## 52. 陌生人的电话/想修改的新法律 / 事物
1. [Part 4] Describe a time when you answered a phone call from someone you didn't know in a public place
You should say:
Where it happened
What he/she said
How you corresponded
And explain how you felt about the experience；
Describe a newly enacted law that you like but you want to change part of it
You should say:
When it was enacted
What the law is about
Which part you want to change
And explain why you want to change the part
   - Answer: 广告电话 (6~6.5)
   - Summary: 我想谈谈我上个月的一个令人沮丧的经历，一个意想不到的电话——那一刻让我质疑我们的个人信息到底有多安全。
   - Content: I’d like to talk about a frustrating experience I had last month involving an unexpected phone call—a moment that made me question how secure our personal information really is.

It happened on a rainy Thursday evening while I was walking home from the subway station. My phone buzzed, and I saw an unknown number with a local area code. Assuming it might be a delivery update, I answered. A robotic voice immediately said, “Hello! Are you interested in a low-interest loan?” Confused, I replied, “Sorry, I didn’t apply for any loan.” The caller persisted, listing rates and approval guarantees. I interrupted firmly, “Please remove my number from your list,” and hung up.

What bothered me wasn’t just the interruption—it was the implication that my data had been leaked. I’ve never shared my number with financial institutions, but I’d recently signed up for an e-commerce site that required my contact details. This made me suspect irresponsible data handling by third-party platforms.

The incident left me feeling both annoyed and vulnerable. While spam calls are common, this one crossed a line by pushing inappropriate financial products. It’s unsettling to realize how easily our privacy can be compromised for profit.

Ironically, just days earlier, I’d read an article about weak penalties for data breaches in our current privacy laws. This call cemented my belief that reforms are urgent. For instance, regulations could mimic the EU’s GDPR, requiring companies to obtain explicit consent before sharing user data and imposing heavy fines for violations.

Though I reported the number to my carrier, nothing changed—I still get similar calls weekly. It’s a stark reminder that individual vigilance isn’t enough; systemic legal safeguards are crucial. This experience has made me hyper-aware of permissions I grant apps and more supportive of digital privacy campaigns. After all, in an era where data is gold, our phone numbers shouldn’t be sold like cheap souvenirs.

My town’s performance center was hosting a New Year’s concert by our local symphony orchestra, and my mother, who loves classical music, had booked tickets weeks in advance. The venue was grand, with velvet seats and golden lighting enhancing the festive atmosphere.

The performance began with Vivaldi’s Four Seasons and included pieces by Tchaikovsky. I was amazed at how the music conveyed stories without words—the violins mirrored laughter and tears while the cellos provided a deep rhythm. Though not a huge fan of classical music before, that night captivated me completely. My mother sat beside me, sharing insights about the composers with sparkling eyes.

The highlight came during the encore when the orchestra surprised us with an energetic medley of folk tunes mixed with New Year’s melodies. The conductor encouraged audience participation through clapping, transforming the formal hall into a lively celebration. When it ended, applause erupted—some even stood up cheering.

What made this experience special wasn’t just the music but how it brought my mother and me closer together. Between performances, we shared stories about her childhood music lessons and my choir struggles. It struck me how rare it was for us to have such uninterrupted time together without screens. By evening's end, I felt awe for the artists’ talent and gratitude for our bonding moment.

Returning home that night left me feeling refreshed; my usual academic stress gave way to calmness.

It’s an ancient Chinese building and is known as one of the “Four Famous Buildings of Ancient China.” The tower is mainly made of wood and has a rich history—it was once used for political and military purposes in ancient times, but today it’s a popular tourist attraction.

I find this building particularly interesting because of my uncle, who is an architect. He’s a relative I’ve known since childhood, and he’s always been someone I admire. He’s not only knowledgeable but also very approachable, and he loves sharing his passion for architecture with me. When we visited the Yellow Crane Tower together, he told me so many fascinating stories about its history. For example, he explained how the tower was destroyed and rebuilt several times over the centuries due to wars and natural disasters. He also pointed out the unique architectural features, like the intricate woodwork and the symbolic designs that reflect ancient Chinese culture.

What makes this building special to me isn’t just its historical significance or architectural beauty—it’s also the memories I associate with it. My uncle’s willingness to openly share his knowledge made the visit so much more meaningful. His stories helped me appreciate the tower not just as a structure but as a symbol of resilience and cultural heritage.

Overall, the Yellow Crane Tower is a building I deeply admire, and my uncle’s passion for architecture has made it even more memorable for me.

   - Answer: 朝天宫 (6~6.5)
   - Summary: 我参观了南京的朝天宫。它现在实际上是一个博物馆，但它曾经是一个传统的中国古典建筑。当我和我的同学去那里的时候，那是一次很酷的经历。我们都在学校学习南京的历史，去朝天宫就像一个实践课。我们能够看到所有这些展示这座城市历史的文物和展品。
   - Content: Well, I had the pleasure of visiting an old building called the Chaotian Palace in Nanjing. It has been transformed into a museum now, but it used to represent traditional Chinese classical architecture back in its heyday. Stepping inside truly feels like taking a journey into the past, doesn’t it?

When I visited with my classmates, it was such an enriching experience. We were all studying Nanjing's history at school, and going to the Chaotian Palace felt like an engaging hands-on lesson. We had the opportunity to explore numerous artifacts and exhibits that beautifully showcased the city’s rich history.

I recall how excited everyone was; we couldn’t stop chatting and sharing our insights with one another. It felt like a large study session infused with fun! We gained so much knowledge about the city's past and how it has evolved over time.

In my opinion, this is an excellent place for learning. Rather than being confined to a classroom setting, field trips allow us to learn in such vivid ways. The Chaotian Palace makes me feel connected to historical events from ancient times; it's heartwarming to realize how closely our lives are intertwined with those of our ancestors from thousands of years ago—this connection brings me great joy in my studies.

I genuinely believe that visiting Chaotian Palace is wonderful if you wish to deepen your understanding of Nanjing. It's far from just another dull museum; rather, it's a vibrant space where history comes alive, allowing you to fully immerse yourself in the culture and heritage of this remarkable city.

## 65. 【疑似淘汰】喜欢买便宜货的人\ 音乐爱好者 / 人物

   - Answer: 朋友 (6~6.5)

   - Content: I have a friend who is a true music enthusiast. He loves to buy discounted CDs, headphones, and other music-related products. We often visit a small store together that specializes in selling these items. This store used to be located in an older part of the city, but with the recent urban development, a new shopping mall was built, and the store relocated there. The new location is much more convenient and has allowed the store to expand its range of products.

My friend and I usually go to this store on weekends. The store is now situated on the second floor of the shopping mall, which is only a short bus ride from where we live. The shop is cozy and well-organized, with a wide variety of music products displayed neatly on the shelves. The staff are friendly and knowledgeable, often recommending new releases or the best deals available.(工作人员很友好，知识渊博，经常推荐新发行的电影或最好的优惠。).

(他对折扣有敏锐的眼光，总是能在高质量的音乐产品上找到很好的交易。) He believes that music is an essential part of life and enjoys exploring different genres and artists. His passion for music and his ability to find affordable products have made our shopping trips both fun and rewarding.

The new shopping mall has significantly improved our local area. It took about a year to complete, and its opening has brought more convenience and variety to our shopping experiences. The mall is modern and spacious, with numerous stores, restaurants, and entertainment options. This development has made our neighborhood more vibrant and lively.

Overall, I feel very positive about these changes. The relocation of our favorite music store to the new shopping mall has been a great improvement. We still enjoy our visits, and the expanded range of products means we always find something new and exciting. The development has not only enhanced our shopping experiences but also contributed to a more dynamic and enjoyable community.

## 69. 【疑似淘汰】想换掉的东西/少年的榜样 / 事件

What it is
Where it is
How you got it
And explain why you want to replace it；
Describe someone (a famous person) that is a role model for young people
You should say:
Who he/she is
How you knew him/her
What he/she has done
And explain why he/she can be a role model for young people
   - Answer: 海伦·凯勒 (6~6.5)
   - Summary: 我想换掉的一本书是海伦·凯勒的《我的人生故事》。海伦·凯勒是年轻人的优秀榜样。她是一位美国作家和活动家，尽管又聋又盲，但她为社会做出了卓越的贡献。我想替换这本书的原因不是因为它的状况很差，而是因为我相信更多的人应该有机会了解海伦·凯勒。
   - Content: One item I own that I would like to replace is a book titled "The Story of My Life" by Helen Keller. This book is currently sitting on my bookshelf in my living room. I acquired it a few years ago from a local bookstore because I was fascinated by Helen Keller's life story and her achievements despite her disabilities.

The reason I want to replace this book is not because it's in poor condition, but because I believe that more people should have the opportunity to learn about Helen Keller. I would like to exchange it for a newer edition or a different format to share her inspiring story with a broader audience. Helen Keller's life is a powerful testament to overcoming obstacles and achieving greatness against all odds, and I think it would be beneficial to have more accessible copies of her story available.

Helen Keller is an excellent role model for young people. She was an American author and activist who, despite being both deaf and blind, made remarkable contributions to society. Her achievements include advocating for people with disabilities and co-founding the American Civil Liberties Union (ACLU). Keller's life demonstrates that perseverance, determination, and a positive attitude can lead to extraordinary accomplishments. Her story encourages young people to overcome their own challenges and strive for their goals, making her an inspiring figure for anyone facing difficulties.

Anyway, I managed to replace the book and hope that more people will learn about Helen Keller's story and learn from her spirit.

## 71. 【疑似淘汰】宜居之城\描述一种植物 / 地点
1. [Part 4] Describe a place (city/town) that is good for people to live in
You should say:
Where it is
How you knew this place
What it is like
And explain why it is better than other places to live in;
Describe an important plant in your country
You should say:
What it is 
Where you see it
What it looks like
Why it is important
   - Answer: 广州 (6~6.5)
   - Summary: 广州是一个繁华的大都市，现代与传统完美融合。它拥有良好的基础设施。木棉则是广州和中国南方大部分地区的一种重要植物。
   - Content: One place that I believe is great for people to live in is Guangzhou, a major city in southern China. I first learned about Guangzhou through friends and family who either live there or have visited. Over time, I had the chance to visit the city myself and was deeply impressed by its vibrant lifestyle, rich culture, and pleasant living environment.

Guangzhou is a bustling metropolis with a perfect mix of modernity and tradition. It has excellent infrastructure, including well-developed public transportation, modern shopping malls, and a wide variety of restaurants offering both local and international cuisine. The city also offers many green spaces, such as parks and riverside areas, where residents can relax. The pleasant climate and subtropical weather make it an enjoyable place to live throughout the year. Compared to other cities, I think Guangzhou offers a balanced lifestyle, combining urban convenience with a laid-back vibe.

An important plant in Guangzhou, and in much of southern China, is the kapok tree. The kapok tree is the city flower of Guangzhou and is often seen lining the streets, especially in parks and gardens. It has tall, sturdy trunks and produces large, vibrant red flowers that bloom in spring. The sight of kapok flowers in full bloom is truly stunning and gives the city a unique charm.

The kapok tree holds cultural significance as well. In traditional Chinese medicine, its fibers and seeds are used for various health treatments. It symbolizes resilience and strength, making it an important symbol for the city and its people.

What difficulty you had

And explain why you felt proud of it
   - Answer: 灵隐寺 (6~6.5)
   - Summary: 我和安娜曾经一起参加过一个比赛，在这个比赛中每个队伍要历史建筑为主题创作绘画作品。为此，我们参观了杭州的灵隐寺，并讨论的创作方案。经过多次修改，我们打磨出了满意的作品，并获得了奖项，我对此感到骄傲。
   - Content: Anna is someone I aspire to work with because of her intelligence and diligence. We first met during a painting competition where each team had to create artworks themed around historical buildings. For this competition, we visited Lingyin Temple in Hangzhou to gather inspiration and discuss our creative approach.

Lingyin Temple is a renowned historical building located amidst lush greenery and serene surroundings. Its architecture reflects traditional Chinese Buddhist design, with intricate carvings, colorful decorations, and towering pagodas. (它的建筑反映了中国传统的佛教设计，有复杂的雕刻，丰富多彩的装饰和高耸的宝塔。) As we explored the temple grounds, we were fascinated by its rich history and cultural significance.

During our visit, Anna and I spent hours brainstorming ideas and refining our painting concept. We faced challenges in translating the grandeur of Lingyin Temple onto canvas while staying true to its essence. Despite the difficulties, we collaborated closely, sharing ideas and supporting each other's artistic vision.(尽管困难重重，我们还是紧密合作，分享想法，支持彼此的艺术愿景。).

After numerous revisions and adjustments, we finally completed our painting, capturing the timeless beauty and spiritual aura of Lingyin Temple. Our hard work and dedication paid off when our artwork received recognition and won an award in the competition.

Reflecting on this experience fills me with pride. Not only did we create a meaningful piece of art together, but we also formed a strong bond based on mutual respect and creative synergy. (我们不仅一起创造了一件有意义的艺术品，而且还在相互尊重和创造性协同的基础上形成了牢固的纽带。) Working with Anna taught me the importance of teamwork, perseverance, and collaboration in achieving shared goals. It was a proud moment to see our efforts acknowledged and rewarded, reaffirming my belief in the power of collaboration and dedication.

What made this experience even more memorable was the opportunity to interact with the local farmers and learn about their way of life. We gained insight into the challenges and joys of rural living, fostering a deeper appreciation for the simplicity and authenticity of countryside living.

I found this countryside farmstay fascinating for its tranquility, natural beauty, and the chance to engage in hands-on activities. It was a refreshing escape from the hustle and bustle of city life, offering a glimpse into a slower-paced, more sustainable way of living. (这是一种逃离喧嚣的城市生活的清新方式，让人瞥见了一种节奏较慢、更可持续的生活方式。) Our culinary adventure, coupled with the scenic surroundings and warm hospitality, made it a truly memorable and enriching experience.

Overall, the experience of teaching my cousin and receiving money as a token of appreciation was both fulfilling and heartwarming. It reinforced the importance of sharing knowledge and supporting each other within the family. Additionally, it served as a reminder of the value of hard work and dedication in helping others achieve their goals.

## 76. 【疑似淘汰】嘈杂地\新法律 / 地点
1. [Part 4] Describe a noisy place you have been to
You should say:
What it is
When you went there
What you did there
And explain why you feel it's a noisy place；
Describe a new law you would like to introduce 
You should say
What law it is
What changes this law has
Whether this new law will be popular
How you came up with the new law
And explain how you feel about this new law
   - Answer: 工厂污染 (6~6.5)
   - Summary: 我家附近的工厂经常产生噪音与空气污染，我向政府投诉这个问题。后来颁布了《工厂污染管理法》，工厂的污染问题得到了控制。我对于这个结果很满意。
   - Content: I live near a factory that used to emit excessive noise and air pollution, which greatly affected the surrounding area. Fed up with the situation, I decided to lodge a complaint with the local government. The authorities responded by implementing the "Factory Pollution Management Law," (《工厂污染管理法》) which aimed to regulate and control the pollution emitted by factories.

This law required factories to adhere to strict emissions standards and implement measures to mitigate their environmental impact.(这项法律要求工厂遵守严格的排放标准，并采取措施减轻对环境的影响。) It also mandated regular inspections and imposed penalties for non-compliance. The implementation of this law brought about significant improvements in air quality and noise levels in my neighborhood.

I felt satisfied with the result of my complaint because it addressed the problem effectively and brought tangible improvements to the quality of life in the area. The once polluted air became cleaner, and the incessant noise from the factory diminished significantly. The new law not only improved the environment but also ensured the health and well-being of the community.(新法律不仅改善了环境，而且确保了社区的健康和福祉。).

The satisfaction I felt stemmed from the realization that my complaint had made a positive difference. It demonstrated the power of citizen action and government intervention in addressing environmental issues. Knowing that my efforts had contributed to creating a healthier and more pleasant living environment for myself and my neighbors was immensely gratifying.

In conclusion, the introduction of the "Factory Pollution Management Law" was a positive outcome of my complaint. It effectively addressed the pollution problem caused by the nearby factory and brought about significant improvements in air quality and noise levels. This experience has reinforced my belief in the importance of advocating for environmental protection and holding polluters accountable for their actions.

   - Answer: 朋友 (6~6.5)

The mall is modern and spacious, with numerous stores, restaurants, and entertainment options. This development has made our neighborhood more vibrant and lively.

Overall, I feel very positive about these changes. The relocation of our favorite music store to the new shopping mall has been a great improvement. The development has not only enhanced our shopping experiences but also contributed to a more dynamic and enjoyable community.

The natural park remains a special place for me, not only because of its beauty but also because of the memories and experiences it holds. Revisiting those moments through photos brings a sense of nostalgia and happiness, making the park a cherished part of my past.

(他的指导是无价的，他对我能力的信任增强了我的信心。) Despite the challenges of managing my schoolwork and preparing for the competition, his support made it possible for me to persevere.

This achievement was particularly important to me because it demonstrated that I could excel in public speaking without compromising my academic responsibilities.(这一成就对我来说尤其重要，因为它证明了我可以在不牺牲学术责任的情况下，在公开演讲方面表现出色。).

My grandfather’s encouragement and assistance were pivotal in my success. This experience has had a lasting impact on me, and I am deeply grateful for his guidance.

In summary, my bedroom is my favorite place in the house. It serves as a perfect retreat for both relaxation and study, making it an essential part of my daily routine.

## 81. 【疑似淘汰】迟到\冒风险 / 事物
1. [Part 4] Describe a time when you missed or were late for a meeting/event
You should say:
When it happened
What happened
Why you missed/were late for it
And explain how you felt about this experience；
Describe a risk you took that you thought would lead to a terrible result but ended up with a positive result
You should say:
When you took the risk
Why you took the risk
How it went
And explain how you felt about it
   - Answer: 急救 (6~6.5)
   - Summary: 高中开学第一天，我在路上看到了突发疾病的路人。冒着被老师批评的风险，我选择帮助路人叫救护车。虽然开学典礼我迟到了，但是路人获救了，我也获得了老师的理解与表扬。
   - Content: I clearly remember the first day of high school, which was a particularly memorable and eventful day for me. This happened a few years ago, at the beginning of September, when I was about 16 years old. My high school is located in the heart of the city, about a 20-minute walk from my home.

On that day, I was filled with a mixture of excitement and nervousness as I walked to school, eager to start this new chapter in my life. (那天，我怀着既兴奋又紧张的心情走向学校，渴望开启人生的新篇章。) However, on my way, I encountered an elderly man who had suddenly collapsed on the sidewalk. It was evident that he was in need of immediate medical assistance. Faced with this urgent situation, I had to make a quick decision. Despite knowing that it was the first day of school and that being late would not leave a good impression, I decided to stay and help.

I called an ambulance and stayed with the man until it arrived. This whole incident took about 20 minutes, and as a result, I missed the beginning of the opening ceremony. When I finally arrived at school, I explained the situation to my teacher, fully expecting a reprimand for my tardiness. To my surprise, the teacher and my classmates were very understanding and praised my actions. The teacher even mentioned my act of kindness during the assembly, which made me feel proud and relieved.(老师甚至在集会上提到了我的善举，这让我感到骄傲和宽慰。).

Reflecting on this experience, I realized that sometimes taking a risk and doing what you believe is right can lead to unexpectedly positive outcomes. Helping the man in need not only ensured his safety but also taught me an invaluable lesson about compassion and responsibility.(帮助有需要的人不仅确保了他的安全，也教会了我关于同情和责任的宝贵一课。) It’s an experience I still remember vividly because it marked the beginning of my high school journey with an important life lesson.

The watch had been a symbol of a memorable trip and a personal achievement. I felt a mix of frustration and sadness, and it served as a reminder of the importance of being careful with valuable items.

## 88. 重遇旧友/阅读爱好者 / 人物

   - Answer: 故宫博物院 (6~6.5)
   - Summary: 我想描述一下我参观过的一个文化场所，那就是北京的故宫博物馆。国庆节期间，我和家人一起参观了故宫。然而，由于是假日，这个地方非常拥挤。
   - Content: I'd like to describe a cultural place I visited, which is the Forbidden City Museum in Beijing. Located in the heart of Beijing, the Forbidden City is one of China’s most famous landmarks and a symbol of its imperial history. I first learned about this place in school, and I’ve always been fascinated by its historical significance and grandeur.

The Forbidden City is a massive complex with beautiful palaces, gardens, and courtyards, all surrounded by high walls. The architecture is stunning, with its red walls, golden roofs, and intricate carvings that reflect traditional Chinese culture. Once the home of Chinese emperors for nearly 500 years, it is now a museum displaying artifacts, artworks, and treasures from the Ming and Qing dynasties. This museum is deeply related to Chinese culture because it offers a rich insight into the country’s ancient traditions, art, and history.

I visited the Forbidden City during the National Day holiday with my family. We decided to go because we wanted to explore this iconic cultural site and learn more about China’s history. However, since it was a holiday, the place was extremely crowded. There were tourists everywhere, making it difficult to move around freely. At times, the crowds felt overwhelming, and it was hard to fully appreciate the surroundings due to the noise and congestion.

Despite the crowded environment, I still felt excited to be there. I admired the incredible architecture and felt a deep connection to Chinese history and culture. The experience taught me to appreciate the importance of cultural heritage, even if it means sharing it with many others.

On the other hand, at family gatherings, her insistence can be a bit excessive, since everyone has to follow her way. However, I deeply respect her and the dumplings we make together are always delicious and filled with love and care that makes them even more special.

In short, my grandmother is a person who takes food, holidays and family seriously, and I respect and love my grandmother.

There were traditional dances, calligraphy demonstrations, and even a tea ceremony. I had the opportunity to learn about the intricate rituals and customs of that time, which I found incredibly captivating.

What I enjoyed most about this party was the opportunity to engage with like-minded individuals who shared a passion for history and culture. I had the chance to interact with fellow attendees, exchange knowledge, and learn from their experiences. It was truly a valuable and enriching experience that left me with a desire to explore more about the Tang and Song dynasties.

It provided a fascinating glimpse into a historical period that I was previously unfamiliar with. The intricate details, immersive experience, and the opportunity to interact with others passionate about history made this party incredibly enjoyable and educational. I am now inspired to further explore and learn more about this intriguing era of Chinese history.

   - Content: Fuzhou, located in southeastern China, is a city I consider ideal for a short-term stay due to its livable environment and pleasant subtropical monsoon climate. I first became acquainted with Fuzhou through travel recommendations and research about cities with favorable climates.

The subtropical monsoon climate of Fuzhou is characterized by mild winters, warm summers, and abundant rainfall throughout the year. Summers are typically warm and humid, with temperatures ranging from 25 to 35 degrees Celsius, while winters are mild, with temperatures seldom dropping below 10 degrees Celsius.

What attracts me to Fuzhou's climate is its moderate temperatures and ample rainfall, which create lush vegetation and scenic landscapes. I appreciate the mild winters that allow outdoor activities comfortably and the refreshing summer showers that provide relief from the heat.( 我喜欢温和的冬天，因为它能让户外活动变得舒适，也喜欢凉爽的夏天淋浴，让人从炎热中解脱出来。).

Because of its pleasant climate and fascinating culture, I would like to spend a week or two in Fuzhou to explore its natural beauty, historical sites and food. To actually feel the tall banyan trees and the cool experience and cultural treasures they bring. I might go to Fuzhou with friends or family, eager to immerse myself in the local culture, sample the local cuisine and discover the city's hidden gems.( 沉浸在当地文化中，品尝当地美食，发现这座城市隐藏的瑰宝。).

While I find Fuzhou's climate and cultural offerings appealing, I would opt for a short-term stay to experience its highlights without committing to long-term residency. Such a visit would allow me to enjoy the best of what Fuzhou has to offer while satisfying my curiosity about this vibrant city.

   - Answer: 农家乐 (6~6.5)
   - Summary: 有次，我和朋友去了一个有趣的地方，那是一个很少人去乡下农家乐。农家乐坐落于山间，不仅有自然的景色，还可以提供采集蔬果、购买农产品的服务。我的朋友购买了一只鸡，并在那里做了一道东南亚风味的香茅烤鸡。这是美味又不寻常的一餐。
   - Content: My friend and I once ventured to an intriguing place—a rustic countryside farmstay that few people visit. Nestled amidst the mountains, this farmstay offered not only breathtaking natural scenery but also unique experiences such as fruit and vegetable picking, and purchasing farm-fresh produce.

Accompanied by my adventurous friend, we embarked on this journey to explore the charms of rural life. We visited the farm on a sunny weekend, eager to immerse ourselves in nature and try something different. Upon arrival, we were greeted by rolling hills, lush greenery, and the soothing sounds of nature.( 到达后，迎接我们的是连绵起伏的丘陵、郁郁葱葱的绿色植物和大自然舒缓的声音。).

While at the farm, my friend decided to purchase a chicken to cook for our lunch. Inspired by Southeast Asian flavors, he prepared a delicious lemongrass roasted chicken using fresh herbs and spices sourced from the farm itself.(受到东南亚风味的启发，他用农场出产的新鲜香草和香料制作了美味的香茅烤鸡。) It was a delightful meal, bursting with aromatic flavors and tender textures, unlike anything we had tasted before.

What made this experience even more memorable was the opportunity to interact with the local farmers and learn about their way of life. We gained insight into the challenges and joys of rural living, fostering a deeper appreciation for the simplicity and authenticity of countryside living.

I found this countryside farmstay fascinating for its tranquility, natural beauty, and the chance to engage in hands-on activities. It was a refreshing escape from the hustle and bustle of city life, offering a glimpse into a slower-paced, more sustainable way of living. (这是一种逃离喧嚣的城市生活的清新方式，让人瞥见了一种节奏较慢、更可持续的生活方式。) Our culinary adventure, coupled with the scenic surroundings and warm hospitality, made it a truly memorable and enriching experience.

## 102. 空气糟糕之地\ 嘈杂地\投诉并得到满意结果 \新法律 / 地点
1. [Part 4] Describe a place you visited where the air was polluted
You should say:
Where the place is
When you visited there
Why the air was not good
And explain how you felt about the place；
Describe a noisy place you have been to
You should say:
What it is
When you went there
What you did there
And explain why you feel it's a noisy place；
Describe a complaint that you were satisfied with the result. 
You should say:
Who you complained to
What you complained about
When it happened
And explain why you were satisfied with the result；
Describe a new law you would like to introduce 
You should say
What law it is
What changes this law has
Whether this new law will be popular
How you came up with the new law
And explain how you feel about this new law
   - Answer: 工厂污染 (6~6.5)
   - Summary: 我家附近的工厂经常产生噪音与空气污染，我向政府投诉这个问题。后来颁布了《工厂污染管理法》，工厂的污染问题得到了控制。我对于这个结果很满意。
   - Content: I live near a factory that used to emit excessive noise and air pollution, which greatly affected the surrounding area. Fed up with the situation, I decided to lodge a complaint with the local government. The authorities responded by implementing the "Factory Pollution Management Law," (《工厂污染管理法》) which aimed to regulate and control the pollution emitted by factories.

This law required factories to adhere to strict emissions standards and implement measures to mitigate their environmental impact.(这项法律要求工厂遵守严格的排放标准，并采取措施减轻对环境的影响。) It also mandated regular inspections and imposed penalties for non-compliance. The implementation of this law brought about significant improvements in air quality and noise levels in my neighborhood.

I felt satisfied with the result of my complaint because it addressed the problem effectively and brought tangible improvements to the quality of life in the area. The once polluted air became cleaner, and the incessant noise from the factory diminished significantly. The new law not only improved the environment but also ensured the health and well-being of the community.(新法律不仅改善了环境，而且确保了社区的健康和福祉。).

The satisfaction I felt stemmed from the realization that my complaint had made a positive difference. It demonstrated the power of citizen action and government intervention in addressing environmental issues. Knowing that my efforts had contributed to creating a healthier and more pleasant living environment for myself and my neighbors was immensely gratifying.

In conclusion, the introduction of the "Factory Pollution Management Law" was a positive outcome of my complaint. It effectively addressed the pollution problem caused by the nearby factory and brought about significant improvements in air quality and noise levels. This experience has reinforced my belief in the importance of advocating for environmental protection and holding polluters accountable for their actions.

   - Content: I have a friend who is a true music enthusiast. He loves to buy discounted CDs, headphones, and other music-related products. We often visit a small store together that specializes in selling these items. This store used to be located in an older part of the city, but with the recent urban development, a new shopping mall was built, and the store relocated there. His passion for music and his ability to find affordable products have made our shopping trips both fun and rewarding.

The new shopping mall has significantly improved our local area. It took about a year to complete, and its opening has brought more convenience and variety to our shopping experiences. The mall is modern and spacious, with numerous stores, restaurants, and entertainment options. This development has made our neighborhood more vibrant and lively.

Overall, I feel very positive about these changes. The relocation of our favorite music store to the new shopping mall has been a great improvement. We still enjoy our visits, and the expanded range of products means we always find something new and exciting. The development has not only enhanced our shopping experiences but also contributed to a more dynamic and enjoyable community.

(他的指导是无价的，他对我能力的信任增强了我的信心。) Despite the challenges of managing my schoolwork and preparing for the competition, his support made it possible for me to persevere.

When I was announced as the champion of the citywide speech competition, I felt a tremendous sense of accomplishment. This achievement was particularly important to me because it demonstrated that I could excel in public speaking without compromising my academic responsibilities.(这一成就对我来说尤其重要，因为它证明了我可以在不牺牲学术责任的情况下，在公开演讲方面表现出色。).

My grandfather’s encouragement and assistance were pivotal in my success. His unwavering support not only helped me win the competition but also taught me valuable lessons about discipline, hard work, and the importance of having a mentor. This experience has had a lasting impact on me, and I am deeply grateful for his guidance.

(我的卧室是一个舒适而安静的庇护所，装饰着柔和的色彩和舒适的家具。) There’s a large window that lets in plenty of natural light during the day, creating a calm and inviting atmosphere.

I spend a significant amount of time in my bedroom, both relaxing and studying. When it comes to studying, I have a well-organized desk where I review and prepare for my classes. This space is perfect for focusing on my studies because it is free from distractions, and the quiet environment helps me concentrate better. I usually study in the afternoons or evenings, depending on my schedule. The subjects I study here range from school assignments to additional readings and preparations for exams.

Apart from studying, my bedroom is also the place where I unwind. I enjoy listening to music, which helps me relax and recharge. Sometimes, I take short naps to refresh my mind and body. The tranquility of my bedroom makes it an ideal place for these activities.

My daily routine includes spending a few hours in my bedroom each day, either studying or relaxing. This routine is relatively easy to follow because I have everything I need within reach, and the environment is conducive to both productivity and relaxation.(这个例行程序相对容易遵循，因为我有我需要的一切触手可及，而且环境有利于生产力和放松。) I particularly enjoy this routine because it allows me to balance my academic responsibilities with moments of rest and leisure.

In summary, my bedroom is my favorite place in the house. It serves as a perfect retreat for both relaxation and study, making it an essential part of my daily routine.

## 108. 开学第一天\迟到\ 冒风险 / 事物
1. [Part 4] Describe the first day you went to school that you remember You should say:
When it happened
How you felt about the experience
Where the school is
And explain why you still remember the experience；
Describe a time when you missed or were late for a meeting/event
You should say:
When it happened
What happened
Why you missed/were late for it
And explain how you felt about this experience；
Describe a risk you took that you thought would lead to a terrible result but ended up with a positive result
You should say:
When you took the risk
Why you took the risk
How it went
And explain how you felt about it
   - Answer: 急救 (6~6.5)
   - Summary: 高中开学第一天，我在路上看到了突发疾病的路人。冒着被老师批评的风险，我选择帮助路人叫救护车。虽然开学典礼我迟到了，但是路人获救了，我也获得了老师的理解与表扬。
   - Content: I clearly remember the first day of high school, which was a particularly memorable and eventful day for me. This happened a few years ago, at the beginning of September, when I was about 16 years old. My high school is located in the heart of the city, about a 20-minute walk from my home.

On that day, I was filled with a mixture of excitement and nervousness as I walked to school, eager to start this new chapter in my life. (那天，我怀着既兴奋又紧张的心情走向学校，渴望开启人生的新篇章。) However, on my way, I encountered an elderly man who had suddenly collapsed on the sidewalk. It was evident that he was in need of immediate medical assistance. Faced with this urgent situation, I had to make a quick decision. Despite knowing that it was the first day of school and that being late would not leave a good impression, I decided to stay and help.

I called an ambulance and stayed with the man until it arrived. This whole incident took about 20 minutes, and as a result, I missed the beginning of the opening ceremony. When I finally arrived at school, I explained the situation to my teacher, fully expecting a reprimand for my tardiness. To my surprise, the teacher and my classmates were very understanding and praised my actions. The teacher even mentioned my act of kindness during the assembly, which made me feel proud and relieved.(老师甚至在集会上提到了我的善举，这让我感到骄傲和宽慰。).

Reflecting on this experience, I realized that sometimes taking a risk and doing what you believe is right can lead to unexpectedly positive outcomes. Helping the man in need not only ensured his safety but also taught me an invaluable lesson about compassion and responsibility.(帮助有需要的人不仅确保了他的安全，也教会了我关于同情和责任的宝贵一课。) It’s an experience I still remember vividly because it marked the beginning of my high school journey with an important life lesson.

## 109. 使用困难的科技产品/不喜欢的广告/想换掉的东西/向他人展示新东西 / 事件

What you got it for
How often you use it
And explain how you feel about it；

What product or service it advertises
And explain why you don't like it；

You should say:
What it is
Where it is
How you got it
And explain why you want to replace it；
Describe a time that you showed something new to others
You should say:
When it was
What it was
Who you showed it to
How you showed it
And explain how you felt about it
   - Answer: 蓝牙音箱 (6~6.5)
   - Summary: 因为一个广告，我购买了蓝牙音箱，并向朋友们展示了这个音箱。然而音箱的一些功能使用困难，并不像广告演示的一样方便。因此，我不喜欢这个广告，也想换掉这个产品
   - Content: I remember seeing an advertisement for a Bluetooth speaker about a year ago. It was a flashy, engaging ad that I first saw on a social media platform, probably around late evening while I was scrolling through my feed. The advertisement portrayed the speaker as incredibly easy to use, with excellent sound quality and seamless connectivity, making it seem like the perfect addition to my home audio setup.(广告将这款音箱描述为非常容易使用，音质出色，连接无缝，使它看起来像是我家庭音频设置的完美补充。) It was a video ad that showed people effortlessly connecting their devices and enjoying music in high definition.

I decided to purchase the speaker shortly after seeing the ad. I bought it online and eagerly awaited its arrival, hoping it would live up to the promises made in the advertisement. The main reason I got it was to enhance my music-listening experience and to have a portable option for outdoor gatherings with friends.(我买它的主要原因是为了增强我的音乐聆听体验，并为与朋友在户外聚会提供一个便携的选择。).

However, once I received the speaker and started using it, I quickly realized that it wasn't as user-friendly as the advertisement had suggested. The Bluetooth connectivity was often unreliable, and it would frequently disconnect from my devices. Additionally, the sound quality was not as impressive as it had been portrayed. I found myself struggling to get it to work properly, which was frustrating given the high expectations set by the ad.

Despite these issues, I did use the speaker quite often, trying to make the best out of my purchase. I also showed it to my friends during a small get-together at my place. I demonstrated how to connect it and played some music, but it was clear that they also found it a bit cumbersome to use. Their feedback mirrored my own frustrations.

Because of these ongoing difficulties, I’ve grown to dislike the product and the misleading advertisement that convinced me to buy it. I’m now considering replacing the speaker with a more reliable and user-friendly option. The experience taught me to be more cautious and critical of advertisements in the future, ensuring that I thoroughly research products before making a purchase.(这段经历教会了我以后对广告要更加谨慎和批判，确保在购买之前对产品进行彻底的研究。).

## 110. 【疑似淘汰】不喜欢的工作/投诉 / 事物
1. [Part 4] Describe a job you would not like to do.
You should say:
What the job is?
How do you know about it?
Whether it is an easy or difficult job?
And explain why you would not like to do it?
Describe an occasion when you heard someone complaining about something in a restaurant/store or other business places
You should say:
When and where it happened
What he/she complained about
What the result was
And explain how you felt about the experience
   - Answer: 快餐店 (6~6.5)
   - Summary: 在家附近有一家连锁快餐馆，在餐点经常会有人来用餐。因为店内人手并不是很多，在用餐高峰期的出餐速度不是很快。我在前几周去餐厅吃饭的时候就看到了一位急性子的客人就会选择投诉店家，因为他无法在工作休息的时间完成用餐，他感到十分着急。服务员表示十分抱歉，帮他催促了菜品的制作，并保证在下次来吃饭的时候给他一定的优惠。这让我感到餐厅服务员虽然是一份很有意义的工作，但并不一份简单的工作，得面临顾客投诉以及餐点高峰期的压力，这让我在未来不想当一名餐厅服务员。
   - Content: There is a popular chain of fast food restaurants in my neighborhood, which is especially busy during mealtimes. Frequent patronage there has given me an initial understanding of the demanding food service industry(经常光顾那里让我对要求苛刻的餐饮服务业有了初步了解). A recent experience at this restaurant in particular highlighted the challenges faced by waiters and influenced my view of the profession.

A few weeks ago, amidst the typical dinner rush(正值晚餐高峰期), the restaurant was understaffed, leading to slower service. Amid this chaos(在这种混乱的情况下), a situation unfolded that captured my attention. A customer, evidently under time pressure from his work schedule, voiced his frustration over the delayed service. This incident was a clear example of the challenges waiters frequently encounter. The waiter's response was both professional and empathetic(既专业又富有同情心). He not only apologized profusely but also expedited the preparation of the customer's meal. Furthermore, he offered a discount for the customer's next visit, a gesture that exemplified excellent customer service(他不仅深表歉意，还加快了为顾客准备餐点的速度。此外，他还为顾客的下次光临提供了折扣，这一举动体现了出色的客户服务).

This encounter made me reflect on the role of a restaurant waiter. It is a job that requires a unique blend of skills – the ability to multitask, manage time efficiently, and handle customer complaints with composure and diplomacy(能够一心多用、高效管理时间、沉着冷静地处理顾客投诉). The waiter's role goes beyond merely taking orders and serving food; it involves managing customer expectations and maintaining a high level of service quality, even under stressful conditions like peak meal times.

Witnessing the pressures and challenges inherent in this role, I realized that a career as a restaurant waiter might not align with my personal aspirations. While it is undoubtedly a rewarding job, offering the chance to interact with a diverse range of people and play a key role in their dining experience, it also demands resilience, patience, and exceptional problem-solving skills(要坚韧不拔的精神、耐心和出色的解决问题的能力). This experience has led me to appreciate the hard work and dedication of those in the service industry, while also understanding that it may not be the right fit for everyone.

## 111. 【疑似淘汰】帮助学习工作的事情/家中重要物品 / 事件

And explain how you feel about it

What it is
What you can do with it
How often you use it
And explain why you cannot live without it
   - Answer: 笔记本电脑 (6~6.5)
   - Summary: 笔记本电脑是我家中最重要的物品之一，我觉得如果没有笔记本电脑我无法像平日一样正常生活。我每天都需要使用电脑，因为笔记本有很多功能，能帮我和朋友们取得联系，能让我上网查阅资料，也能让我玩游戏放松。当然最重要的是电脑上还有很好用的软件，比如有一个软件可以制作思维导图，可以帮助整理每天所学的知识。我平常在每天回到宿舍之后都会制作当天所学知识的思维导图，帮助我在未来更好地进行复习。我觉得使用在电脑上制作的思维导图来帮助学习和工作都是很实用的，并想把这个方法分享给我的同学们。
   - Content: In the digital age we live in, technology plays an indispensable role in our lives, and for me, this is epitomized by my laptop(笔记本电脑就是一个缩影). This device is not just a piece of technology; it's a vital tool that significantly enhances my daily life, making it almost unimaginable to function without it.

My reliance on the laptop stems from its multifaceted capabilities. It serves as a portal to the world, connecting me to a vast ocean of information available on the internet(它是通向世界的门户，将我与互联网上浩瀚的信息海洋连接起来). This access is crucial for both my academic pursuits and personal interests. Additionally, it acts as a bridge to my social circle, enabling me to stay in touch with friends through various digital platforms. Beyond these practical uses, it also provides a source of entertainment, allowing me to unwind(放松) with games after a long day.

However, the most significant aspect of my laptop is its powerful software applications. Particularly noteworthy is the mind map software that has become an integral part of my daily routine. Every evening, after returning to my dormitory, I use this software to create mind maps of the day's learnings. This visual organization of information(视觉化的信息组织方式) has proven to be a highly effective method for reviewing and retaining knowledge. It helps me make connections between different concepts, thereby enhancing my understanding and memory.

I've found this approach so beneficial that I'm keen to share it with my peers. I believe that this method of using technology to assist in study and work can be a game-changer for many students. It's a perfect example of how digital tools can be harnessed for educational purposes, transforming the traditional methods of learning and organizing information. In a world where information overload is a common challenge, such tools can provide a much-needed structure(这种工具可以提供急需的结构), aiding in effective learning and productivity.

## 112. 【疑似淘汰】放松之地/延期旅行/改善的公共设施 / 事物
1. [Part 4] Describe a place you would like to go to relax 
You should say:
Where is it
When you would like to go there
What you would do there

Where you planned to travel to
Why you were looking forward to it
Why it had to be delayed
And explain how you felt about the experience
Describe a public facility（e.g. a museum, a library） that has been renovated and improved
You should say:
What the facility is
When it was renovated and improved
What has been renovated and improved
And explain how you feel about it
   - Answer: 三亚 (6~6.5)
   - Summary: 去年的暑假我所在城市的机场完成了升级，不仅升级了的硬件设施，还新增了许多的航线，比如我很期待的直达海南三亚的航班。因为那里一直都是我想去放松的地方，那里有着阳光、沙滩和美丽的大海。我希望在航线开通后就去到三亚，在那里的沙滩上欣赏自然风光，品尝当地的美食，探索热带雨林。可惜航班开通后遇到了台风，我无法搭乘那趟航班去到三亚，更糟的是之后我得参加一个竞赛。因此，我在去年的三亚之行被延期了，我希望我在今年能有更好的行程规划和有更好的运气，能够顺利去到三亚度假。
   - Content: Last summer marked a significant development in my city: the completion of a major upgrade at our local airport. This wasn't just a routine enhancement of facilities; it was a transformation that expanded our horizons, literally. The airport's upgrade included the addition of several new routes(新的航线), the most exciting of which, for me, was the direct flight to Sanya, Hainan.

Sanya had always been a dream destination for me(我梦寐以求的旅游胜地), a place synonymous(代名词) with relaxation and natural beauty. Its reputation for sun-drenched beaches, azure seas(蔚蓝的海洋), and a laid-back lifestyle(悠闲的生活方式) had captivated my imagination for years. The announcement of this direct route filled me with anticipation. I envisaged myself basking in the sunshine, strolling along the sandy shores, indulging in the local cuisine, and exploring the lush tropical rainforests(我憧憬着自己沐浴在阳光下，在沙滩上漫步，品尝当地美食，探索郁郁葱葱的热带雨林).

However, life often has other plans. Just as the new route commenced, a typhoon swept through, derailed my plans to visit Sanya(一场台风席卷而来，使我的三亚之行计划落空). The cancellation of the flight due to this natural event was a significant disappointment. To add to my woes(雪上加霜的是), I had a competition lined up immediately afterward, which further delayed my travel plans.

Reflecting on this experience, I realized that while we can plan, we can't control everything. Last year's setback(挫折) was a lesson in patience and adaptability. As I look forward to this year's vacation, my desire to visit Sanya remains strong. This time, I am approaching my travel plans with a sense of cautious optimism, hoping that better planning and a stroke of good luck will finally allow me to experience the charm and beauty of Sanya. This anticipation of exploring a new place, experiencing its culture, and enjoying its natural beauty is a reminder of the joys and unpredictability(不可预见性) of travel.

what holiday it was
When and where you went
