And explain why it was unusual
   - Answer: 夏令营 (6~6.5)
   - Summary: 我十岁时的暑假假期是一个不寻常的假期，因为我参加了一个夏令营。妈妈帮我买了夏令营的制服，分别是橙色的T恤和黑色的短裤，十分的轻便透气，上面还有着每个人的名字和夏令营的标志。虽然当时我觉得这件衣服并不好看，但是事实上这件衣服在让我们找到大部队很有用，极大方便了老师的管理。这个夏令营的营地在一个风景秀美的山区，我们有进行了各种各样的户外活动，比如登山、钓鱼和放风筝。我喜欢和朋友们一起爬山，一边聊天一边欣赏美景，这让我感觉运动是一件快乐的事情。虽然这个夏令营的时光仅仅只有两个星期，但带给我很多美好的回忆。
   - Content: Reflecting on my childhood, one summer vacation stands out distinctly in my memory. When I was ten, I had the unique opportunity to attend a summer camp, an experience that turned out to be far from ordinary and incredibly enriching.

Before the camp began, my mother prepared me by purchasing the official camp uniform. At first glance(乍一看), the outfit – an orange T-shirt paired with black shorts – didn't strike me as particularly stylish(并不特别时髦). However, it was light, breathable, and, importantly, each shirt bore our names and the camp's logo. This simple uniform played a crucial role(发挥重要作用) in the camp's daily life. It aided the teachers in managing us, a group of energetic kids, and made it easier for us to identify each other during our various activities.

The camp was nestled in a picturesque mountainous region(风景如画的山区), providing the perfect backdrop for a plethora of outdoor activities. Our days were filled with hiking, fishing, kite flying, and more. Among these, hiking was my favorite. Walking along the trails with friends, engaging in lively conversations, and soaking in the breathtaking scenery(我和朋友们漫步在山间小路上，热烈地交谈着，欣赏着壮丽的景色), I discovered the joy in physical activity. It was during these hikes that I realized exercise could be a delightful and fulfilling pursuit.

This two-week camp not only offered a break from the usual routine but also left me with a treasure trove of memories(不仅让我打破了常规，还为我留下了丰富的回忆). The experiences I had and the friendships I formed there have had a lasting impact on me. It taught me valuable lessons about independence, teamwork, and the joy of exploring the great outdoors. This summer camp was more than just a holiday; it was a pivotal chapter in my childhood that shaped my appreciation for nature and adventure.

## 114. 【疑似淘汰】捡到失物/忙碌时期/匆忙做事 / 事物

And explain how you felt about the experience

You should say:
What it was
When it happened
How you finished it
Why you had to finish it quickly
And explain how you felt about it
   - Answer: 复习资料 (6~6.5)
   - Summary: 我的大二学期期末是非常繁忙的时期，因为要参加很多的考试，提交很多的报告和论文。为了能取得好成绩，我的每一天都很忙碌。就在有天晚上，我在图书馆完成了当天的任务，想要回到宿舍休息。在路上我发现了角落里有同学遗失的复习资料。我发现物品的主人应该和我是同一个学院的，并且里面还有明天考试所需的材料。我想同学一定很着急，就迅速通过老师和失主取得了联系。同学对我的帮助感到十分的感激，我感到自己做了一件好事，很有成就感。
   - Content: The end of my sophomore semester(大二学期末) was marked by an intense period of academic pressure, where my daily routine was a whirlwind of exams, reports, and paper submissions. Striving for high grades, I found myself completely immersed in my studies, with each day bringing its own set of challenges and tasks.

One evening, after a long day of hard work in the library, I was making my way back to the dormitory, eager for some much-needed rest. It was then that I stumbled upon something unexpected – revision materials(复习材料) that had been accidentally left behind by one of my classmates. These weren't just any materials; they were crucial for an exam scheduled for the following day.

Realizing the urgency of the situation, I felt a strong sense of responsibility to return these materials to their rightful owner. The thought of my classmate being frantic over the loss of these important notes (因为丢失这些重要的笔记而焦急万分) spurred me into action. With a sense of purpose, I reached out to our teacher to contact the owner of the materials. Fortunately, my efforts were successful, and I was able to promptly reunite my classmate with their lost notes.

The relief and gratitude expressed by my classmate were immensely rewarding(同学的欣慰和感激让我受益匪浅). This experience, albeit small in the grand scheme of things, was a significant moment for me. It highlighted the importance of empathy and taking action (换位思考和采取行动) to help others, even during times when we are preoccupied with our own challenges. The sense of accomplishment I felt was profound, reinforcing the idea that acts of kindness, no matter how small, can have a big impact. This incident was a valuable lesson in compassion and community spirit, traits that are essential in any collaborative and supportive academic environment.

## 115. 【疑似淘汰】超有共鸣的电影/小学活动/长期目标 / 事物
1. [Part 4] Describe a movie/film that you felt strongly about
You should say:
What it is about
When you watched it
Where you watched it
And explain why you felt strongly about it
Describe an activity you enjoyed most in your primary school
You should say:
What the activity was
How often you did the activity
Who you did it with
And explain why it was your favourite activity
Describe a long-term goal you would like to achieve
You should say:
How long you have had this goal
What the goal is
How you will achieve it
And explain why you set this goal
   - Answer: 龙猫 (6~6.5)
   - Summary: 我的小学是一所寄宿制小学，我们在一些节日的晚上会举行特别的活动“电影之夜”。我很喜欢这个活动，因为电影很有趣，能和同学一起看电影班讨论剧情更是难忘。其中有一部电影给我留下了深刻的印象，那是宫崎骏的《龙猫》，讲述了一对小姐妹回到乡下生活，见到了很多神奇生物的故事。这部电影既温馨又清新，登场的人物可爱又生动，我十分喜欢。自从看了那部电影之后，我就有了我的长期目标，那就是制作自己的动画电影。为了达成这个目标，我经常构思故事剧情，了解如何成为一个编剧或者导演，为此阅读很多相关的书籍，并尝试进行制作。
   - Content: Looking back on my elementary school days at a boarding school(寄宿学校), one of the most cherished memories(最珍贵的回忆) is our special event, "Movie Night," held during festival nights. These evenings were not just about watching films; they were a celebration of camaraderie(庆祝友情) and shared experiences with my classmates, making each movie night unforgettable.

One film that particularly resonated(特别有共鸣) with me was Hayao Miyazaki's "Totoro." (宫崎骏的《龙猫》) This enchanting movie, with its story of two young sisters exploring the countryside and encountering magical creatures, left a lasting impression on me. The heartwarming narrative and refreshing animation style(感人至深的叙事和令人耳目一新的动画风格), coupled with the vividly depicted and adorable mystical beings(加上生动描绘的可爱神秘生物), captivated my imagination. "Totoro" wasn't just a film; it was a window into a world of wonder and creativity.

This movie sparked in me a long-term aspiration: to create my own animated movie. Inspired by Miyazaki's masterpiece, I began to nurture this dream with dedication and enthusiasm(奉献和热情). To bring my vision to life, I engaged in various activities. I spent countless hours brainstorming story ideas, delving into the realms of writing and directing. I immersed myself in books and resources about filmmaking and animation(电影和动画制作), absorbing as much knowledge as possible. Additionally, I experimented with producing small animated sequences, understanding that every great journey begins with small steps.

This goal has become a significant part of my life. It represents more than just a career ambition; it symbolizes the power of inspiration and the importance of pursuing one's passions. The journey toward achieving this dream is a testament to the impact a single movie can have on an individual's life. It highlights the transformative power of art and storytelling, and how they can shape one's aspirations and goals(愿望和目标).

## 116. 【疑似淘汰】噪音/街市购物/地图 / 事物
1. [Part 4] Describe an occasion when there was a lot of noise
You should say:
Where you heard the noise
What kinds of noise it was
Who made the noise
How you reacted to the noise
And explain how you felt about the noise
Describe a time you bought something from a street market
You should say:
When it was
Where the market was
What you bought
And how you felt about the experience
Describe a time when you used a （paper）map
You should say:
When you used the map
Where you were
Why you used a paper map
And explain how you felt about the experience
   - Answer: 泉州 (6~6.5)
   - Summary: 一年前，我在泉州旅游的时候走到了热闹的街市，许多游客开心地聊着天，商家用喇叭放着广告词吸引游客，大家很开心，但我只感觉噪音很吵。我其实想去一个在巷子深处的里的漂亮小店，里面有许多艺术家制作的手工艺品。我自从在网上看到这家店之后就很想造访，但是因为手机地图不过准确找不到。我只好一边忍受噪音一边找路，恰好路过了一个有卖当地地图的店铺。我在店里买了一份漂亮的手绘地图，这张地图不但美观还标记出了我想要去到的地方。我感叹这真是一次难忘的经历，并意识到了纸质地图也有独特的价值。
   - Content: About a year ago, I embarked on a journey to Quanzhou, an experience that led to an unexpected yet enlightening discovery. My adventure in Quanzhou was marked by a particular day that stands out vividly(历历在目) in my memory. I found myself in a bustling market, a place teeming with life and activity. The air was filled with the sounds of happy chatter from tourists and the persistent hum of merchants using loudspeakers to attract customers(空气中弥漫着游客们快乐的交谈声和商人们用扩音器吸引顾客的持续嗡嗡声). The market was a tapestry of vibrant sounds and colors, a true representation of the lively local culture(生动的声音和色彩交织在一起，真实地再现了生机勃勃的当地文化).

Despite the festive atmosphere, I felt somewhat overwhelmed by the noise(人声鼎沸), which I perceived more as a cacophony than a cheerful symphony(更像嘈杂的声音，而不是欢快的交响乐). My true intention was to seek a quieter, more serene experience. I had set my heart on visiting a quaint little store tucked away in a deep alleyway, a gem(宝石) known for its exquisite handicrafts created by local artists. This store, which I had stumbled upon online, promised a unique and intimate glimpse into(窥探) the artistic soul of Quanzhou.

However, my journey to this hidden treasure was not straightforward. The inaccuracy of my phone's map led me through a maze of streets, heightening my sense of being lost amidst the noise and commotion. It was during this search that serendipity guided me to a different store, one that sold hand-drawn maps. The map I purchased there was not only aesthetically beautiful but also incredibly accurate(不仅美观大方，而且精确无比), leading me precisely to my desired destination.

This experience taught me an invaluable lesson about the unique charm and utility of traditional paper maps. In a world increasingly reliant on digital technology, there is still a distinct place for the tactile and reliable nature of paper maps. They hold a certain romantic and practical appeal(既浪漫又实用), providing not just directions but also a tangible connection to the places they represent(与所代表的地方产生切实的联系). This realization was a key takeaway from my travels, reminding me that sometimes, traditional methods have their own irreplaceable value in our modern world.

## 117. 【疑似淘汰】帮助他人/年少学艺/ 给力队友 / 事物
1. [Part 4] Describe something you do regularly to help you work or study
You should say:
What it is
When and where you do it
How you do it
And explain how you feel about it
Describe a skill that you learned as a teenager
You should say:
What the skill is
When and how you learned it
Who you learned it from
Why you learned it
And explain how you felt about learning it
Describe a time when someone who did quite well in a team (e.g. schoolwork or a community)
You should say:
Who this person is
When you worked together
What team project you worked on
And explain why you think he/she was a great team member
   - Answer: 急救 (6~6.5)
   - Summary: 我在14岁时学校开展了关于急救技术的教学活动。我们先是观看了播放的教学视频，然后在红十字会志愿者的教学下，我和同学一起学习了如何给人进行急救，比如说如何安抚患者情绪，进行包扎和心肺复苏。在学习之后开展了急救技术比赛，我和好友小王是队友，他不但技术操作到位，而且很会进行团队合作，是一位很好的队友。恰好在不久之后我和小王在放学途中看到一位老人晕倒了。我们使用了我们学到的急救知识进行了帮助，在救护车到来后我们才离开。这次经历让我意识到急救是很实用的技术，我为能帮助他人而感到颇有成就感。
   - Content: During my secondary school days, when I was 14, a memorable and transformative experience unfolded(难忘且具有转变性的经历就此展开). Our school, emphasizing the practical aspects of education(强调教育的实用性), organized a comprehensive first aid training program(综合急救培训计划). This initiative was not merely a theoretical exercise(理论练习); it was a hands-on learning experience that proved its worth in an unforeseen situation(始料未及的情况下).

Initially, the program commenced with an instructional video(教学视频). This video served as an introductory tool, outlining the basics of first aid. Following this, Red Cross volunteers(红十字会志愿者), who were experts in their field, conducted an interactive session. Their guidance was invaluable; under their watchful eyes, we learned crucial life-saving techniques. These included calming patients, performing bandages, and the critical skill of CPR(安抚病人、进行包扎以及心肺复苏这一关键技能).

The practical nature of this training culminated in a first aid competition(在急救比赛中达到了高潮), which was both challenging and enlightening. In this competition, I teamed up with my good friend Wang. Wang's proficiency in first aid techniques, coupled with his exceptional teamwork skills, made him an ideal partner. Together, we navigated the challenges of the competition, applying our newly acquired skills in a simulated environment.

However, the true test of our learning came unexpectedly. Shortly after the completion of the course, Wang and I encountered a real-life emergency. An elderly man fainted on(晕倒) our way home from school. Drawing upon our training, we sprang into action, employing the first aid techniques we had learned. We stayed with the gentleman, offering assistance and comfort until the arrival of an ambulance.

This experience was a defining moment for me. It underscored the practicality and importance of first aid knowledge. The ability to help others in a critical moment was not only a duty but also a source of deep personal accomplishment(对他人的生活产生深远的影响). It instilled in me a sense of responsibility and a realization that the skills we learn can have a profound impact on the lives of others. This incident, thus, was not just a learning experience but a life lesson in empathy, quick thinking, and the significance of being prepared for emergencies.

## 118. 【疑似淘汰】和老人的有趣谈话/客至如归/能说会道的人 / 人物
1. [Part 4] Describe an interesting conversation you had with a very old person
You should say:
Who this person is
Where you had the conversation
What you talked about
And explain how you felt about the experience
Describe a person who is good at making people feel welcome in his/her home
You should say:
Who this person is
How you knew him/her
How he/she makes you feel welcome
And explain why you think he/she is good at welcoming visitors/guests
Describe a person you know who likes to talk a lot
You should say:
Who this person is
How you knew this person
What he/she usually talks about
And explain how you felt about him/her
   - Answer: 祖母 (6~6.5)
   - Summary: 祖母是一个健谈且热情好客的人，和她的谈话总是很有趣，每位造访她家的人都会感到很愉快。在一次我去她家拜访她的时候，向她请教了如何使用风趣幽默的语言让来来到家里的人感到宾至如归。她先让我我回忆了以前她是如何招待其他的亲戚朋友的，比如提供他们喜欢吃的食物或者聊他们感兴趣的话题。又跟我分享了她的成长经历，这是她总喜欢提到的事情。我从小就很喜欢听祖母说话，在多次聊天后感觉我们的关系更加亲近了，并也想成为热情好客的人。
   - Content: My grandmother was a very talkative and hospitable(健谈又好客) person who had a unique charm(独特魅力) that made anyone who visited her home feel that talking to her was not only interesting, but a pleasant experience. Thinking back on it, I have a vivid memory of one particular visit.

She was not only my grandmother, but a symbol of warmth and friendliness in our home. Her age never dimmed her spirit; on the contrary, it seemed to enrich her ability to connect with people(她的年龄从未削弱她的精神，相反，这似乎丰富了她与人沟通的能力). We last spoke in her cozy living room, a place that always feels more like a sanctuary of memories and warmth. The walls are covered with family photos and the scent of her cooking fills the air, creating an atmosphere that is both cozy and intimate.

During this particular visit, I sought her advice on using witty and humorous(风趣幽默) language to make guests feel welcome, much like she always did. She began by encouraging me to recall how she entertained relatives and friends, emphasizing the importance of personal touches like serving their favorite dishes or engaging in topics that sparked their interest.

She also delved into(探讨) stories of her own upbringing, a topic she was particularly fond of. Her tales were not just stories; they were lessons in life, hospitality, and the art of conversation. Listening to her, I realized how her experiences shaped her approach to making others feel at home.

As the conversation flowed, I felt a profound connection with her. Her words were not just advice; they were a legacy she was passing on. I left with a deep appreciation of her wisdom and a renewed desire to emulate her hospitality(离开时，我对她的智慧深表赞赏，并再次渴望效仿她的热情好客). The experience was enlightening(启发), leaving me with valuable insights into the art of making others feel welcome and the importance of preserving family traditions.

## 141. 第一天上学/迟到 / 事物
1. [Part 4] 第一天上学
Describe the first day you went to school that you remember
You should say:
How you went there
What happened that day
Where the school was
And how you felt on that day

迟到
Describe a time when you missed or were late for a meeting
You should say:
When it happened
What happened
Why you missed/were late for it
And explain how you felt about this experience
   - Answer: 第一天上小学迟到 (6~6.5)
   - Summary: 小学第一天因选择打车而遭遇严重堵车，导致迟到并错过校长的新生欢迎会。当全班同学盯着迟到的我时，场面十分尴尬，老师还警告下次不许迟到。这次经历让我明白：在市区出行应优先选择地铁，才能避免交通拥堵。
Bumper-to-bumper jam - 严重堵车
Snail's pace - 龟速行进
Frustrated - 懊恼的
Embarrassing - 尴尬的
Traffic congestion - 交通堵塞
Lesson learned - 吸取教训
Welcome meeting - 迎新会
   - Content: The first day at my primary school left the deepest impression on me. My primary school was not near our apartment, and usually it would take about 30 minutes to get there. However, on the first day, I was late since we got stuck in some heavy traffic, and I was criticized by my teacher, which was quite a bad experience(糟糕的经历).

If my memory is correct, my dad and I got up and left home early, but we mistakenly chose to take a taxi over using the subway, since we thought it would be the fastest way to get there. However, soon after entering the taxi, we found ourselves in a bumper-to-bumper jam(堵车) and the traffic moved at a snail’s pace(如乌龟一般爬行). We were very frustrated, since it was impossible for us to do anything about it, and the only thing we could do was to wait in the taxi. Eventually we arrived at school, but I was late for my first day and I even missed the whole welcome meeting held by the headmaster. The moment I got into the classroom, all my classmates were staring at me, which was really embarrassing. What’s more, my teacher also warned me not to be late next time.

From the experience, I learned a lesson, which is to use the underground metro to avoid inner city traffic congestion.

## 150. 让你自豪的照片/侍花弄果之人 / 事物
1. [Part 4] 让你自豪的照片/侍花弄果之人
   - Answer: 我拍下喜欢种花的奶奶后得到金钱奖励 (6.5~7)
   - Summary: 奶奶喜欢种植物，做插花；我拍下她做插花的照片，很有艺术性，投稿到摄影报刊上被登在头版，我非常自豪；奶奶很高兴，夸我有天赋，赏给我一笔钱，支持我买最新的摄影设备。
   - Content: My grandma is a person who grows a lot of plants and flowers. She lives on the ground floor, so she has a big yard to grow things. My grandma has planted a variety of beautiful flowers in the yard, such as roses, gardenia(栀子花), begonia(海棠花) and so on. Every year in spring, her garden is always very beautiful. In addition to having a beautiful garden, another reason why she likes to grow flowers is that she likes to arrange them(插花). For this reason, she attends a flower arrangement class. As the oldest student in the class, she always gets a lot of praise(收获到很多掌声).

I like photography very much. I often take my SLR camera(单反相机) to all corners of the city to find inspiration(寻找灵感). About six months ago, I went to the flower arrangement class with my grandma. In the class, I took a picture of her arranging flowers. This photo is very artistic(艺术性), and coupled with(再加上) the bright flowers in the background, it is a very beautiful photo. She encouraged me to submit it to the local newspaper, so I did so, without expecting much. However, the photo was on the front page 3 months later! I am very proud of myself, and my grandma is always boasting(夸赞) about how talented I am.

There was another surprise about two weeks ago when my grandma gave me some money to help me buy the latest photography equipment, so I bought a new lens(镜头) with the money last week. I plan to join her again at the flower arrangement class next week so I can take more beautiful pictures.

## 151. 失约/争论/和朋友的争执/不喜欢到喜欢的朋友 / 事物
1. [Part 4] 同学可以结合题库的具体问题，练习素材。
1. 为了更好的匹配每一道题，素材本身的字数会超过真实的考试同学们能表达字数。
2. 针对不同的问法，同学的开头和结尾需要进行调整。
3. 一定要注意表达的自然程度～必要时增加重音，表情和手势
   - Answer: 没去面试引发的争论 (6.5~7)
   - Summary: 我已经收到了心仪offer，因为之前是海投，所以又收到了新面试邀请，我却没去。对象责怪我不守约定、不再看看机会，我认为已经收到了满意offer就没必要去，因此引发了争论。
Resume – 简历
Interview – 面试
Opportunity – 机会
Urge – 催促
Retract – 撤回
Inexperienced – 缺乏经验的
Satisfactory – 令人满意的
Quarrel – 争吵
Advance – 提前
   - Content: I started looking for a job as soon as I graduated from college last year. I had no work experience and I didn't know enough about myself, so I sent my resume to almost every company I had heard of. After sending them all out, I was invited for an interview by COMPANY A, who offered me a job.

Unfortunately, because I had sent out so many resumes, I also received an interview invitation(面试邀请) from COMPANY B after receiving the offer from COMPANY A. I had a decision to make, but I thought to myself “Why not? It might lead to another opportunity” . I therefore agreed to the invitation. What I didn't expect was COMPANY A urging me(催促我) to start work as soon as possible, otherwise they would retract(默认) their offer. I was only young and inexperienced, so I thought that the best thing to do was to start work at company A.

However, the day I started work was also the day of the interview at COMPANY B, so I had to inform COMPANY B that I could not attend. It was not an easy decision to make, and my boyfriend said that since I had agreed to the interview, I should have attended it, or at least informed them earlier that I could not go. He also said that I should have gone to the interview in case it was a better opportunity, but I was satisfied that I had received a satisfactory offer from COMPANY A and that there was no need to go to company B. For this reason, my boyfriend and I quarreled. However, I did not regret my decision, because I am very satisfied with my job at COMPANY A, and I also informed company B well in advance(提前). My boyfriend might disagree, buy I don’t think I did anything wrong.

## 152. 印象深刻的英语课/信息搜索 / 事物
1. [Part 4] 同学可以结合题库的具体问题，练习素材。
1. 为了更好的匹配每一道题，素材本身的字数会超过真实的考试同学们能表达字数。
2. 针对不同的问法，同学的开头和结尾需要进行调整。
3. 一定要注意表达的自然程度～必要时增加重音，表情和手势
   - Answer: 通过搜索信息写报告学英语 (6.5~7)
   - Summary: 我记得刚上高中的时候，我们学校来了一个外教。他的教学方法和传统的中式教学很不一样，他喜欢让我们自己查询信息，写报告然后做演讲。我记得第一节课的时候，他让我们在网上查中美两国的文化差异，并在一周后做演讲给全班听。于是我们分成了几个小组，按不同的方向每个人都需要查信息。我家里有电脑，所以周末的时候就在家里完成了。这个授课方式我觉得很新颖，同时我认为效果非常好。我不但学习到了检索信息的能力，还通过这个方式学到了文化差异，做演讲也让我有勇气大声讲英语。我非常享受那次课程。
   - Content: I remember in high school when a new foreign teacher from America, called Sam, came to our school. This was my first time taking a foreign teacher's class, and I felt both excited and energized(充满了新鲜感). Sam's teaching method was very different from traditional Chinese teaching. Traditional Chinese teaching is mainly based on books(以书本为主) and learning grammar and vocabulary, because teachers expect students to get a good score in exams. But Sam wanted us to do research projects, write reports and give presentations in front of the class.

I remember in one of his classes when he asked us to research the cultural differences between China and the United States on the Internet, and prepare a presentation for the whole class a week later. So, at Sam's request(在Sam的要求下), we divided into small groups and everyone looked up information on different topics. I had a computer at home so I did my research at home on the weekend.

I think his teaching methods were very innovative and effective. Not only did I develop the ability to retrieve information(检索信息), which will undoubtedly be very helpful for me when I study abroad and write dissertations in the future, but I also discovered many cultural differences. At the same time, giving speeches allowed me to overcome my shyness(克服了自己的羞怯) and gave me the courage to speak English in front of people. I thoroughly enjoyed his classes.

## 153. 糟糕购物/决意等待 / 事物
1. [Part 4] 同学可以结合题库的具体问题，练习素材。
1. 为了更好的匹配每一道题，素材本身的字数会超过真实的考试同学们能表达字数。
2. 针对不同的问法，同学的开头和结尾需要进行调整。
3. 一定要注意表达的自然程度～必要时增加重音，表情和手势
   - Answer: 买到错的电脑但我决意等待 (6.5~7)
   - Summary: 大概半年前我想买一台电脑，为明年要写的毕业论文做准备。选了很久后，我终于决定买某个品牌的最新款电脑。在网上下了订单后我开始兴奋又焦急地等待。没想到电脑还没到，商家就联系了我，因为迟到的订单表达了歉意。
Budget – 预算
Place an order – 下单
Unexpectedly – 出乎意料地
Inconvenience – 不便
Compensation – 补偿
Frustrating – 令人沮丧的
Generous – 慷慨的
Customer service – 客户服务
   - Content: About six months ago, I wanted to buy a computer to prepare for my graduation thesis(毕业论文) that was coming up. There are so many brands and models of computer on the market, and my budget was not very high, so I asked some friends for their opinions and referred to many online guides(参考了很多网上的指南). After a long time considering all the options, I finally decided to buy the latest brand XX computer.

After making the decision, I immediately placed my order(下单) online and started to wait excitedly and anxiously. Unexpectedly, before the computer arrived, the seller contacted me. It turned out that(原来是) the he had sent me the wrong model. As an apology and compensation(补偿) for the inconvenience, the seller offered me a discount on the incorrect order. He also said that if I was not happy with that, I could return the wrong computer when it arrived and he would then ship my correct order. It was frustrating, but I had no choice but to wait for the incorrect order to arrive.

After it was delivered, I found that it actually performed very well, and the discount that the merchant agreed to give me was very generous. Plus, I didn't want to wait another 2 weeks for my original order, so I decided to keep this one. I've been using it for six months now, and I'm very satisfied with my decision. I was also satisfied with the seller’s customer service.

## 154. 喜欢看的电影/有趣小说或故事/搞笑电影 / 事件
1. [Part 4] 喜欢看的电影/有趣小说或故事/搞笑电影
Describe a story or novel you have read that you found interesting
Describe a movie you watched recently and would like to watch again
Describe a film that made you laugh
   - Answer: 傲慢与偏见 (6.5~7)
   - Summary: 简·奥斯汀的这部经典小说通过伊丽莎白与达西的爱情故事，幽默讽刺地展现了19世纪英国社会的阶级观念与婚姻观。机智有趣的对话、生动的人物和深刻的社会洞察力使其成为永恒佳作，改编影视作品也广受喜爱。
Regency era – 摄政时期
Navigates – 探讨
Wit – 机智
Intricate – 复杂的
Cinematography – 电影摄影
Subtlety – 微妙
Resonated – 引起共鸣
Authenticity – 真实性
Evoke – 唤起
Cinematic – 电影的
   - Content: One of the interesting stories that captivated me was the novel "Pride and Prejudice" by Jane Austen. I first read it a few years ago and was drawn to the captivating tale of Elizabeth Bennet and Mr. Darcy set in the Regency era. The novel navigates themes of class, marriage, and societal expectations through the engaging interactions of its characters. Jane Austen's wit and social commentary are brilliantly showcased in this timeless classic. The vivid descriptions and the intricate character developments kept me entranced throughout the book.

Recently, I had the pleasure of watching the movie adaptation of "Pride and Prejudice". This romantic drama set in the same era as the novel beautifully brought to life the complex relationships and societal norms portrayed in Austen's work. I watched it on the popular Chinese video platform Bilibili, where I often find excellent quality films. The film's cinematography, costume design, and talented cast made the viewing experience truly enjoyable. The subtlety of emotions and the chemistry between the lead characters left a lasting impression on me.

Watching this adaptation was a delightful experience that brought both laughter and joy. The elaborate ballroom scenes and the humorous exchanges between Elizabeth and Mr. Darcy provided moments of comedic relief. I watched it with my close friends, and our shared laughter and enjoyment added to the overall experience. The wit and charm of the characters, coupled with the clever dialogue, made the film a perfect blend of humor and romance. It truly captured the essence of Austen's story while adding a modern touch that resonated with the audience.

I would love to watch this movie again because of its timeless appeal and heartwarming storyline. The humor, romance, and intricate plot make it a film that I could rewatch multiple times and still find it engaging. The themes of love, self-discovery, and societal expectations are portrayed with such depth and authenticity that each viewing offers a new perspective. The film's ability to evoke a range of emotions, from laughter to romance, makes it a cinematic treasure that I would eagerly revisit on any given day.

## 156. 侍花弄果之人/让你自豪的照片/激励你做有趣事情的人/聪明的人/劝你的人/被夸赞的经历 / 人物

   - Answer: 激励我种植花草的奶奶 (6.5~7)
   - Summary: 奶奶热爱园艺，因年轻时在乡村务农。如今在城里院子种花种菜，如玫瑰、橘树等，教我体验种植乐趣，强调有机健康，感悟生命成长。
乡村 countryside
有机食物 organic food
农药 pesticides
幼苗 seedlings
结果 bear fruit
   - Content: My grandma really likes to grow all kinds of flowers and vegetables. I think it might have something to do with her experience when she was younger. She lived in the countryside for a while when she was young, and at that time she grew vegetables and fruits. Although she lives in the city now, she still misses the time when she was young. Fortunately, her home on the ground floor has a large yard so she can continue her planting passion. My grandma always plants beautiful flowers and fresh vegetables and fruits in the yard, such as roses, orange trees and so on.

In fact, the orange tree was planted by both of us a year ago. However, the tree is still very small, and it is estimated that(估计) it will take several years to really grow and bear fruit (结果). The vegetables that she has grown in her yard this year, such as green peppers, tomatoes and mint, were also planted by the two of us. It was super interesting and demanding, my grandma give me a praise for my hard work, which I thought was the best reward.

My grandma always inspires me to grow plants with her. She said that, first of all, it is difficult to buy natural vegetables and fruits without pesticides(农药) in the city. If you grow your own, you can eat natural and organic food(有机食物), which is good for your health. Second, she enjoys the process of growing plants from seedlings(植物从小苗长大的过程), and in her words, it is like she has watched me grow from a baby to an adult. She hopes that by growing plants together, I will be able to appreciate the difficulty and reward of taking care of life.

## 157. 塑料废品/漂亮物品/常去的熟人之家/别人家的房间 / 事件
1. [Part 4] 同学可以结合题库的具体问题，练习素材。
1. 为了更好的匹配每一道题，素材本身的字数会超过真实的考试同学们能表达字数。
2. 针对不同的问法，同学的开头和结尾需要进行调整。
3. 一定要注意表达的自然程度～必要时增加重音，表情和手势
   - Answer: 熟人家里有很多塑料废品制作成的工艺品 (6~6.5)
   - Summary: 我的好朋友的父亲是一个艺术家，他最擅长的就是变废为宝。他家里总是有很多的塑料垃圾，比如瓶子什么的，但是他总是能把这些塑料垃圾变成艺术品。我大概每个月都会去朋友家，去看看他的父亲有没有新的作品，我很喜欢他家，虽然他家看起来很乱，每次我都想帮他把这些塑料垃圾收拾干净，但是一想到他父亲能把这些垃圾变废为宝，就觉得很神奇。
Recycling plant – 回收厂
Lifelike – 栩栩如生的
Convey – 传达
Harmony – 和谐
Messy – 杂乱的
Treasure – 珍宝
   - Content: My good friend's father is an artist who is very famous in our local area and has gradually become famous in China. What he does best is turn waste into wonderful works of art(变废为宝). In other words, there is always a lot of plastic waste in his house, such as bottles, bags and packaging, because he goes to the recycling plant(垃圾回收厂) to collect clean plastic and bring it home with him. But this garbage is not garbage to him, it is his art form, and he has always been able to turn plastic waste into art through his magical hands and mind.

My favorite creation of his is an eagle made of plastic bottles and bags, which is very lifelike(栩栩如生), just like a real model of an eagle, and very beautiful. He said that the eagle was influenced by National Geographic(受到了国家地理杂志的影响), and that he wants to convey through this work the idea(传达…的思想) that humans should live in harmony with nature (人类应该和大自然和谐相处). I heard from my friend that his father's most expensive work of art was sold for hundreds of thousands of yuan, which really surprised me.

I go to my friend's house about once a month, sometimes to play with him, but more often to see if his father has created any new works of art. I like his house a lot, even though it looks messy, just like a small recycling plant. Every time I go there, I want to help him clean up all the plastic, but then I am reminded of all the ways his father can turn it into treasure and the meaning it has for people.

## 159. 运动场所/向旅游者推荐你国家的一个地方/想再去一次的城市 / 地点
1. [Part 4] 同学可以结合题库的具体问题，练习素材。
1. 为了更好的匹配每一道题，素材本身的字数会超过真实的考试同学们能表达字数。
2. 针对不同的问法，同学的开头和结尾需要进行调整。
3. 一定要注意表达的自然程度～必要时增加重音，表情和手势
   - Answer: 水立方 (6.5~7)
   - Summary: 我去过的，同时也推荐所有旅游者都去的一个地方是水立方。这是北京的一个标志性建筑，同时也是2008年北京奥运会的运动场馆。我是2008年奥运会去的，非常有幸去里面观看了一场游泳比赛。现在水立方对所有人都开放了，所以任何人都可以进去参观和锻炼。
Iconic – 标志性的
Venue – 场馆
Transform – 改造
Fortunate – 幸运的
Entrance fee – 入场费
Arena – 竞技场
Stand-alone – 单体的
   - Content: One place I've been to, and that I also recommend to travelers, is the Water Cube(水立方) at the National Aquatics Center(国家游泳中心). This is an iconic(标志性的) building in Beijing, located in the Beijing Olympic Park, and was the venue for the swimming events at the 2008 Olympic Games. During the games, 25 world records(打破25项世界纪录) were broken inside the Water Cube. After the Olympic Games, half of the interior of the Water Cube was transformed into(被改造成) a leisure park.

I went to the Water Cube in 2008 because I was very fortunate to have had a ticket to one of the swimming events. Nowadays, the Water Cube is not just a place for swimming competitions, but it's also open to the public, which means anyone can visit it and exercise inside. The entrance fee is relatively cheap. I remember that it only costs 30 RMB per visit and 50 RMB for swimming. If you live around the Water Cube, you can also get a season pass or an annual pass(季票和年票). For such an Olympic-standard national-level arena(奥运标准的国家级赛场), the price is very cheap.

I really like it there and fully support the idea to open it to the public. First of all, the Water Cube is one of the most famous and iconic buildings in China, and anyone who travels to Beijing should visit and experience this huge stand-alone building(单体建筑). Tourists can get a sense of the history that was made at the 2008 Beijing Olympic Games and exercise at the same time, so I highly recommend tourists visiting here.

## 160. 认识的不同文化的人/发小/表达情绪的人/时尚人士/想要一起学习or工作的人 / 人物
1. [Part 4] 同学可以结合题库的具体问题，练习素材。
1. 为了更好的匹配每一道题，素材本身的字数会超过真实的考试同学们能表达字数。
2. 针对不同的问法，同学的开头和结尾需要进行调整。
3. 一定要注意表达的自然程度～必要时增加重音，表情和手势
   - Answer: 时尚的法国发小 (6.5~7)
   - Summary: 我有一个从小就认识的朋友，叫Gabriel, 他来自法国，小的时候因为父母工作的原因在中国上了幼儿园，我非常喜欢他穿衣服的风格，很独特，受到各种亚文化的审美影响。我希望以后能和他一起在这个领域工作
Fascinating – 迷人的
Bilingual – 双语的
Chic – 优雅的
Streetwear – 街头风格
Subcultures – 亚文化
Fusion – 融合
Pastries – 甜点
Multicultural – 多元文化的
Bold – 大胆的
Unique – 独特的
   - Content: I'd like to talk about my childhood friend Gabriel, who has one of the most fascinating cultural backgrounds I know. (我想聊聊我儿时的朋友Gabriel，他有着我所知道的最迷人的文化背景).

Gabriel was born in France (出生在法国), but moved to China when he was just 3 years old because of his parents' work. We met in kindergarten (我们在幼儿园相识) and became inseparable throughout elementary school. What's interesting is that while he's technically French, he's practically bilingual (双语者) and understands Chinese culture as deeply as any local.

What I admire most about Gabriel is his incredible fashion sense (时尚品味). His style is a perfect blend of Parisian chic (巴黎式的优雅) and Chinese streetwear (中国街头风格), with influences from various subcultures like punk and skateboarding (受到朋克、滑板等亚文化影响). While most kids at school wore regular jeans and T-shirts, Gabriel would show up in vintage leather jackets (复古皮夹克) paired with traditional Chinese cloth shoes - and somehow made it look cool!

Beyond fashion, Gabriel has taught me so much about cultural fusion (文化融合). He'd bring French pastries (法式甜点) to share during Chinese festivals, and explain how certain Western art movements influenced modern Asian design. Our conversations always open my eyes to new perspectives.

I really hope we can work together in the fashion industry someday. With his multicultural background (多元文化背景) and bold creativity, I know we could create something truly unique that bridges East and West. (我知道我们可以创造出真正连接东西方的独特作品).

## 168. 社交媒体上常刷的人/感兴趣的名人 / 
1. [Part 4] 社交媒体上常刷的人（确认新题）
Describe a person who you follow on social media

How you knew him/her 
What he/she posts on social media 
And explain why you follow him/her on social media 
感兴趣的名人（确认保留）
Describe a famous person you are interested in
You should say:
Who he/she is
How you knew about him/her
What he/she was like before he/she became famous
And explain why you are interested in him/her
   - Answer: 我在社交媒体上常常刷到的人也是我感兴趣的名人 (6.5~7)
   - Summary: 我在社交媒体上常常刷到的人（who，how，what，why）也是我感兴趣的名人（who，how ，what，why）
   - Content: I am learning German, so I often watch some German movies and listen to German songs. I especially like a rapper from Frankfurt whose name is Vega. He may not be famous in China, and in fact, he's probably not very famous outside of Germany, but that doesn't stop him being my favorite celebrity(并不妨碍他成为我最喜欢的名人).

I know him through my boyfriend who is German and who actually grew up in Frankfurt. I first became aware of the singer when I was introduced to some of his songs, and of course I followed his Instagram. The rapper often posts details about his life on Instagram, and makes fans aware of newly released songs. He also posts some album covers and the stories behind the albums he has recorded. Before Vega was famous, he worked in various bars and clubs, and spent most of his spare time writing songs and composing music. This hard work paid off(功夫不负有心人), as he is now a rising star in the German rap world(德语饶舌界的一枚新星). My boyfriend also likes him very much and has been to several of his concerts. The most unexpected thing is that Vega actually went to his house once! It actually happened because my boyfriend lives with his brother. Three years ago, when we were travelling in New Zealand, only his brother was at home. His brother is a fan of the local football team Eintracht Frankfurt and Vega supports them too. One evening, they met while drinking in a bar, and my boyfriend's younger brother invited Vega to our house, but I didn't expect him to say yes! My boyfriend's brother told him I was a huge fan, and he gave me a jumper as a gift and sang along to some of the albums that he had in the home! What a great surprise when I came back! Although I didn't see him in person, sitting on the sofa he sat on still felt like a dream come true(梦想成真).

## 184. 分享/健康文章/校外学习的重要事情 / 事物
1. [Part 4] 同学可以结合题库的具体问题，练习素材。
1. 为了更好的匹配每一道题，素材本身的字数会超过真实的考试同学们能表达字数。
2. 针对不同的问法，同学的开头和结尾需要进行调整。
3. 一定要注意表达的自然程度～必要时增加重音，表情和手势
   - Answer: 在网上买了本健康杂志分享给朋友 (6.5~7)
   - Summary: 这商店有各类图书，我看到了一本叫《健康世界》的杂志，它封面上的标题—“如何提高睡眠质量”。因为我的朋友Emily最近被失眠所困扰，经常找我抱怨。于是我买下了这本书并迫不及待地分享给了Emily。
Specialize – 专营
Second-hand – 二手的
Out of print – 绝版的
Insomnia – 失眠
Reliable – 可靠的
Posture – 姿势
Unconsciousness – 无意识
Meditation – 冥想
Professionalism – 专业性
   - Content: When I was shopping online last week, I happened to come to a store that specialized in second-hand books and magazines. This store was full of second-hand bookstores, with all kinds of books, comics, magazines, new and old, and even many books that were out of print(绝版书). I am a person who likes to read very much, so I wandered around.

While browsing, I saw a magazine called "Health World". What attracted me was the title on its cover --- "How to Improve Sleep Quality". My friend Emily had recently been suffering from insomnia(失眠), and she often complained to me in the middle of the night. She tried to find a professional doctor and took sleeping pills, but her quality of sleep was still not improving. After reading this article, I felt that its methods to solve insomnia mentioned in it looked very reliable and should be of great help to Emily. For example, it mentioned in the article that you need to adopt a comfortable sleeping position when sleeping. We may feel that it is impossible to control our sleeping posture when we sleep because we will be in a state of unconsciousness(无意识状态). In fact, this can be done using the methods mentioned in the article. You can also use meditation(冥想) to help sleep. You can think about things that make you happy, or things that you want to do before sleep.

So, I bought this magazine and couldn't wait to share it with Emily. Just yesterday, Emily told me that the method from the article was highly effective. I am very happy that by sharing this I could help her. At the same time, I also think the professionalism of this article is worthy of recognition(这篇文章的专业性是值得肯定的).

## 197. 现场体育比赛/教别人的技能/看过的体育比赛/喜欢的节目/想看的体育赛事/经常登录的网站 / 事物
1. [Part 4] 现场体育比赛/教别人的技能/看过的体育比赛/喜欢的节目/想看的体育赛事/经常登录的网站Describe a sports event you would like to watch
Describe a sports competition you watched.
Describe a website you often visit
   - Answer: 被排球赛吸引以致于可以教别人打排球 (6.5~7)
   - Summary: 我两年前在我们城市的体育馆里观看了一次现场的排球比赛。整场比赛气氛非常好，选手们在比赛前会拥抱，在比赛中也会给对方加油、打气，排球在他们的传击下舞动、飞跃，非常具有观赏性。
Atmosphere – 氛围
Magnificent – 壮观的
Pique – 激起（兴趣）
Eager – 渴望的
Selection – 选择
Acquire – 掌握
Defend – 防守
Practical – 实用的
Improve – 提高
   - Content: Two years ago, I watched a live volleyball match in the stadium of my city. To be honest, the atmosphere was quite good. Players hugged each other before the match and they were encouraging each other(加油打气) during it. The ball rose, traveled and fell, which was quite magnificent(壮观的).

Because of this match, my interest in playing volleyball was piqued(被激发起对......的兴趣), so I joined the volleyball club at school. I was eager to be a good player so I practiced every day. After two years’ practice, I was able to play very well. On weekends(每逢周末), I always went to play with my friends and I think it was a good way to keep fit and stay in shape(保持身材) as well. What’s more, when I learnt that my cousin chose volleyball as her PE selection in the Senior High School Entrance Exam next year, I decided to teach her how to play it.

For a start, I’m going to teach her some basic knowledge of playing volleyball, such as how to move her hands, how to shoot and so on. When she’s acquired this knowledge(学会......知识), I’d like to show her some useful skills, such as how to defend, which is particularly helpful and practical in matches. After that, I’ll practice with her every day to make sure she improves quickly and gets a good grade in her test.

## 241. 收钱作为礼物/喜欢的节目/被夸赞的经历/家里放松的地方 / 事物
1. [Part 4] 给钱作为礼物/漂亮物品/收到想要的物品/喜欢的节目
Describe a time when someone gave 
you money as a gift
Describe an object that you think is beautiful. 
Describe a program you like to watch.
Describe a time when someone gave you something that you really wanted.
   - Answer: 给钱作为礼物/漂亮物品/收到想要的物品/喜欢的节目 (6~6.5)
   - Summary: 庆祝春节的活动，我们在看我们最喜欢的春晚，因为春晚里面有各种各样的节目，长辈给了我们小辈一个大大的红包作为礼物，作为我们在去年表现良好，好好学习的奖励和夸赞，也祝愿我们明年能更加努力。
Showcase – 展示
Delightful – 愉快的
Generous – 慷慨的
Well-designed – 精心设计的
Outline – 勾勒
Decorate – 装饰
Strive – 奋斗
Cherish – 珍惜
Savor – 品味
Bond – 纽带
Anticipate – 期待
   - Content: During the Lunar New Year celebration, my favorite activity is watching the Spring Festival Gala with my family. The Gala showcases various programs related to traditional Chinese culture, making it a delightful experience. Interestingly, during this celebration, the elders in the family would give the younger ones like me a generous red envelope as a gift.

You know, the red envelope is not a typical envelope with red color, our envelopes are usually so well-designed that everyone would find it beautiful on the first sight. We would use golden glitters to outline ancient animals like dragon, phoenix or animal of the year to decorate it.

This tradition serves as a reward and recognition for our good behavior and hard work in the past year, while also encouraging us to strive for even better in the coming year. I truly cherish the Lunar New Year festival as it allows us to gather together, enjoy the performances, and savor delicious festive treats. The bond created through these moments with my family fills my heart with joy and warmth, making it a celebration that I eagerly anticipate every year.

## 242. 环保人士/有趣的演讲 / 事物
1. [Part 4] Describe a person who helps to protect 
the environment 
Describe an interesting talk or lecture
   - Answer: 环保人士/有趣的演讲 (6~6.5)
   - Summary: 我参加了市图书馆举办的环保讲座，主讲人是一位从事垃圾回收20年的前清洁工。他分享了垃圾分类的实践经验，并以法国每月强制回收2公斤分类垃圾等生动例子，让环保话题变得有趣而发人深省。
Descendants - 子孙后代
Environmentalist - 环保专家
Peak tourist season - 旅游高峰期
Recyclable - 可回收的
Mandatory - 强制性的
Sorted collection - 分类回收
Activist - 环保活动家
Overlooked - 被忽视的
   - Content: I always care about environmental protection as it not only concerns people living in the world now, but also is related to the happiness of our descendants(子孙后代). Therefore, when my friend told me the Environment Bureau were to hold a lecture themed on environmental protection and they invite a professional environmentalist(环保主义者). Therefore, on last weekend, I went to the city library to listen to the lecture.

The speaker has been recycling garbage for nearly two decades, and he has accumulated much experience. He was once a cleaner, responsible for sweeping the floor in a famous scenic spot. He said he could collect over one ton of garbage a day during the peak tourist season(旅游旺季). In work, through his personal practice, he gradually found out ways to sort the garbage into recyclable and inrecyclable. According to him, the biggest difficulty is that residents have weak awareness of environmental protection. They just litter trash around or put them all in the same rubbish bin instead of throwing them in different bins. When he retired, he tried his best in promoting garbage recycling(垃圾回收). The topic may seem a bit boring, but the speech was not. He used vivid and humorous language, and gave us many examples. For instance, when explaining how developed countries performed garbage classification, he mentioned that France has forced residents to hand in 2 kg trash per month for sorted collection. I admire him very much.

## 250. 看到野生动物的地方/特别的照片/公园&花园 / 地点
1. [Part 4] Describe a place you have been to where you can see wild animals
You should say:
Where it is
When you went there
What animals you saw there
How you feel about the place；
Describe a photo that is special to you
You should say:
When and where it was taken
Who are in the photo
Why it is special to you
And explain whether you will keep it for a long time；
Describe a public park or garden
You should say:
Where it is
What it is like
How often you go there
What you often do there
And explain how you feel about it
   - Answer: 森林公园 (6~6.5)
   - Summary: 我去了城外的一个森林公园，该公园以其多样的野生动物和郁郁葱葱的绿色景观而闻名。我还拍到了蜡嘴鸟的照片。
   - Content: I'd like to describe a place I visited where I had the chance to see wild animals. It was a forest park located just outside my city. I went there last spring, seeking a break from the hustle and bustle of urban life. The park is known for its diverse wildlife and lush, green landscapes.

During my visit, I was fortunate to spot various wild birds. The park is home to species like woodpeckers, robins, and even the occasional hawk. I spent hours walking along the trails, quietly observing and photographing these beautiful creatures in their natural habitat. The experience was both exhilarating and calming, as the tranquility of the forest and the sight of the animals in their element were truly captivating.

The forest park is a special place for me because it offers a rare chance to connect with nature and see wildlife up close. I feel a deep sense of peace and appreciation whenever I visit. The photos I took of the wild birds are precious to me, capturing moments of natural beauty and serenity.

In addition, I got a special photo in this park: it's a vibrant red cardinal perched on a tree branch. This photo is special because it perfectly captures the essence of the park and the joy I felt during my visit. I plan to keep this photo for a long time to remind me of this peaceful escape and the amazing wildlife I encountered.

## 256. 喜欢到不喜欢的人/熊孩子 / 人物
1. [Part 4] 不喜欢到喜欢的人/熊孩子
Describe a person you disliked at first but ended up being friends with
Describe a time when you saw children behave badly in public
   - Answer: 不喜欢到喜欢的人/熊孩子/希望一起工作/学习的人 (6~6.5)
   - Summary: 在咖啡馆目睹一个5岁男孩吵闹捣乱，起初以为他被宠坏了。但当他温柔帮妹妹捡玩具并道歉时，才明白孩子并非"顽劣"，只是情绪失控或正在学习规矩。这个"小捣蛋鬼"的暖心举动让我消气，也教会我不要过早评判他人。
Demanding – 吵闹要求的
Smeared – 沾满
Disapproving – 不赞成的
Unruly – 不守规矩的
Tantrum – 发脾气
Demeanor – 态度
Irritation – 烦躁
Overwhelmed – 情绪失控的
Troublemaker – 捣蛋鬼
   - Content: A few months ago, I was at a small café(咖啡馆), enjoying a quiet afternoon with a book. Suddenly, a little boy, around 5 years old, started running around, knocking over chairs and loudly demanding(吵闹着要) ice cream from his mother. His face was smeared with(沾满) chocolate, and his energy seemed endless. The other customers, including me, were clearly annoyed(恼火)—some sighed, while others gave disapproving looks(不赞成的眼神). His mother looked exhausted(精疲力尽), trying to calm him down, but he kept shouting and even bumped into a waiter carrying drinks.

At first, I thought he was just a spoiled, unruly(被宠坏的、不守规矩的) kid. But then, something unexpected happened. When his little sister dropped her stuffed toy, he immediately stopped his tantrum(发脾气), picked it up, and gently handed it back to her, saying, "Don’t cry, I got it!" His whole demeanor(态度) changed—his loudness turned into soft murmurs(小声嘀咕) as he comforted her. Seeing that, my irritation(烦躁) melted away.

Later, I even overheard him apologizing(道歉) to the waiter in a tiny voice. It made me realize that kids aren’t just "bad"—sometimes, they’re just overwhelmed(情绪失控) or still learning how to behave. That little troublemaker(捣蛋鬼) turned out to have a sweet heart underneath all the chaos(混乱). Now, whenever I remember that moment, I smile. It taught me not to judge too quickly(过早下定论).
